utpadyante 'śubhānyeva pratikarmapravṛttiṣu
dṛśyante dāruṇāḥ svapnā daurātmyamupajāyate
preṣyāḥ pratīpatāṃ yānti pretākṛtirudīryate
prakṛtirhīyate 'tyarthaṃ vikṛtiścābhivardhate
kṛtsnamautpātikaṃ ghoram ariṣṭam upalakṣyate
ityetāni manuṣyāṇāṃ bhavanti vinaśiṣyatām
lakṣaṇāni yathoddeśaṃ yānyuktāni yathāgamam
maraṇāyeha rūpāṇi paśyatāpi bhiṣagvidā
apṛṣṭena na vaktavyaṃ maraṇaṃ pratyupasthitam
pṛṣṭenāpi na vaktavyaṃ tatra yatropaghātakam
āturasya bhavedduḥkhamathavānyasya kasyacit
abruvanmaraṇaṃ tasya nainamiccheccikitsitum
yasya paśyedvināśāya liṅgāni kuśalo bhiṣak
liṅgebhyo maraṇākhyebhyo viparītāni paśyatā
liṅgānyārogyamāgantu vaktavyaṃ bhiṣajā dhruvam
dūtairautpātikairbhāvaiḥ pathyāturakulāśrayaiḥ
āturācāraśīleṣṭadravyasaṃpattilakṣaṇaiḥ
svācāraṃ hṛṣṭamavyaṅgaṃ yaśasyaṃ śuklavāsasam
amuṇḍam ajaṭaṃ dūtaṃ jātiveśakriyāsamam
anuṣṭrakharayānastham asaṃdhyāsv agraheṣu ca
adāruṇeṣu nakṣatreṣv anugreṣu dhruveṣu ca
vinā caturthīṃ navamīṃ vinā riktāṃ caturdaśīm
madhyāhnamardharātraṃ ca bhūkampaṃ rāhudarśanam
vinā deśamaśastaṃ cāśastautpātikalakṣaṇam
dūtaṃ praśastamavyagraṃ nirdiśedāgataṃ bhiṣak
dadhyakṣatadvijātīnāṃ vṛṣabhāṇāṃ nṛpasya ca
ratnānāṃ pūrṇakumbhānāṃ sitasya turagasya ca
suradhvajapatākānāṃ phalānāṃ yāvakasya ca
kanyāpuṃvardhamānānāṃ baddhasyaikapaśostasthā
pṛthivyā uddhṛtāyāśca vahneḥ prajvalitasya ca
modakānāṃ sumanasāṃ śuklānāṃ candanasya ca
manojñasyānnapānasya pūrṇasya śakaṭasya ca
nṛbhirdhenvāḥ savatsāyā vaḍavāyāḥ striyāstathā
jīvañjīvakasiddhārthasārasapriyavādinām
haṃsānāṃ śatapatrāṇāṃ cāṣāṇāṃ śikhināṃ tathā
matsyājadvijaśaṅkhānāṃ priyaṅgūnāṃ ghṛtasya ca
rucakādarśasiddhārtharocanānāṃ ca darśanam
gandhaḥ surabhirvarṇaśca suśuklo madhuro rasaḥ
mṛgapakṣimanuṣyāṇāṃ praśastāśca giraḥ śubhāḥ
chatradhvajapatākānāmutkṣepaṇamabhiṣṭutiḥ
bherīmṛdaṅgaśaṅkhānāṃ śabdāḥ puṇyāhanisvanāḥ
vedādhyayanaśabdāśca sukho vāyuḥ pradakṣiṇaḥ
pathi veśmapraveśe tu vidyādārogyalakṣaṇam
maṅgalācārasampannaḥ sāturo vaiśmiko janaḥ
śraddadhāno 'nukūlaśca prabhūtadravyasaṃgrahaḥ
dhanaiśvaryasukhāvāptiriṣṭalābhaḥ sukhena ca
dravyāṇāṃ tatra yogyānāṃ yojanā siddhireva ca
gṛhaprāsādaśailānāṃ nāgānāmṛṣabhasya ca
hayānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ ca svapne samadhirohaṇam
somārkāgnidvijātīnāṃ gavāṃ nṝṇāṃ payasvinām
arṇavānāṃ prataraṇaṃ vṛddhiḥ saṃbādhaniḥsṛtiḥ
svapne devaiḥ sapitṛbhiḥ prasannaiścābhibhāṣaṇam
darśanaṃ śuklavastrāṇāṃ hradasya vimalasya ca
māṃsamatsyaviṣāmedhyacchatrādarśaparigrahaḥ
svapne sumanasāṃ caiva śuklānāṃ darśanaṃ śubham
aśvagorathayānaṃ ca yānaṃ pūrvottareṇa ca
rodanaṃ patitotthānaṃ dviṣatāṃ cāvamardanam
sattvalakṣaṇasaṃyogo bhaktirvaidyadvijātiṣu
sādhyatvaṃ na ca nirvedastadārogyasya lakṣaṇaṃ
ārogyādbalamāyuśca sukhaṃ ca labhate mahat
iṣṭāṃścāpyaparān bhāvān puruṣaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥ
uktaṃ gomayacūrṇīye maraṇārogyalakṣaṇam
dūtasvapnāturotpātayuktisiddhivyapāśrayam
itīdamuktaṃ prakṛtaṃ yathātathaṃ tadanvavekṣyaṃ satataṃ bhiṣagvidā
tathā hi siddhiṃ ca yaśaśca śāśvataṃ sa siddhakarmā labhate dhanāni ca
athāto 'bhayāmalakīyaṃ rasāyanapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
cikitsitaṃ vyādhiharaṃ pathyaṃ sādhanamauṣadham
prāyaścittaṃ praśamanaṃ prakṛtisthāpanaṃ hitam
vidyād bheṣajanāmāni bheṣajaṃ dvividhaṃ ca tat
svasthasyorjaskaraṃ kiṃcit kiṃcidārtasya roganut
abheṣajaṃ ca dvividhaṃ bādhanaṃ sānubādhanam
svasthasyorjaskaraṃ yattu tadvṛṣyaṃ tadrasāyanam
prāyaḥ prāyeṇa rogāṇāṃ dvitīyaṃ praśame matam
prāyaḥśabdo viśeṣārtho hy ubhayaṃ hy ubhayārthakṛt
dīrghamāyuḥ smṛtiṃ medhāmārogyaṃ taruṇaṃ vayaḥ
prabhāvarṇasvaraudāryaṃ dehendriyabalaṃ param
vāksiddhiṃ praṇatiṃ kāntiṃ labhate nā rasāyanāt
lābhopāyo hi śastānāṃ rasādīnāṃ rasāyanam
apatyasaṃtānakaraṃ yat sadyaḥ sampraharṣaṇam
vājīvātibalo yena yātyapratihataḥ striyaḥ
bhavatyatipriyaḥ strīṇāṃ yena yenopacīyate
jīryato 'pyakṣayaṃ śukraṃ phalavadyena dṛśyate
prabhūtaśākhaḥ śākhīva yena caityo yathā mahān
bhavatyarcyo bahumataḥ prajānāṃ subahuprajaḥ
saṃtānamūlaṃ yeneha pretya cānantyamaśnute
yaśaḥ śriyaṃ balaṃ puṣṭiṃ vājīkaraṇameva tat
svasthasyorjaskaraṃ tv etad dvividhaṃ proktam auṣadham
yadvyādhinirghātakaraṃ vakṣyate taccikitsite
cikitsitārtha etāvān vikārāṇāṃ yadauṣadham
rasāyanavidhiścāgre vājīkaraṇameva ca
abheṣajamiti jñeyaṃ viparītaṃ yadauṣadhāt
tadasevyaṃ niṣevyaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi yadauṣadham
rasāyanānāṃ dvividhaṃ prayogamṛṣayo viduḥ
kuṭīprāveśikaṃ caiva vātātapikameva ca
kuṭīprāveśikasyādau vidhiḥ samupadekṣyate
nṛpavaidyadvijātīnāṃ sādhūnāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
nivāse nirbhaye śaste prāpyopakaraṇe pure
diśi pūrvottarasyāṃ ca subhūmau kārayetkuṭīm
vistārotsedhasampannāṃ trigarbhāṃ sūkṣmalocanām
ghanabhittimṛtusukhāṃ suspaṣṭāṃ manasaḥ priyām
śabdādīnām aśastānām agamyāṃ strīvivarjitām
iṣṭopakaraṇopetāṃ sajjavaidyauṣadhadvijām
athodagayane śukle tithinakṣatrapūjite
muhūrtakaraṇopete praśaste kṛtavāpanaḥ
dhṛtismṛtibalaṃ kṛtvā śraddadhānaḥ samāhitaḥ
vidhūya mānasāndoṣān maitrīṃ bhūteṣu cintayan
devatāḥ pūjayitvāgre dvijātīṃśca pradakṣiṇam
devagobrāhmaṇān kṛtvā tatas tāṃ praviśet kuṭīm
tasyāṃ saṃśodhanaiḥ śuddhaḥ sukhī jātabalaḥ punaḥ
rasāyanaṃ prayuñjīta tatpravakṣyāmi śodhanam
harītakīnāṃ cūrṇāni saindhavāmalake guḍam
vacāṃ viḍaṅgaṃ rajanīṃ pippalīṃ viśvabheṣajam
pibeduṣṇāmbunā jantuḥ snehasvedopapāditaḥ
tena śuddhaśarīrāya kṛtasaṃsarjanāya ca
trirātraṃ yāvakaṃ dadyāt pañcāhaṃ vāpi sarpiṣā
saptāhaṃ vā purāṇasya yāvacchuddhestu varcasaḥ
śuddhakoṣṭhaṃ tu taṃ jñātvā rasāyanamupācaret
vayaḥprakṛtisātmyajño yaugikaṃ yasya yadbhavet
harītakīṃ pañcarasāmuṣṇāmalavaṇāṃ śivām
doṣānulomanīṃ laghvīṃ vidyāddīpanapācanīm
āyuṣyāṃ pauṣṭikīṃ dhanyāṃ vayasaḥ sthāpanīṃ parām
sarvarogapraśamanīṃ buddhīndriyabalapradām
kuṣṭhaṃ gulmamudāvartaṃ śoṣaṃ pāṇḍvāmayaṃ madam
arśāṃsi grahaṇīdoṣaṃ purāṇaṃ viṣamajvaram
hṛdrogaṃ saśirorogam atīsāram arocakam
kāsaṃ pramehamānāhaṃ plīhānam udaraṃ navam
kaphaprasekaṃ vaisvaryaṃ vaivarṇyaṃ kāmalāṃ krimīn
śvayathuṃ tamakaṃ chardiṃ klaibyamaṅgāvasādanam
srotovibandhān vividhān pralepaṃ hṛdayorasoḥ
smṛtibuddhipramohaṃ ca jayecchīghraṃ harītakī
ajīrṇino rūkṣabhujaḥ strīmadyaviṣakarśitāḥ
severan nābhayām ete kṣuttṛṣṇoṣṇārditāś ca ye
tān guṇāṃstāni karmāṇi vidyādāmalakīṣvapi
yānyuktāni harītakyā vīryasya tu viparyayaḥ
ataścāmṛtakalpāni vidyāt karmabhirīdṛśaiḥ
harītakīnāṃ śasyāni bhiṣagāmalakasya ca
oṣadhīnāṃ parā bhūmir himavāñśailasattamaḥ
tasmātphalāni tajjāni grāhayetkālajāni tu
āpūrṇarasavīryāṇi kāle kāle yathāvidhi
ādityapavanacchāyāsalilaprīṇitāni ca
yāny ajagdhāny apūtīni nirvraṇānyagadāni ca
teṣāṃ prayogaṃ vakṣyāmi phalānāṃ karma cottamam
pañcānāṃ pañcamūlānāṃ bhāgān daśapalonmitān
harītakīsahasraṃ ca triguṇāmalakaṃ navam
vidārigandhāṃ bṛhatīṃ pṛśniparṇīṃ nidigdhikām
vidyādvidārigandhādyaṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāpañcamaṃ gaṇam
bilvāgnimanthaśyonākaṃ kāśmaryamatha pāṭalām
punarnavāṃ śūrpaparṇyau balām eraṇḍameva ca
jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ jīvantīṃ saśatāvarīm
śarekṣudarbhakāśānāṃ śālīnāṃ mūlameva ca
ityeṣāṃ pañcamūlānāṃ pañcānāmupakalpayet
bhāgān yathoktāṃstatsarvaṃ sādhyaṃ daśaguṇe 'mbhasi
daśabhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu pūtaṃ taṃ grāhayedrasam
harītakīśca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāṇyāmalakāni ca
tāni sarvāṇyanasthīni phalānyāpothya kūrcanaiḥ
vinīya tasminniryūhe cūrṇānīmāni dāpayet
maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ pippalyāḥ śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ plavasya ca
mustānāṃ saviḍaṅgānāṃ candanāguruṇostathā
madhukasya haridrāyā vacāyāḥ kanakasya ca
bhāgāṃś catuṣpalān kṛtvā sūkṣmailāyās tvacas tathā
sitopalāsahasraṃ ca cūrṇitaṃ tulayādhikam
tailasya hy āḍhakaṃ tatra dadyāt trīṇi ca sarpiṣaḥ
sādhyamaudumbare pātre tat sarvaṃ mṛdunāgninā
jñātvā lehyamadagdhaṃ ca śītaṃ kṣaudreṇa saṃsṛjet
kṣaudrapramāṇaṃ snehārdhaṃ tatsarvaṃ ghṛtabhājane
tiṣṭhet saṃmūrchitaṃ tasya mātrāṃ kāle prayojayet
yā noparundhyādāhāramekaṃ mātrā jarāṃ prati
ṣaṣṭikaḥ payasā cātra jīrṇe bhojanamiṣyate
vaikhānasā vālakhilyāstathā cānye tapodhanāḥ
rasāyanamidaṃ prāśya babhūvur amitāyuṣaḥ
muktvā jīrṇaṃ vapuścāgryamavāpustaruṇaṃ vayaḥ
vītatandrāklamaśvāsā nirātaṅkāḥ samāhitāḥ
medhāsmṛtibalopetāś cirarātraṃ tapodhanāḥ
brāhmaṃ tapo brahmacaryaṃ ceruścātyantaniṣṭhayā
rasāyanamidaṃ brāhmamāyuṣkāmaḥ prayojayet
dīrgham āyur vayaś cāgryaṃ kāmāṃśceṣṭān samaśnute
yathoktaguṇānām āmalakānāṃ sahasraṃ piṣṭasvedanavidhinā payasa ūṣmaṇā susvinnamanātapaśuṣkamanasthi cūrṇayet
tadāmalakasahasrasvarasaparipītaṃ sthirāpunarnavājīvantīnāgabalābrahmasuvarcalāmaṇḍūkaparṇīśatāvarīśaṅkhapuṣpīpippalīvacāviḍaṅgasvayaṅguptāmṛtā candanāgurumadhukamadhūkapuṣpotpalapadmamālatīyuvatīyūthikācūrṇāṣṭabhāgasaṃyuktaṃ punar nāgabalāsahasrapalasvarasaparipītam anātapaśuṣkaṃ dviguṇitasarpiṣā kṣaudrasarpiṣā vā kṣudraguḍākṛtiṃ kṛtvā śucau dṛḍhe ghṛtabhāvite kumbhe bhasmarāśer adhaḥ sthāpayed antarbhūmeḥ pakṣaṃ kṛtarakṣāvidhānam atharvavedavidā pakṣātyaye coddhṛtya kanakarajatatāmrapravālakālāyasacūrṇāṣṭabhāgasaṃyuktam ardhakarṣavṛddhyā yathoktena vidhinā prātaḥ prātaḥ prayuñjāno 'gnibalam abhisamīkṣya jīrṇe ca ṣaṣṭikaṃ payasā sasarpiṣkam upasevamāno yathoktān guṇān samaśnuta iti
idaṃ rasāyanaṃ brāhmaṃ maharṣigaṇasevitam
bhavatyarogo dīrghāyuḥ prayuñjāno mahābalaḥ
kāntaḥ prajānāṃ siddhārthaś candrādityasamadyutiḥ
śrutaṃ dhārayate sattvamārṣaṃ cāsya pravartate
dharaṇīdharasāraśca vāyunā samavikramaḥ
sa bhavatyaviṣaṃ cāsya gātre saṃpadyate viṣam
bilvo 'gnimanthaḥ śyonākaḥ kāśmaryaḥ pāṭalirbalā
parṇyaś catasraḥ pippalyaḥ śvadaṃṣṭrā bṛhatīdvayam
śṛṅgī tāmalakī drākṣā jīvantī puṣkarāguru
abhayā cāmṛtā ṛddhir jīvakarṣabhakau śaṭī
mustaṃ punarnavā medā sailā candanamutpalam
vidārī vṛṣamūlāni kākolī kākanāsikā
eṣāṃ palonmitān bhāgāñśatāny āmalakasya ca
pañca dadyāttadaikadhyaṃ jaladroṇe vipācayet
jñātvā gatarasānyetāny auṣadhānyatha taṃ rasam
taccāmalakamuddhṛtya niṣkulaṃ tailasarpiṣoḥ
paladvādaśake bhṛṣṭvā dattvā cārdhatulāṃ bhiṣak
matsyaṇḍikāyāḥ pūtāyā lehavatsādhu sādhayet
ṣaṭpalaṃ madhunaścātra siddhaśīte pradāpayet
catuṣpalaṃ tugākṣīryāḥ pippalīdvipalaṃ tathā
palamekaṃ nidadhyācca tvagelāpattrakesarāt
ityayaṃ cyavanaprāśaḥ paramukto rasāyanaḥ
kāsaśvāsaharaś caiva viśeṣeṇopadiśyate
kṣīṇakṣatānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ bālānāṃ cāṅgavardhanaḥ
svarakṣayam urorogaṃ hṛdrogaṃ vātaśoṇitam
pipāsāṃ śukrasthān doṣāṃścāpyapakarṣati
asya mātrāṃ prayuñjīta yoparundhyānna bhojanam
asya prayogāc cyavanaḥ suvṛddho'bhūtpunaryuvā
medhāṃ smṛtiṃ kāntimanāmayatvam āyuḥprakarṣaṃ balamindriyāṇām
strīṣu praharṣaṃ paramagnivṛddhiṃ varṇaprasādaṃ pavanānulomyam
rasāyanasyāsya naraḥ prayogāl labheta jīrṇo 'pi kuṭīpraveśāt
jarākṛtaṃ rūpamapāsya sarvaṃ bibharti rūpaṃ navayauvanasya
athāmalakaharītakīnām āmalakavibhītakānāṃ harītakīvibhītakānām āmalakaharītakīvibhītakānāṃ vā palāśatvagavanaddhānāṃ mṛdāvaliptānāṃ kukūlasvinnānām akulakānāṃ palasahasramulūkhale saṃpothya dadhighṛtamadhupalalatailaśarkarāsaṃyuktaṃ bhakṣayed anannabhug yathoktena vidhinā tasyānte yavāgvādibhiḥ pratyavasthāpanam abhyaṅgotsādanaṃ sarpiṣā yavacūrṇaiśca ayaṃca rasāyanaprayogaprakarṣo dvistāvadagnibalam abhisamīkṣya pratibhojanaṃ yūṣeṇa payasā vā ṣaṣṭikaḥ sasarpiṣkaḥ ataḥ paraṃ yathāsukhavihāraḥ kāmabhakṣyaḥ syāt
anena prayogeṇarṣayaḥ punar yuvatvam avāpur babhūvuś cānekavarṣaśatajīvino nirvikārāḥ paraśarīrabuddhīndriyabalasamuditāś ceruś cātyantaniṣṭhayā tapaḥ
harītakyāmalakavibhītakapañcapañcamūlaniryūhe pippalīmadhukamadhūkakākolīkṣīrakākolyātmaguptājīvakarṣabhakakṣīraśuklākalkasamprayuktena vidārīsvarasena kṣīrāṣṭaguṇasamprayuktena ca sarpiṣaḥ kumbhaṃ sādhayitvā prayuñjāno 'gnibalasamāṃ mātrāṃ jīrṇe ca kṣīrasarpirbhyāṃ śāliṣaṣṭikam uṣṇodakānupānam aśnañjarāvyādhipāpābhicāravyapagatabhayaḥ śarīrendriyabuddhibalam atulam upalabhyāpratihatasarvārambhaḥ paramāyur avāpnuyāt
harītakyāmalakavibhītakaharidrāsthirābalāviḍaṅgāmṛtavallīviśvabheṣajamadhukapippalīsomavalkasiddhena kṣīrasarpiṣā madhuśarkarābhyāmapi ca saṃnīyāmalakasvarasaśataparipītam āmalakacūrṇam ayaścūrṇacaturbhāgasamprayuktaṃ pāṇitalamātraṃ prātaḥ prātaḥ prāśya yathoktena vidhinā sāyaṃ mudgayūṣeṇa payasā vā sasarpiṣkaṃ śāliṣaṣṭikānnam aśnīyāt trivarṣaprayogādasya varṣaśatam ajaraṃ vayas tiṣṭhati śrutam avatiṣṭhate sarvāmayāḥ praśāmyanti viṣamaviṣaṃ bhavati gātre gātram aśmavat sthirībhavati adhṛṣyo bhūtānāṃ bhavati
yathāmarāṇām amṛtaṃ yathā bhogavatāṃ sudhā
tathābhavan maharṣīṇāṃ rasāyanavidhiḥ purā
na jarāṃ na ca daurbalyaṃ nāturyaṃ nidhanaṃ na ca
jagmurvarṣasahasrāṇi rasāyanaparāḥ purā
na kevalaṃ dīrghamihāyuraśnute rasāyanaṃ yo vidhivanniṣevate
gatiṃ sa devarṣiniṣevitāṃ śubhāṃ prapadyate brahma tatheti cākṣayam
abhayāmalakīye 'smin ṣaḍ yogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
rasāyanānāṃ siddhānām āyur yair anuvartate
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne rasāyanādhyāye 'bhayāmalakīyo nāma rasāyanapādaḥ prathamaḥ
athātaḥ prāṇakāmīyaṃ rasāyanapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavān ātreyaḥ
prāṇakāmāḥ śuśrūṣadhvam idam ucyamānam amṛtam ivāparam aditisutahitakaram acintyādbhutaprabhāvam āyuṣyam ārogyakaraṃ vayasaḥ sthāpanaṃ nidrātandrāśramaklamālasyadaurbalyāpaharam anilakaphapittasāmyakaraṃ sthairyakaram abaddhamāṃsaharam antaragnisaṃdhukṣaṇaṃ prabhāvarṇasvarottamakaraṃ rasāyanavidhānam
anena cyavanādayo maharṣayaḥ punaryuvatvam āpur nārīṇāṃ ceṣṭatamā babhūvuḥ sthirasamasuvibhaktamāṃsāḥ susaṃhatasthiraśarīrāḥ suprasannabalavarṇendriyāḥ sarvatrāpratihataparākramāḥ kleśasahāś ca
sarve śarīradoṣā bhavanti grāmyāhārād amlatvalavaṇakaṭukakṣāraśukraśākamāṃsatilapalalapiṣṭānnabhojināṃ virūḍhanavaśūkaśamīdhānyaviruddhāsātmyarūkṣakṣārābhiṣyandibhojināṃ klinnagurupūtiparyuṣitabhojināṃ viṣamādhyaśanaprāyāṇāṃ divāsvapnastrīmadyanityānāṃ viṣamātimātravyāyāmasaṃkṣobhitaśarīrāṇāṃ bhayakrodhaśokalobhamohāyāsabahulānām atonimittaṃ hi śithilībhavanti māṃsāni vimucyante saṃdhayaḥ vidahyate raktaṃ viṣyandate cānalpaṃ medaḥ na saṃdhīyate 'sthiṣu majjā śukraṃ na pravartate kṣayamupaityojaḥ sa evaṃbhūte glāyati sīdati nidrātandrālasyasamanvito nirutsāhaḥ śvasiti asamarthaśceṣṭānāṃ śārīramānasīnāṃ naṣṭasmṛtibuddhicchāyo rogāṇām adhiṣṭhānabhūto na sarvamāyuravāpnoti
tasmādetāndoṣānavekṣamāṇaḥ sarvān yathoktān ahitān apāsyāhāravihārān rasāyanāni prayoktumarhatītyuktvā bhagavān punarvasur ātreya uvāca
āmalakānāṃ subhūmijānāṃ kālajānām anupahatagandhavarṇarasānām āpūrṇasapramāṇavīryāṇāṃ svarasena punarnavākalkapādasamprayuktena sarpiṣaḥ sādhayedāḍhakam ataḥ paraṃ vidārīsvarasena jīvantīkalkasamprayuktena ataḥ paraṃ caturguṇena payasā balātibalākaṣāyeṇa śatāvarīkalkasaṃyuktena anena krameṇaikaikaṃ śatapākaṃ sahasrapākaṃ vā śarkarākṣaudracaturbhāgasamprayuktaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mārttike vā śucau dṛḍhe ghṛtabhāvite kumbhe sthāpayet tadyathoktena vidhinā yathāgni prātaḥ prātaḥ prayojayet jīrṇe ca kṣīrasarpirbhyāṃ śāliṣaṣṭikam aśnīyāt
asya prayogādvarṣaśataṃ vayo'jaraṃ tiṣṭhati śrutamavatiṣṭhate sarvāmayāḥ praśāmyanti apratihatagatiḥ strīṣu apatyavān bhavatīti
bṛhaccharīraṃ girisārasāraṃ sthirendriyaṃ cātibalendriyaṃ ca
adhṛṣyamanyair atikāntarūpaṃ praśastipūjāsukhacittabhāk ca
balaṃ mahadvarṇaviśuddhir agryā svaro ghanaughastanitānukārī
bhavatyapatyaṃ vipulaṃ sthiraṃ ca samaśnato yogamimaṃ narasya
āmalakasahasraṃ pippalīsahasrasamprayuktaṃ palāśataruṇakṣārodakottaraṃ tiṣṭhet tadanugatakṣārodakam anātapaśuṣkam anasthi cūrṇīkṛtaṃ caturguṇābhyāṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ saṃnīya śarkarācūrṇacaturbhāgasamprayuktaṃ ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ ṣaṇmāsān sthāpayedantarbhūmeḥ
tasyottarakālamagnibalasamāṃ mātrāṃ khādet paurvāhṇikaḥ prayogo nāparāhṇikaḥ sātmyāpekṣaścāhāravidhiḥ
asya prayogād varṣaśatamajaraṃ vayas tiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
āmalakacūrṇāḍhakam ekaviṃśatirātram āmalakasvarasaparipītaṃ madhughṛtāḍhakābhyāṃ dvābhyāmekīkṛtam aṣṭabhāgapippalīkaṃ śarkarācūrṇacaturbhāgasamprayuktaṃ ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśau nidadhyāt tadvarṣānte sātmyapathyāśī prayojayet asya prayogād varṣaśatam ajaram āyus tiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
viḍaṅgataṇḍulacūrṇānām āḍhakamāḍhakaṃ pippalītaṇḍulānām adhyardhāḍhakaṃ sitopalāyāḥ sarpistailamadhvāḍhakaiḥ ṣaḍbhir ekīkṛtaṃ ghṛtabhājanasthaṃ prāvṛṣi bhasmarāśāv iti sarvaṃ samānaṃ pūrveṇa yāvad āśīḥ
yathoktaguṇānāmāmalakānāṃ sahasramārdrapalāśadroṇyāṃ sapidhānāyāṃ bāṣpam anudvamantyām āraṇyagomayāgnibhir upasvedayet tāni susvinnaśītāny uddhṛtakulakāny āpothyāḍhakena pippalīcūrṇānāmāḍhakena ca viḍaṅgataṇḍulacūrṇānām adhyardhena cāḍhakena śarkarāyā dvābhyāṃ dvābhyām āḍhakābhyāṃ tailasya madhunaḥ sarpiṣaśca saṃyojya śucau dṛḍhe ghṛtabhāvite kumbhe sthāpayed ekaviṃśatirātram ata ūrdhvaṃ prayogaḥ asya prayogādvarṣaśatam ajaram āyus tiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
dhanvani kuśāstīrṇe snigdhakṛṣṇamadhuramṛttike suvarṇavarṇamṛttike vā vyapagataviṣaśvāpadapavanasalilāgnidoṣe karṣaṇavalmīkaśmaśānacaityoṣarāvasathavarjite deśe yathartusukhapavanasalilādityasevite jātāny anupahatāny anadhyārūḍhāny abālāny ajīrṇāny adhigatavīryāṇi śīrṇapurāṇaparṇāny asaṃjātāny aparṇāni tapasi tapasye vā māse śuciḥ prayataḥ kṛtadevārcanaḥ svasti vācayitvā dvijātīn cale sumuhūrte nāgabalāmūlāny uddharet teṣāṃ suprakṣālitānāṃ tvakpiṇḍam āmramātram akṣamātraṃ vā ślakṣṇapiṣṭamāloḍya payasā prātaḥ prayojayet cūrṇīkṛtāni vā pibet payasā madhusarpirbhyāṃ vā saṃyojya bhakṣayet jīrṇe ca kṣīrasarpirbhyāṃ śāliṣaṣṭikam aśnīyāt
saṃvatsaraprayogādasya varṣaśatamajaraṃ vayastiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
balātibalācandanāgurudhavatiniśakhadiraśiṃśapāsanasvarasāḥ punarnavāntāścauṣadhayo daśa nāgabalayā vyākhyātāḥ
svarasānāmalābhe tv ayaṃ svarasavidhiś cūrṇānām āḍhakam āḍhakam udakasyāhorātrāsthitaṃ mṛditapūtaṃ svarasavat prayojyam
bhallātakāny anupahatāny anāmayāny āpūrṇarasapramāṇavīryāṇi pakvajāmbavaprakāśāni śucau śukre vā māse saṃgṛhya yavapalle māṣapalle vā nidhāpayet tāni caturmāsasthitāni sahasi sahasye vā māse prayoktum ārabheta śītasnigdhamadhuropaskṛtaśarīraḥ
pūrvaṃ daśabhallātakānyāpothyāṣṭaguṇenāmbhasā sādhu sādhayet teṣāṃ rasamaṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣaṃ pūtaṃ sapayaskaṃ pibet sarpiṣāntar mukham abhyajya
tāny ekaikabhallātakotkarṣāpakarṣeṇa daśabhallātakāny ā triṃśataḥ prayojyāni nātaḥ paramutkarṣaḥ
prayogavidhānena sahasrapara eva bhallātakaprayogaḥ
jīrṇe ca sasarpiṣā payasā śāliṣaṣṭikāśanam upacāraḥ prayogānte ca dvis tāvat payasaivopacāraḥ
tatprayogādvarṣaśatamajaraṃ vayas tiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
bhallātakānāṃ jarjarīkṛtānāṃ piṣṭasvedanaṃ pūrayitvā bhūmāv ākaṇṭhaṃ nikhātasya snehabhāvitasya dṛḍhasyopari kumbhasyāropyoḍupenāpidhāya kṛṣṇamṛttikāvaliptaṃ gomayāgnibhir upasvedayet teṣāṃ yaḥ svarasaḥ kumbhaṃ prapadyeta tam aṣṭabhāgamadhusamprayuktaṃ dviguṇaghṛtam adyāt tatprayogādvarṣaśatamajaraṃ vayastiṣṭhatīti samānaṃ pūrveṇa
bhallātakatailapātraṃ sapayaskaṃ madhukena kalkenākṣamātreṇa śatapākaṃ kuryāditi samānaṃ pūrveṇa
bhallātakasarpiḥ bhallātakakṣīraṃ bhallātakakṣaudraṃ guḍabhallātakaṃ bhallātakayūṣaḥ bhallātakatailaṃ bhallātakapalalaṃ bhallātakasaktavaḥ bhallātakalavaṇaṃ bhallātakatarpaṇam iti bhallātakavidhānamuktaṃ bhavati
bhallātakāni tīkṣṇāni pākīnyagnisamāni ca
bhavantyamṛtakalpāni prayuktāni yathāvidhi
ete daśavidhāstveṣāṃ prayogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
rogaprakṛtisātmyajñas tān prayogān prakalpayet
kaphajo na sa rogo'sti na vibandho'sti kaścana
yaṃ na bhallātakaṃ hanyācchīghraṃ medhāgnivardhanam
prāṇakāmāḥ purā jīrṇāścyavanādyā maharṣayaḥ
rasāyanaiḥ śivair etair babhūvur amitāyuṣaḥ
brāhmaṃ tapo brahmacaryamadhyātmadhyānameva ca
dīrghāyuṣo yathākāmaṃ saṃbhṛtya tridivaṃ gatāḥ
tasmādāyuḥprakarṣārthaṃ prāṇakāmaiḥ sukhārthibhiḥ
rasāyanavidhiḥ sevyo vidhivat susamāhitaiḥ
rasāyanānāṃ saṃyogāḥ siddhā bhūtahitaiṣiṇā
nirdiṣṭāḥ prāṇakāmīye saptatriṃśanmaharṣiṇā
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne rasāyanādhyāye prāṇakāmīyo nāma rasāyanapādo dvitīyaḥ
athāto jvaracikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
vijvaraṃ jvarasaṃdehaṃ paryapṛcchat punarvasum
vivikte śāntamāsīnamagniveśaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
dehendriyamanastāpī sarvarogāgrajo balī
jvaraḥ pradhāno rogāṇāmukto bhagavatā purā
tasya prāṇisapatnasya dhruvasya pralayodaye
prakṛtiṃ ca pravṛttiṃ ca prabhāvaṃ kāraṇāni ca
pūrvarūpamadhiṣṭhānaṃ balakālātmalakṣaṇam
vyāsato vidhibhedācca pṛthagbhinnasya cākṛtim
liṅgamāmasya jīrṇasya sauṣadhaṃ ca kriyākramam
vimuñcataḥ praśāntasya cihnaṃ yacca pṛthak pṛthak
jvarāvasṛṣṭo rakṣyaśca yāvatkālaṃ yato yataḥ
praśāntaḥ kāraṇairyaiśca punarāvartate jvaraḥ
yāścāpi punarāvṛttaṃ kriyāḥ praśamayanti tam
jagaddhitārthaṃ tat sarvaṃ bhagavan vaktumarhasi
tadagniveśasya vaco niśamya gururabravīt
jvarādhikāre yadvācyaṃ tat saumya nikhilaṃ śṛṇu
jvaro vikāro rogaśca vyādhirātaṅka eva ca
eko 'rtho nāmaparyāyairvividhairabhidhīyate
tasya prakṛtiruddiṣṭā doṣāḥ śārīramānasāḥ
dehinaṃ na hi nirdoṣaṃ jvaraḥ samupasevate
kṣayastamo jvaraḥ pāpmā mṛtyuścoktā yamātmakāḥ
pañcatvapratyayānnṝṇāṃ kliśyatāṃ svena karmaṇā
ityasya prakṛtiḥ proktā pravṛttistu parigrahāt
nidāne pūrvamuddiṣṭā rudrakopācca dāruṇāt
dvitīye hi yuge śarvamakrodhavratamāsthitam
divyaṃ sahasraṃ varṣāṇāmasurā abhidudruvuḥ
tapovighnāśanāḥ kartuṃ tapovighnaṃ mahātmanaḥ
paśyan samarthaścopekṣāṃ cakre dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ
punarmāheśvaraṃ bhāgaṃ dhruvaṃ dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ
yajñe na kalpayāmāsa procyamānaḥ surairapi
ṛcaḥ paśupateryāśca śaivya āhatayaśca yāḥ
yajñasiddhipradāstābhirhīnaṃ caiva sa iṣṭavān
athottīrṇavrato devo buddhvā dakṣavyatikramam
rudro raudraṃ puraskṛtya bhāvamātmavidātmanaḥ
sṛṣṭvā lalāṭe cakṣurvai dagdhvā tānasurān prabhuḥ
bālaṃ krodhāgnisaṃtaptam asṛjat satranāśanam
tato yajñaḥ sa vidhvasto vyathitāśca divaukasaḥ
dāhavyathāparītāśca bhrāntā bhūtagaṇā diśaḥ
atheśvaraṃ devagaṇaḥ saha saptarṣibhirvibhum
tam ṛgbhir astuvan yāvacchaive bhāve śivaḥ sthitaḥ
śivaṃ śivāya bhūtānāṃ sthitaṃ jñātvā kṛtāñjaliḥ
bhiyā bhasmapraharaṇas triśirā navalocanaḥ
jvālāmālākulo raudro hrasvajaṅghodaraḥ kramāt
krodhāgniruktavān devamahaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi te
tamuvāceśvaraḥ krodhaṃ jvaro loke bhaviṣyasi
janmādau nidhane ca tvamapacārāntareṣu ca
saṃtāpaḥ sārucistṛṣṇā sāṅgamardo hṛdi vyathā
jvaraprabhāvo janmādau nidhane ca mahattamaḥ
prakṛtiśca pravṛttiśca prabhāvaśca pradarśitaḥ
nidāne kāraṇānyaṣṭau pūrvoktāni vibhāgaśaḥ
ālasyaṃ nayane sāsre jṛmbhaṇaṃ gauravaṃ klamaḥ
jvalanātapavāyvambubhaktidveṣāvaniścitau
avipākāsyavairasye hāniśca balavarṇayoḥ
śīlavaikṛtamalpaṃ ca jvaralakṣaṇamagrajam
kevalaṃ samanaskaṃ ca jvarādhiṣṭhānamucyate
śarīraṃ balakālastu nidāne saṃpradarśitaḥ
jvarapratyātmikaṃ liṅgaṃ saṃtāpo dehamānasaḥ
jvareṇāviśatā bhūtaṃ na hi kiṃcinna tapyate
dvividho vidhibhedena jvaraḥ śārīramānasaḥ
punaśca dvividho dṛṣṭaḥ saumyaścāgneya eva vā
antarvego bahirvego dvividhaḥ punarucyate
prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva sādhyaścāsādhya eva ca
punaḥ pañcavidho dṛṣṭo doṣakālabalābalāt
saṃtataḥ satato 'nyedyustṛtīyakacaturthakau
punarāśrayabhedena dhātūnāṃ saptadhā mataḥ
bhinnaḥ kāraṇabhedena punaraṣṭavidho jvaraḥ
śārīro jāyate pūrvaṃ dehe manasi mānasaḥ
vaicittyamaratirglānirmanasastāpalakṣaṇam
indriyāṇāṃ ca vaikṛtyaṃ jñeyaṃ saṃtāpalakṣaṇam
vātapittātmakaḥ śītamuṣṇaṃ vātakaphātmakaḥ
icchatyubhayametattu jvaro vyāmiśralakṣaṇaḥ
yogavāhaḥ paraṃ vāyuḥ saṃyogādubhayārthakṛt
dāhakṛttejasā yuktaḥ śītakṛt somasaṃśrayāt
antardāho 'dhikastṛṣṇā pralāpaḥ śvasanaṃ bhramaḥ
sandhyasthiśūlamasvedo doṣavarcovinigrahaḥ
antarvegasya liṅgāni jvarasyaitāni lakṣayet
saṃtāpo 'bhyadhiko bāhyastṛṣṇādīnāṃ ca mārdavam
bahirvegasya liṅgāni sukhasādhyatvameva ca
prākṛtaḥ sukhasādhyastu vasantaśaradudbhavaḥ
uṣṇamuṣṇena saṃvṛddhaṃ pittaṃ śaradi kupyati
citaḥ śīte kaphaścaivaṃ vasante samudīryate
varṣāsvamlavipākābhir adbhir oṣadhibhis tathā
saṃcitaṃ pittamudriktaṃ śaradyādityatejasā
jvaraṃ saṃjanayatyāśu tasya cānubalaḥ kaphaḥ
prakṛtyaiva visargasya tatra nānaśanādbhayam
adbhiroṣadhibhiścaiva madhurābhiścitaḥ kaphaḥ
hemante sūryasaṃtaptaḥ sa vasante prakupyati
vasante śleṣmaṇā tasmājjvaraḥ samupajāyate
ādānamadhye tasyāpi vātapittaṃ bhavedanu
ādāvante ca madhye ca buddhvā doṣabalābalam
śaradvasantayorvidvāñjvarasya pratikārayet
kālaprakṛtimuddiśya nirdiṣṭaḥ prākṛto jvaraḥ
prāyeṇānilayo duḥkhaḥ kāleṣvanyeṣu vaikṛtaḥ
hetavo vividhāstasya nidāne saṃpradarśitāḥ
balavatsvalpadoṣeṣu jvaraḥ sādhyo 'nupadravaḥ
hetubhirbahubhirjāto balibhirbahulakṣaṇaḥ
jvaraḥ prāṇāntakṛdyaśca śīghramindriyanāśanaḥ
saptāhādvā daśāhādvā dvādaśāhāttathaiva ca
sapralāpabhramaśvāsastīkṣṇo hanyājjvaro naram
jvaraḥ kṣīṇasya śūnasya gambhīro dairgharātrikaḥ
asādhyo balavān yaśca keśasīmantakṛjjvaraḥ
srotobhirvisṛtā doṣā guravo rasavāhibhiḥ
sarvadehānugāḥ stabdhā jvaraṃ kurvanti saṃtatam
daśāhaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā saptāhaṃ vā suduḥsahaḥ
sa śīghraṃ śīghrakāritvāt praśamaṃ yāti hanti vā
kāladūṣyaprakṛtibhirdoṣastulyo hi saṃtatam
niṣpratyanīkaḥ kurute tasmājjñeyaḥ suduḥsahaḥ
yathā dhātūṃstathā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ cānilādayaḥ
yugapaccānupadyante niyamāt saṃtate jvare
sa śuddhyā vāpyaśuddhyā vā rasādīnām aśeṣataḥ
saptāhādiṣu kāleṣu praśamaṃ yāti hanti vā
yadā tu nātiśudhyanti na vā śudhyanti sarvaśaḥ
dvādaśaite samuddiṣṭāḥ saṃtatasyāśrayāstadā
visargaṃ dvādaśe kṛtvā divase 'vyaktalakṣaṇam
durlabhopaśamaḥ kālaṃ dīrghamapyanuvartate
iti buddhvā jvaraṃ vaidya upakrāmettu saṃtatam
kriyākramavidhau yuktaḥ prāyaḥ prāgapatarpaṇaiḥ
raktadhātvāśrayaḥ prāyo doṣaḥ satatakaṃ jvaram
sapratyanīkaḥ kurute kālavṛddhikṣayātmakam
ahorātre satatako dvau kālāvanuvartate
kālaprakṛtidūṣyāṇāṃ prāpyaivānyatamādbalam
anyedyuṣkaṃ doṣo ruddhvā medovahāḥ sirāḥ
sapratyanīko janayatyekakālamaharniśi
doṣo 'sthimajjagaḥ kuryāttṛtīyakacaturthakau
gatir dvyekāntarānyedyur doṣasyoktānyathā paraiḥ
anyedyuṣkaṃ jvaraṃ kuryādapi saṃśritya śoṇitam
māṃsasrotāṃsyanugato janayettu tṛtīyakam
saṃśrito medaso mārgaṃ doṣaścāpi caturthakam
anyedyuṣkaḥ pratidinaṃ dinaṃ hitvā tṛtīyakaḥ
dinadvayaṃ yo viśramya pratyeti sa caturthakaḥ
adhiśete yathā bhūmiṃ bījaṃ kāle ca rohati
adhiśete tathā dhātuṃ doṣaḥ kāle ca kupyati
sa vṛddhiṃ balakālaṃ ca prāpya doṣastṛtīyakam
caturthakaṃ ca kurute pratyanīkabalakṣayāt
kṛtvā vegaṃ gatabalāḥ sve sve sthāne vyavasthitāḥ
punarvivṛddhāḥ sve kāle jvarayanti naraṃ malāḥ
kaphapittāttrikagrāhī pṛṣṭhādvātakaphātmakaḥ
vātapittācchirogrāhī trividhaḥ syāttṛtīyakaḥ
caturthako darśayati prabhāvaṃ dvividhaṃ jvaraḥ
jaṅghābhyāṃ ślaiṣmikaḥ pūrvaṃ śirasto 'nilasaṃbhavaḥ
viṣamajvara evānyaścaturthakaviparyayaḥ
trividho dhāturekaiko dvidhātusthaḥ karoti yam
prāyaśaḥ sannipātena dṛṣṭaḥ pañcavidho jvaraḥ
sannipāte tu yo bhūyān sa doṣaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
ṛtvahorātradoṣāṇāṃ manasaśca balābalāt
kālamarthavaśāccaiva jvarastaṃ taṃ prapadyate
gurutvaṃ dainyamudvegaḥ sadanaṃ chardyarocakau
rasasthite bahistāpaḥ sāṅgamardo vijṛmbhaṇam
raktoṣṇāḥ piḍakāstṛṣṇā saraktaṃ ṣṭhīvanaṃ muhuḥ
dāharāgabhramamadapralāpā raktasaṃsthite
antardāhaḥ satṛṇmohaḥ saglāniḥ sṛṣṭaviṭkatā
daurgandhyaṃ gātravikṣepo jvare māṃsasthite bhavet
svedastīvrā pipāsā ca pralāpo vamyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ
svagandhasyāsahatvaṃ ca medaḥsthe glānyarocakau
virekavamane cobhe sāsthibhedaṃ prakūjanam
vikṣepaṇaṃ ca gātrāṇāṃ śvāsaścāsthigate jvare
hikkā śvāsastathā kāsastamasaścātidarśanam
marmacchedo bahiḥ śaityaṃ dāho 'ntaścaiva majjage
śukrasthānagataḥ śukramokṣaṃ kṛtvā vināśya ca
prāṇaṃ vāyvagnisomaiśca sārdhaṃ gacchatyasau vibhuḥ
rasaraktāśritaḥ sādhyo medomāṃsagataśca yaḥ
asthimajjagataḥ kṛcchraḥ śukrastho naiva sidhyati
hetubhirlakṣaṇaiścoktaḥ pūrvam aṣṭavidho jvaraḥ
samāsenopadiṣṭasya vyāsataḥ śṛṇu lakṣaṇam
śiroruk parvaṇāṃ bhedo dāho romṇāṃ praharṣaṇam
kaṇṭhāsyaśoṣo vamathustṛṣṇā mūrcchā bhramo 'ruciḥ
svapnanāśo 'tivāgjṛmbhā vātapittajvarākṛtiḥ
śītako gauravaṃ tandrā staimityaṃ parvaṇāṃ ca ruk
śirograhaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ kāsaḥ svedāpravartanam
santāpo madhyavegaśca vātaśleṣmajvarākṛtiḥ
muhurdāho muhuḥ śītaṃ svedastambho muhurmuhuḥ
mohaḥ kāso 'rucistṛṣṇā śleṣmapittapravartanam
liptatiktāsyatā tandrā śleṣmapittajvarākṛtiḥ
ityete dvandvajāḥ proktāḥ sannipātaja ucyate
sannipātajvarasyordhvaṃ trayodaśavidhasya hi
prāksūtritasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ vai pṛthak pṛthak
bhramaḥ pipāsā dāhaśca gauravaṃ śiraso 'tiruk
vātapittolbaṇe vidyālliṅgaṃ mandakaphe jvare
śaityaṃ kāso 'rucistandrāpipāsādāharugvyathāḥ
vātaśleṣmolbaṇe vyādhau liṅgaṃ pittāvare viduḥ
chardiḥ śaityaṃ muhurdāhastṛṣṇā moho 'sthivedanā
mandavāte vyavasyanti liṅgaṃ pittakapholbaṇe
sandhyasthiśirasaḥ śūlaṃ pralāpo gauravaṃ bhramaḥ
vātolbaṇe syād dvyanuge tṛṣṇā kaṇṭhāsyaśuṣkatā
raktaviṇmūtratā dāhaḥ svedastṛḍ balasaṃkṣayaḥ
mūrcchā ceti tridoṣe syālliṅgaṃ pitte garīyasi
ālasyārucihṛllāsadāhavamyaratibhramaiḥ
kapholbaṇaṃ sannipātaṃ tandrākāsena cādiśet
pratiśyā chardirālasyaṃ tandrārucyagnimārdavam
hīnavāte pittamadhye liṅgaṃ śleṣmādhike matam
hāridramūtranetratvaṃ dāhastṛṣṇā bhramo 'ruciḥ
hīnavāte madhyakaphe liṅgaṃ pittādhike matam
śirorugvepathuḥ śvāsaḥ pralāpaśchardyarocakau
hīnapitte madhyakaphe liṅgaṃ syānmārutādhike
śītako gauravaṃ tandrā pralāpo 'sthiśiro'tiruk
hīnapitte vātamadhye liṅgaṃ śleṣmādhike viduḥ
śvāsaḥ kāsaḥ pratiśyāyo mukhaśoṣo 'tipārśvaruk
kaphahīne pittamadhye liṅgaṃ vātādhike matam
varcobhedo 'gnidaurbalyaṃ tṛṣṇā dāho 'cirbhramaḥ
kaphahīne vātamadhye liṅgaṃ pittādhike viduḥ
sannipātajvarasyordhvamato vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam
kṣaṇe dāhaḥ kṣaṇe śītam asthisandhiśirorujā
sāsrāve kaluṣe rakte nirbhugne cāpi darśane
sasvanau sarujau karṇau kaṇṭhaḥ śūkairivāvṛtaḥ
tandrā mohaḥ pralāpaśca kāsaḥ śvāso 'rucirbhramaḥ
paridagdhā kharasparśā jihvā srastāṅgatā param
ṣṭhīvanaṃ raktapittasya kaphenonmiśritasya ca
śiraso loṭhanaṃ tṛṣṇā nidrānāśo hṛdi vyathā
svedamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ cirāddarśanamalpaśaḥ
kṛśatvaṃ nātigātrāṇāṃ pratataṃ kaṇṭhakūjanam
koṭhānāṃ śyāvaraktānāṃ maṇḍalānāṃ ca darśanam
mūkatvaṃ srotasāṃ pāko gurutvamudarasya ca
cirāt pākaśca doṣāṇāṃ sannipātajvarākṛtiḥ
doṣe vibaddhe naṣṭe 'gnau sarvasampūrṇalakṣaṇaḥ
sannipātajvaro 'sādhyaḥ kṛcchrasādhyastvato 'nyathā
nidāne trividhā proktā yā pṛthagjvarākṛtiḥ
saṃsargasannipātānāṃ tayā coktaṃ svalakṣaṇam
āganturaṣṭamo yastu sa nirdiṣṭaścaturvidhaḥ
abhighātābhiṣaṅgābhyāmabhicārābhiśāpataḥ
śastraloṣṭakaśākāṣṭhamuṣṭyaratnitaladvijaiḥ
tadvidhaiśca hate gātre jvaraḥ syādabhighātajaḥ
tatrābhighātaje vāyuḥ prāyo raktaṃ pradūṣayan
savyathāśophavaivarṇyaṃ karoti sarujaṃ jvaram
kāmaśokabhayakrodhairabhiṣaktasya yo jvaraḥ
so 'bhiṣaṅgajvaro jñeyo yaśca bhūtābhiṣaṅgajaḥ
kāmaśokabhayādvāyuḥ krodhāt pittaṃ trayo malāḥ
bhūtābhiṣaṅgāt kupyanti bhūtasāmānyalakṣaṇāḥ
bhūtādhikāre vyākhyātaṃ tadaṣṭavidhalakṣaṇam
viṣavṛkṣānilasparśāttathānyairviṣasaṃbhavaiḥ
abhiṣaktasya cāpyāhurjvarameke 'bhiṣaṅgajam
cikitsayā viṣaghnyaiva sa śamaṃ labhate naraḥ
abhicārābhiśāpābhyāṃ siddhānāṃ yaḥ pravartate
sannipātajvaro ghoraḥ sa vijñeyaḥ suduḥsahaḥ
sannipātajvarasyoktaṃ liṅgaṃ yattasya tat smṛtam
cittendriyaśarīrāṇāmartayo 'nyāśca naikaśaḥ
prayogaṃ tvabhicārasya dṛṣṭvā śāpasya caiva hi
svayaṃ śrutvānumānena lakṣyate praśamena vā
vaividhyād abhicārasya śāpasya ca tadātmake
yathākarmaprayogeṇa lakṣaṇaṃ syāt pṛthagvidham
dhyānaniḥśvāsabahulaṃ liṅgaṃ kāmajvare smṛtam
śokaje bāṣpabahulaṃ trāsaprāyaṃ bhayajvare
krodhaje bahusaṃrambhaṃ bhūtāveśe tvamānuṣam
mūrcchāmohamadaglānibhūyiṣṭhaṃ viṣasaṃbhave
keṣāṃcid eṣāṃ liṅgānāṃ saṃtāpo jāyate puraḥ
paścāttulyaṃ tu keṣāṃcid eṣu kāmajvarādiṣu
kāmādijānāmuddiṣṭaṃ jvarāṇāṃ yadviśeṣaṇam
kāmādijānāṃ rogāṇāmanyeṣāmapi tat smṛtam
manasyabhihate pūrvaṃ kāmādyairna tathā balam
jvaraḥ prāpnoti vātādyairdeho yāvanna dūṣyati
dehe cābhihate pūrvaṃ vātādyairna tathā balam
jvaraḥ prāpnoti kāmādyair mano yāvanna dūṣyati
te pūrvaṃ kevalāḥ paścānnijairvyāmiśralakṣaṇāḥ
hetvauṣadhaviśiṣṭāśca bhavantyāgantavo jvarāḥ
saṃsṛṣṭāḥ saṃnipatitāḥ pṛthagvā kupitā malāḥ
rasākhyaṃ dhātumanvetya paktiṃ sthānānnirasya ca
svena tenoṣmaṇā caiva kṛtvā dehoṣmaṇo balam
srotāṃsi ruddhvā samprāptāḥ kevalaṃ dehamulbaṇāḥ
saṃtāpamadhikaṃ dehe janayanti narastadā
bhavaty atyuṣṇasarvāṅgo jvaritastena cocyate
srotasāṃ saṃniruddhatvāt svedaṃ nā nādhigacchati
svasthānāt pracyute cāgnau prāyaśastaruṇe jvare
aruciścāvipākaśca gurutvamudarasya ca
hṛdayasyāviśuddhiśca tandrā cālasyameva ca
jvaro 'visargī balavān doṣāṇāmapravartanam
lālāpraseko hṛllāsaḥ kṣunnāśo virasaṃ mukham
stabdhasuptagurutvaṃ ca gātrāṇāṃ bahumūtratā
na viḍ jīrṇā na ca glānirjvarasyāmasya lakṣaṇam
jvaravego 'dhikastṛṣṇā pralāpaḥ śvasanaṃ bhramaḥ
malapravṛttirutkleśaḥ pacyamānasya lakṣaṇam
kṣut kṣāmatā laghutvaṃ ca gātrāṇāṃ jvaramārdavam
doṣapravṛttiraṣṭāho nirāmajvaralakṣaṇam
navajvare divāsvapnasnānābhyaṅgānnamaithunam
krodhapravātavyāyāmān kaṣāyāṃśca vivarjayet
jvare laṅghanamevādāvupadiṣṭamṛte jvarāt
kṣayānilabhayakrodhakāmaśokaśramodbhavāt
laṅghanena kṣayaṃ nīte doṣe saṃdhukṣite 'nale
vijvaratvaṃ laghutvaṃ ca kṣuccaivāsyopajāyate
prāṇāvirodhinā cainaṃ laṅghanenopapādayet
balādhiṣṭhānamārogyaṃ yadartho 'yaṃ kriyākramaḥ
laṅghanaṃ svedanaṃ kālo yavāgvastiktako rasaḥ
pācanānyavipakvānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ taruṇe jvare
tṛṣyate salilaṃ coṣṇaṃ dadyādvātakaphajvare
madyotthe paittike cātha śītalaṃ tiktakaiḥ śṛtam
dīpanaṃ pācanaṃ caiva jvaraghnamubhayaṃ hi tat
srotasāṃ śodhanaṃ balyaṃ rucisvedakaraṃ śivam
mustaparpaṭakośīracandanodīcyanāgaraiḥ
śṛtaśītaṃ jalaṃ dadyāt pipāsājvaraśāntaye
kaphapradhānānutkliṣṭān doṣānāmāśayasthitān
buddhvā jvarakarān kāle vamyānāṃ vamanairharet
anupasthitadoṣāṇāṃ vamanaṃ taruṇe jvare
hṛdrogaṃ śvāsamānāhaṃ mohaṃ ca janayedbhṛśam
sarvadehānugāḥ sāmā dhātusthā asunirharāḥ
doṣāḥ phalānāmāmānāṃ svarasā iva sātyayāḥ
vamitaṃ laṅghitaṃ kāle yavāgūbhirupācaret
yathāsvauṣadhasiddhābhirmaṇḍapūrvābhirāditaḥ
yāvajjvaramṛdūbhāvāt ṣaḍahaṃ vā vicakṣaṇaḥ
tasyāgnirdīpyate tābhiḥ samidbhiriva pāvakaḥ
tāśca bheṣajasaṃyogāllaghutvāccāgnidīpanāḥ
vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ doṣāṇāṃ cānulomanāḥ
svedanāya dravoṣṇatvād dravatvāt tṛṭpraśāntaye
āhārabhāvāt prāṇāya saratvāllāghavāya ca
jvaraghnyo jvarasātmyatvāttasmāt peyābhirāditaḥ
jvarānupacareddhīmānṛte madyasamutthitāt
madātyaye madyanitye grīṣme pittakaphādhike
ūrdhvage raktapitte ca yavāgūrna hitā jvare
tatra tarpaṇamevāgre prayojyaṃ lājasaktubhiḥ
jvarāpahaiḥ phalarasairyuktaṃ samadhuśarkaram
tataḥ sātmyabalāpekṣī bhojayejjīrṇatarpaṇam
tanunā mudgayūṣeṇa jāṅgalānāṃ rasena vā
annakāleṣu cāpyasmai vidheyaṃ dantadhāvanam
yo 'sya vaktrarasastasmādviparītaṃ priyaṃ ca yat
tadasya mukhavaiśadyaṃ prakāṅkṣāṃ cānnapānayoḥ
dhatte rasaviśeṣāṇāmabhijñatvaṃ karoti yat
viśodhya drumaśākhāgrairāsyaṃ prakṣālya cāsakṛt
mastvikṣurasamadyādyair yathāhāram avāpnuyāt
pācanaṃ śamanīyaṃ vā kaṣāyaṃ pāyayedbhiṣak
jvaritaṃ ṣaḍahe 'tīte laghvannapratibhojitam
stabhyante na vipacyante kurvanti viṣamajvaram
doṣā baddhāḥ kaṣāyeṇa stambhitvāttaruṇe jvare
na tu kalpanamuddiśya kaṣāyaḥ pratiṣidhyate
yaḥ kaṣāyakaṣāyaḥ syāt sa varjyastaruṇajvare
yūṣairamlairanamlairvā jāṅgalairvā rasairhitaiḥ
daśāhaṃ yāvadaśnīyāllaghvannaṃ jvaraśāntaye
ata ūrdhvaṃ kaphe mande vātapittottare jvare
paripakveṣu doṣeṣu sarpiṣpānaṃ yathāmṛtam
nirdaśāhamapi jñātvā kaphottaramalaṅghitam
na sarpiḥ pāyayedvaidyaḥ kaṣāyaistamupācaret
yāvallaghutvādaśanaṃ dadyānmāṃsarasena ca
balaṃ hyalaṃ nigrahāya doṣāṇāṃ balakṛcca tat
dāhatṛṣṇāparītasya vātapittottaraṃ jvaram
baddhapracyutadoṣaṃ vā nirāmaṃ payasā jayet
kriyābhirābhiḥ praśamaṃ na prayāti yadā jvaraḥ
akṣīṇabalamāṃsāgneḥ śamayettaṃ virecanaiḥ
jvarakṣīṇasya na hitaṃ vamanaṃ na virecanam
kāmaṃ tu payasā tasya nirūhairvā harenmalān
nirūho balam agniṃ ca vijvaratvaṃ mudaṃ rucim
paripakveṣu doṣeṣu prayuktaḥ śīghramāvahet
pittaṃ vā kaphapittaṃ vā pittāśayagataṃ haret
sraṃsanaṃ trīnmalān bastirharet pakvāśayasthitān
jvare purāṇe saṃkṣīṇe kaphapitte dṛḍhāgnaye
rūkṣabaddhapurīṣāya pradadyādanuvāsanam
gaurave śirasaḥ śūle vibaddheṣvindriyeṣu ca
jīrṇajvare rucikaraṃ kuryānmūrdhavirecanam
abhyaṅgāṃśca pradehāṃśca pariṣekāvagāhane
vibhajya śītoṣṇakṛtaṃ kuryājjīrṇe jvare bhiṣak
tairāśu praśamaṃ yāti bahirmārgagato jvaraḥ
labhante sukhamaṅgāni balaṃ varṇaśca vardhate
dhūpanāñjanayogaiśca yānti jīrṇajvarāḥ śamam
tvaṅmātraśeṣā yeṣāṃ ca bhavatyāganturanvayaḥ
iti kriyākramaḥ siddho jvaraghnaḥ saṃprakāśitaḥ
yeṣāṃ tveṣa kramastāni dravyāṇyūrdhvamataḥ śṛṇu
raktaśālyādayaḥ śastāḥ purāṇāḥ ṣaṣṭikaiḥ saha
yavāgvodanalājārthe jvaritānāṃ jvarāpahāḥ
lājapeyāṃ sukhajarāṃ pippalīnāgaraiḥ śṛtām
pibejjvarī jvaraharāṃ kṣudvānalpāgnirāditaḥ
amlābhilāṣī tāmeva dāḍimāmlāṃ sanāgarām
sṛṣṭaviṭ paittiko vātha śītāṃ madhuyutāṃ pibet
peyāṃ vā raktaśālīnāṃ pārśvabastiśiroruji
śvadaṃṣṭrākaṇṭakāribhyāṃ siddhāṃ jvaraharāṃ pibet
jvarātisārī peyāṃ vā pibet sāmlāṃ śṛtāṃ naraḥ
pṛśniparṇībalābilvanāgarotpaladhānyakaiḥ
śṛtāṃ vidārīgandhādyair dīpanīṃ svedanīṃ naraḥ
kāsī śvāsī ca hikkī ca yavāgūṃ jvaritaḥ pibet
vibaddhavarcāḥ sayavāṃ pippalyāmalakaiḥ śṛtām
sarpiṣmatīṃ pibet peyāṃ jvarī doṣānulomanīm
koṣṭhe vibaddhe saruji pibet peyāṃ śṛtāṃ jvarī
mṛdvīkāpippalīmūlacavyāmalakanāgaraiḥ
pibet sabilvāṃ peyāṃ vā jvare saparikartike
balāvṛkṣāmlakolāmlakalaśīdhāvanīśṛtām
asvedanidrastṛṣṇārtaḥ pibet peyāṃ saśarkarām
nāgarāmalakaiḥ siddhāṃ ghṛtabhṛṣṭāṃ jvarāpahām
mudgānmasūrāṃścaṇakān kulatthān samakuṣṭakān
yūṣārthe yūṣasātmyānāṃ jvaritānāṃ pradāpayet
paṭolapatraṃ saphalaṃ kulakaṃ pāpacelikam
karkoṭakaṃ kaṭhillaṃ ca vidyācchākaṃ jvare hitam
lāvān kapiñjalāneṇāṃścakorān upacakrakān
kuraṅgān kālapucchāṃśca hariṇān pṛṣatāñchaśān
pradadyānmāṃsasātmyāya jvaritāya jvarāpahān
īṣadamlān anamlān vā sarān kāle vicakṣaṇaḥ
kukkuṭāṃśca mayūrāṃśca tittirikrauñcavartakān
gurūṣṇatvānna śaṃsanti jvare keciccikitsakāḥ
laṅghanenānilabalaṃ jvare yadyadhikaṃ bhavet
bhiṣaṅmātrāvikalpajño dadyāttānapi kālavit
gharmāmbu cānupānārthaṃ tṛṣitāya pradāpayet
madyaṃ vā madyasātmyāya yathādoṣaṃ yathābalam
gurūṣṇasnigdhamadhurān kaṣāyāṃśca navajvare
āhārān doṣapaktyarthaṃ prāyaśaḥ parivarjayet
annapānakramaḥ siddho jvaraghnaḥ saṃprakāśitaḥ
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyante kaṣāyā jvaranāśanāḥ
pākyaṃ śītakaṣāyaṃ vā mustaparpaṭakaṃ pibet
sanāgaraṃ parpaṭakaṃ pibedvā sadurālabham
kirātatiktakaṃ mustaṃ guḍūcīṃ viśvabheṣajam
pāṭhāmuśīraṃ sodīcyaṃ pibedvā jvaraśāntaye
jvaraghnā dīpanāścaite kaṣāyā doṣapācanāḥ
tṛṣṇārucipraśamanā mukhavairasyanāśanāḥ
kaliṅgakāḥ paṭolasya patraṃ kaṭukarohiṇī
paṭolaḥ sārivā mustaṃ pāṭhā kaṭukarohiṇī
nimbaḥ paṭolastriphalā mṛdvīkā mustavatsakau
kirātatiktamamṛtā candanaṃ viśvabheṣajam
guḍūcyāmalakaṃ mustamardhaślokasamāpanāḥ
kaṣāyāḥ śamayantyāśu pañca pañcavidhāñjvarān
saṃtataṃ satatānyedyustṛtīyakacaturthakān
vatsakāragvadhau pāṭhāṃ ṣaḍgranthāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm
mūrvāṃ sātiviṣāṃ nimbaṃ paṭolaṃ dhanvayāsakam
vacāṃ mustamuśīraṃ ca madhukaṃ triphalāṃ balām
pākyaṃ śītakaṣāyaṃ vā pibejjvaraharaṃ naraḥ
madhūkamustamṛdvīkākāśmaryāṇi parūṣakam
trāyamāṇāmuśīraṃ ca triphalāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm
pītvā niśi sthitaṃ janturjvarācchīghraṃ vimucyate
jātyāmalakamustāni tadvaddhanvayavāsakam
vibaddhadoṣo jvaritaḥ kaṣāyaṃ saguḍaṃ pibet
triphalāṃ trāyamāṇāṃ ca mṛdvīkāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm
pittaśleṣmaharastveṣa kaṣāyo hyānulomikaḥ
trivṛtāśarkarāyuktaḥ pittaśleṣmajvarāpahaḥ
bṛhatyau vatsakaṃ mustaṃ devadāru mahauṣadham
kolavallī ca yogo 'yaṃ saṃnipātajvarāpahaḥ
śaṭī puṣkaramūlaṃ ca vyāghrī śṛṅgī durālabhā
guḍūcī nāgaraṃ pāṭhā kirātaṃ kaṭurohiṇī
eṣa śaṭyādiko vargaḥ sannipātajvarāpahaḥ
kāsahṛdgrahapārśvārtiśvāsatandrāsu śasyate
bṛhatyau pauṣkaraṃ bhārgī śaṭī śṛṅgī durālabhā
vatsakasya ca bījāni paṭolaṃ kaṭurohiṇī
bṛhatyādirgaṇaḥ proktaḥ sannipātajvarāpahaḥ
kāsādiṣu ca sarveṣu dadyāt sopadraveṣu ca
kaṣāyāśca yavāgvaśca pipāsājvaranāśanāḥ
nirdiṣṭā bheṣajādhyāye bhiṣaktānapi yojayet
jvarāḥ kaṣāyairvamanairlaṅghanairlaghubhojanaiḥ
rūkṣasya ye na śāmyanti sarpisteṣāṃ bhiṣagjitam
rūkṣaṃ tejo jvarakaraṃ tejasā rūkṣitasya ca
yaḥ syādanubalo dhātuḥ snehavadhyaḥ sa cānilaḥ
kaṣāyāḥ sarva evaite sarpiṣā saha yojitāḥ
prayojyā jvaraśāntyarthamagnisaṃdhukṣaṇāḥ śivāḥ
pippalyaścandanaṃ mustamuśīraṃ kaṭurohiṇī
kaliṅgakāstāmalakī sārivātiviṣā sthirā
drākṣāmalakabilvāni trāyamāṇā nidigdhikā
siddhametairghṛtaṃ sadyo jīrṇajvaramapohati
kṣayaṃ kāsaṃ śiraḥśūlaṃ pārśvaśūlaṃ halīmakam
aṃsābhitāpamagniṃ ca viṣamaṃ saṃniyacchati
vasāṃ guḍūcīṃ triphalāṃ trāyamāṇāṃ yavāsakam
paktvā tena kaṣāyeṇa payasā dviguṇena ca
pippalīmustamṛdvīkācandanotpalanāgaraiḥ
kalkīkṛtaiśca vipacedghṛtaṃ jīrṇajvarāpaham
balāṃ śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ bṛhatīṃ kalasīṃ dhāvanīṃ sthirām
nimbaṃ parpaṭakaṃ mustaṃ trāyamāṇāṃ durālabhām
kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ peṣyārthe dadyāttāmalakīṃ śaṭīm
drākṣāṃ puṣkaramūlaṃ ca medāmāmalakāni ca
ghṛtaṃ payaśca tat siddhaṃ sarpirjvaraharaṃ param
kṣayakāsaśiraḥśūlapārśvaśūlāṃsatāpanut
jvaribhyo bahudoṣebhya ūrdhvaṃ cādhaśca buddhimān
dadyāt saṃśodhanaṃ kāle kalpe yadupadekṣyate
madanaṃ pippalībhirvā kaliṅgairmadhukena vā
yuktamuṣṇāmbunā peyaṃ vamanaṃ jvaraśāntaye
kṣaudrāmbunā rasenekṣorathavā lavaṇāmbunā
jvare pracchardanaṃ śastaṃ madyairvā tarpaṇena vā
mṛdvīkāmalakānāṃ vā rasaṃ praskandanaṃ pibet
rasamāmalakānāṃ vā ghṛtabhṛṣṭaṃ jvarāpaham
lihyādvā traivṛtaṃ cūrṇaṃ saṃyuktaṃ madhusarpiṣā
pibedvā kṣaudramāvāpya saghṛtaṃ triphalārasam
āragvadhaṃ vā payasā mṛdvīkānāṃ rasena vā
trivṛtāṃ trāyamāṇāṃ vā payasā jvaritaḥ pibet
jvarādvimucyate pītvā mṛdvīkābhiḥ sahābhayām
payo 'nupānamuṣṇaṃ vā pītvā drākṣārasaṃ naraḥ
kāsācchvāsācchiraḥśūlāt pārśvaśūlāccirajvarāt
mucyate jvaritaḥ pītvā pañcamūlīśṛtaṃ payaḥ
eraṇḍamūlotkvathitaṃ jvarāt saparikartikāt
payo vimucyate pītvā tadvadbilvaśalāṭubhiḥ
trikaṇṭakabalāvyāghrīguḍanāgarasādhitam
varcomūtravibandhaghnaṃ śophajvaraharaṃ payaḥ
sanāgaraṃ samṛdvīkaṃ saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram
śṛtaṃ payaḥ sakharjūraṃ pipāsājvaranāśanam
caturguṇenāmbhasā vā śṛtaṃ jvaraharaṃ payaḥ
dhāroṣṇaṃ vā payaḥ sadyo vātapittajvaraṃ jayet
jīrṇajvarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ payaḥ praśamanaṃ param
peyaṃ taduṣṇaṃ śītaṃ vā yathāsvaṃ bheṣajaiḥ śṛtam
prayojayejjvaraharānnirūhān sānuvāsanān
pakvāśayagate doṣe vakṣyante ye ca siddhiṣu
paṭolāriṣṭapatrāṇi sośīraścaturaṅgulaḥ
hrīberaṃ rohiṇī tiktā śvadaṃṣṭrā madanāni ca
sthirā balā ca tat sarvaṃ payasyardhodake śṛtam
kṣīrāvaśeṣaṃ niryūhaṃ saṃyuktaṃ madhusarpiṣā
kalkairmadanamustānāṃ pippalyā madhukasya ca
vatsakasya ca saṃyuktaṃ bastiṃ dadyājjvarāpaham
śuddhe mārge hṛte doṣe viprasanneṣu dhātuṣu
gatāṅgaśūlo laghvaṅgaḥ sadyo bhavati vijvaraḥ
āragvadhamuśīraṃ ca madanasya phalaṃ tathā
catasraḥ parṇinīścaiva niryūhamupakalpayet
priyaṅgurmadanaṃ mustaṃ śatāhvā madhuyaṣṭikā
kalkaḥ sarpirguḍaḥ kṣaudraṃ jvaraghno bastiruttamaḥ
guḍūcīṃ trāyamāṇāṃ ca candanaṃ madhukaṃ vṛṣam
sthirāṃ balāṃ pṛśniparṇīṃ madanaṃ ceti sādhayet
rasaṃ jāṅgalamāṃsasya rasena sahitaṃ bhiṣak
pippalīphalamustānāṃ kalkena madhukasya ca
īṣatsalavaṇaṃ yuktyā nirūhaṃ madhusarpiṣā
jvarapraśamanaṃ dadyādbalasvedarucipradam
jīvantīṃ madhukaṃ medāṃ pippalīṃ madanaṃ vacām
ṛddhiṃ rāsnāṃ balāṃ viśvaṃ śatapuṣpāṃ śatāvarīm
piṣṭvā kṣīraṃ jalaṃ sarpistailaṃ ca vipacedbhiṣak
ānuvāsanikaṃ snehametaṃ vidyājjvarāpaham
paṭolapicumardābhyāṃ guḍūcyā madhukena ca
madanaiśca śṛtaḥ sneho jvaraghnamanuvāsanam
candanāgurukāśmaryapaṭolamadhukotpalaiḥ
siddhaḥ sneho jvaraharaḥ snehabastiḥ praśasyate
yaduktaṃ bheṣajādhyāye vimāne rogabheṣaje
śirovirecanaṃ kuryādyuktijñastajjvarāpaham
yacca nāvanikaṃ tailaṃ yāśca prāgdhūmavartayaḥ
mātrāśitīye nirdiṣṭāḥ prayojyāstā jvareṣvapi
abhyaṅgāṃśca pradehāṃśca pariṣekāṃśca kārayet
yathābhilāṣaṃ śītoṣṇaṃ vibhajya dvividhaṃ jvaram
sahasradhautaṃ sarpirvā tailaṃ vā candanādikam
dāhajvarapraśamanaṃ dadyād abhyañjanaṃ bhiṣak
atha candanādyaṃ tailamupadekṣyāmaḥ candanabhadraśrīkālānusāryakālīyakapadmāpadmakośīrasārivāmadhukaprapauṇḍarīka nāgapuṣpodīcyavanyapadmotpalanalinakumudasaugandhikapuṇḍarīkaśatapatrabisamṛṇāla śālūkaśaivālakaśerukānantākuśakāśekṣudarbhaśaranalaśālimūlajambuvetasavānīragundrākakubhāsanāśvakarṇasyandana vātapothaśālatāladhavatiniśakhadirakadarakadambakāśmaryaphalasarjaplakṣavaṭakapītanodumbarāśvattha nyagrodhadhātakīdūrvetkaṭaśṛṅgāṭakamañjiṣṭhājyotiṣmatīpuṣkarabījakrauñcādanabadarīkovidārakadalīsaṃvartakāriṣṭaśataparvāśītakumbhikā śatāvarīśrīparṇīśrāvaṇīmahāśrāvaṇīrohiṇīśītapākyodanapākīkālābalāpayasyāvidārījīvakarṣabhakamedāmahāmedā madhurasarṣyaproktātṛṇaśūnyamocarasāṭarūṣakabakulakuṭajapaṭolanimbaśālmalīnārikelakharjūramṛdvīkāpriyālapriyaṅgudhanvanātmaguptāmadhūkānām anyeṣāṃ ca śītavīryāṇāṃ yathālābhamauṣadhānāṃ kaṣāyaṃ kārayet
tena kaṣāyeṇa dviguṇitapayasā teṣāmeva ca kalkena kaṣāyārdhamātraṃ mṛdvagninā sādhayettailam
etat tailamabhyaṅgāt sadyo dāhajvaramapanayati
etaireva cauṣadhairaślakṣṇapiṣṭaiḥ suśītaiḥ pradehaṃ kārayet
etaireva ca śṛtaśītaṃ salilamavagāhapariṣekārthaṃ prayuñjīta
iti candanādyaṃ tailam
madhvāranālakṣīradadhighṛtasalilasekāvagāhāśca sadyo dāhajvaramapanayanti śītasparśatvāt
bhavanti cātra
pauṣkareṣu suśīteṣu padmotpaladaleṣu ca
kadalīnāṃ ca patreṣu kṣaumeṣu vimaleṣu ca
candanodakaśīteṣu śīte dhārāgṛhe 'pi vā
himāmbusikte sadane dāhārtaḥ saṃviśet sukham
hemaśaṅkhapravālānāṃ maṇīnāṃ mauktikasya ca
candanodakaśītānāṃ saṃsparśānurasān spṛśet
sragbhirnīlotpalaiḥ padmairvyajanairvividhairapi
śītavātāvahair vyajyeccandanodakavarṣibhiḥ
nadyastaḍāgāḥ padminyo hradāśca vimalodakāḥ
avagāhe hitā dāhatṛṣṇāglānijvarāpahāḥ
priyāḥ pradakṣiṇācārāḥ pramadāścandanokṣitāḥ
sāntvayeyuḥ paraiḥ kāmairmaṇimauktikabhūṣaṇāḥ
śītāni cānnapānāni śītānyupavanāni ca
vāyavaścandrapādāśca śītā dāhajvarāpahāḥ
athoṣṇābhiprāyiṇāṃ jvaritānām abhyaṅgādīn upakramān upadekṣyāmaḥ agurukuṣṭhatagarapatranaladaśaileyadhyāmakahareṇukāsthauṇeyaka kṣemakailāvarāṅgadalapuratamālapatrabhūtīkarohiṣasaralaśallakī devadārvagnimanthabilvasyonākakāśmaryapāṭalāpunarnavā vṛścīrakaṇṭakārībṛhatīśālaparṇīpṛśniparṇīmāṣaparṇīmudgaparṇīgokṣurakairaṇḍaśobhāñjanakavaruṇārkacirabilvatilvaka śaṭīpuṣkaramūlagaṇḍīrorubūkapattūrākṣīvāśmantakaśigrumātuluṅgapīlukamūlakaparṇītilaparṇīpīluparṇīmeṣaśṛṅgī hiṃsrādantaśaṭhairāvatakabhallātakāsphotakāṇḍīrātmajaikeṣīkākarañjadhānyakājamodapṛthvīkāsumukhasurasakuṭherakakālamālakaparṇāsakṣavakaphaṇijjhaka bhūstṛṇaśṛṅgaverapippalīsarṣapāśvagandhārāsnāruhārohāvacābalātibalāguḍūcī śatapuṣpāśītavallīnākulīgandhanākulīśvetājyotiṣmatīcitrakādhyaṇḍāmlacāṅgerītilabadarakulatthamāṣāṇām evaṃvidhānām anyeṣāṃ coṣṇavīryāṇāṃ yathālābhamauṣadhānāṃ kaṣāyaṃ kārayet tena kaṣāyeṇa teṣāmeva ca kalkena surāsauvīrakatuṣodakamaireyamedakadadhimaṇḍāranālakaṭvaraprativinītena tailapātraṃ vipācayet
tena sukhoṣṇena tailenoṣṇābhiprāyiṇaṃ jvaritamabhyañjyāt tathā śītajvaraḥ praśāmyati etaireva cauṣadhaiḥ ślakṣṇapiṣṭaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ pradehaṃ kārayet etaireva ca śṛtaṃ sukhoṣṇaṃ salilamavagāhanārthaṃ pariṣekārthaṃ ca prayuñjīta śītajvarapraśamārtham
bhavanti cātra
trayodaśavidhaḥ svedaḥ svedādhyāye nidarśitaḥ
mātrākālavidā yuktaḥ sa ca śītajvarāpahaḥ
sā kuṭī tacca śayanaṃ taccāvacchādanaṃ jvaram
śītaṃ praśamayantyāśu dhūpāścāgurujā ghanāḥ
cārūpacitagātryaśca taruṇyo yauvanoṣmaṇā
āśleṣācchamayantyāśu pramadāḥ śiśirajvaram
svedanānyannapānāni vātaśleṣmaharāṇi ca
śītajvaraṃ jayantyāśu saṃsargabalayojanāt
vātaje śramaje caiva purāṇe kṣataje jvare
laṅghanaṃ na hitaṃ vidyācchamanaistānupācaret
vikṣipyāmāśayoṣmāṇaṃ yasmādgatvā rasaṃ nṛṇām
jvaraṃ kurvanti doṣāstu hīyate 'gnibalaṃ tataḥ
yathā prajvalito vahniḥ sthālyāmindhanavānapi
na pacatyodanaṃ samyaganilaprerito bahiḥ
paktisthānāttathā doṣairūṣmā kṣipto bahirnṛṇām
na pacatyabhyavahṛtaṃ kṛcchrāt pacati vā laghu
ato 'gnibalarakṣārthaṃ laṅghanādikramo hitaḥ
saptāhena hi pacyante saptadhātugatā malāḥ
nirāmaścāpyataḥ prokto jvaraḥ prāyo 'ṣṭame 'hani
udīrṇadoṣas tvalpāgnir aśnan guru viśeṣataḥ
mucyate sahasā prāṇaiściraṃ kliśyati vā naraḥ
etasmātkāraṇādvidvān vātike 'pyādito jvare
nāti gurvati vā snigdhaṃ bhojayet sahasā naram
jvare mārutaje tv ādāv anapekṣyāpi hi kramam
kuryānniranubandhānāmabhyaṅgādīnupakramān
pāyayitvā kaṣāyaṃ ca bhojayedrasabhojanam
jīrṇajvaraharaṃ kuryāt sarvaśaścāpyupakramam
śleṣmalānāmavātānāṃ jvaro 'nuṣṇaḥ kaphādhikaḥ
paripākaṃ na saptāhenāpi yāti mṛdūṣmaṇām
taṃ krameṇa yathoktena laṅghanālpāśanādinā
ā daśāham upakramya kaṣāyādyairupācaret
sāmā ye ye ca kaphajāḥ kaphapittajvarāśca ye
laṅghanaṃ laṅghanīyoktaṃ teṣu kāryaṃ prati prati
vamanaiśca virekaiśca bastibhiśca yathākramam
jvarānupacareddhīmān kaphapittānilodbhavān
saṃsṛṣṭān saṃnipatitān buddhvā taratamaiḥ samaiḥ
jvarān doṣakramāpekṣī yathoktairauṣadhairjayet
vardhanenaikadoṣasya kṣapaṇenocchritasya vā
kaphasthānānupūrvyā vā sannipātajvaraṃ jayet
sannipātajvarasyānte karṇamūle sudāruṇaḥ
śothaḥ saṃjāyate tena kaścideva pramucyate
raktāvasecanaiḥ śīghraṃ sarpiṣpānaiśca taṃ jayet
pradehaiḥ kaphapittaghnairnāvanaiḥ kavalagrahaiḥ
śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣādyairjvaro yasya na śāmyati
śākhānusārī raktasya so 'vasekāt praśāmyati
visarpeṇābhighātena yaśca visphoṭakairjvaraḥ
tatrādau sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ kaphapittottaro na cet
daurbalyāddehadhātūnāṃ jvaro jīrṇo 'nuvartate
balyaiḥ saṃbṛṃhaṇais tasmād āhārais tam upācaret
karma sādhāraṇaṃ jahyāttṛtīyakacaturthakau
āganturanubandho hi prāyaśo viṣamajvare
vātapradhānaṃ sarpirbhirbastibhiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ
snigdhoṣṇairannapānaiśca śamayedviṣamajvaram
virecanena payasā sarpiṣā saṃskṛtena ca
viṣamaṃ tiktaśītaiśca jvaraṃ pittottaraṃ jayet
vamanaṃ pācanaṃ rūkṣamannapānaṃ vilaṅghanam
kaṣāyoṣṇaṃ ca viṣame jvare śastaṃ kaphottare
yogāḥ parāḥ pravakṣyante viṣamajvaranāśanāḥ
prayoktavyā matimatā doṣādīn pravibhajya te
surā samaṇḍā pānārthe bhakṣyārthe caraṇāyudhaḥ
tittiriśca mayūraśca prayojyā viṣamajvare
pibedvā ṣaṭpalaṃ sarpirabhayāṃ vā prayojayet
triphalāyāḥ kaṣāyaṃ vā guḍūcyā rasameva vā
nīlinīmajagandhāṃ ca trivṛtāṃ kaṭurohiṇīm
pibejjvarāgame yuktyā snehasvedopapāditaḥ
sarpiṣo mahatīṃ mātrāṃ pītvā vā chardayet punaḥ
upayujyānnapānaṃ vā prabhūtaṃ punarullikhet
sānnaṃ madyaṃ prabhūtaṃ vā pītvā svapyājjvarāgame
āsthāpanaṃ yāpanaṃ vā kārayedviṣamajvare
payasā vṛṣadaṃśasya śakṛdvā tadahaḥ pibet
vṛṣasya dadhimaṇḍena surayā vā sasaindhavam
pippalyāstriphalāyāśca dadhnastakrasya sarpiṣaḥ
pañcagavyasya payasaḥ prayogo viṣamajvare
rasonasya satailasya prāgbhaktamupasevanam
medyānāmuṣṇavīryāṇāmāmiṣāṇāṃ ca bhakṣaṇam
hiṅgutulyā tu vaiyāghrī vasā nasyaṃ sasaindhavā
purāṇasarpiḥ siṃhasya vasā tadvat sasaindhavā
saindhavaṃ pippalīnāṃ ca taṇḍulāḥ samanaḥśilāḥ
netrāñjanaṃ tailapiṣṭaṃ śasyate viṣamajvare
palaṅkaṣā nimbapatraṃ vacā kuṣṭhaṃ harītakī
sarṣapāḥ sayavāḥ sarpirdhūpanaṃ jvaranāśanam
ye dhūmā dhūpanaṃ yacca nāvanaṃ cāñjanaṃ ca yat
manovikāre nirdiṣṭaṃ kāryaṃ tadviṣamajvare
maṇīnāmoṣadhīnāṃ ca maṅgalyānāṃ viṣasya ca
dhāraṇādagadānāṃ ca sevanānna bhavejjvaraḥ
somaṃ sānucaraṃ devaṃ samātṛgaṇamīśvaram
pūjayan prayataḥ śīghraṃ mucyate viṣamajvarāt
viṣṇuṃ sahasramūrdhānaṃ carācarapatiṃ vibhum
stuvannāmasahasreṇa jvarān sarvānapohati
brahmāṇamaśvināvindraṃ hutabhakṣaṃ himācalam
gaṅgāṃ marudgaṇāṃś ceṣṭyā pūjayañjayati jvarān
bhaktyā mātuḥ pituścaiva gurūṇāṃ pūjanena ca
brahmacaryeṇa tapasā satyena niyamena ca
japahomapradānena vedānāṃ śravaṇena ca
jvarādvimucyate śīghraṃ sādhūnāṃ darśanena ca
jvare rasasthe vamanamupavāsaṃ ca kārayet
sekapradehau raktasthe tathā saṃśamanāni ca
virecanaṃ sopavāsaṃ māṃsamedaḥsthite hitam
asthimajjagate deyā nirūhāḥ sānuvāsanāḥ
śāpābhicārādbhūtānāmabhiṣaṅgācca yo jvaraḥ
daivavyapāśrayaṃ tatra sarvamauṣadhamiṣyate
abhighātajvaro naśyet pānābhyaṅgena sarpiṣaḥ
raktāvasekairmadyaiśca sātmyairmāṃsarasaudanaiḥ
sānāho madyasātmyānāṃ madirārasabhojanaiḥ
kṣatānāṃ vraṇitānāṃ ca kṣatavraṇacikitsayā
āśvāseneṣṭalābhena vāyoḥ praśamanena ca
harṣaṇaiśca śamaṃ yānti kāmaśokabhayajvarāḥ
kāmyairarthairmanojñaiśca pittaghnaiścāpyupakramaiḥ
sadvākyaiśca śamaṃ yāti jvaraḥ krodhasamutthitaḥ
kāmāt krodhajvaro nāśaṃ krodhāt kāmasamudbhavaḥ
yāti tābhyāmubhābhyāṃ ca bhayaśokasamutthitaḥ
jvarasya vegaṃ kālaṃ ca cintayañjvaryate tu yaḥ
jvarapramokṣe puruṣaḥ kūjan vamati ceṣṭate
śvasanvivarṇaḥ svinnāṅgo vepate līyate muhuḥ
pralapatyuṣṇasarvāṅgaḥ śītāṅgaśca bhavatyapi
visaṃjño jvaravegārtaḥ sakrodha iva vīkṣyate
sadoṣaśabdaṃ ca śakṛddravaṃ sravati vegavat
liṅgānyetāni jānīyājjvaramokṣe vicakṣaṇaḥ
bahudoṣasya balavān prāyeṇābhinavo jvaraḥ
satkriyādoṣapaktyā cedvimuñcati sudāruṇam
kṛtvā doṣavaśādvegaṃ kramāduparamanti ye
teṣāmadāruṇo mokṣo jvarāṇāṃ cirakāriṇām
vigataklamasaṃtāpamavyathaṃ vimalendriyam
yuktaṃ prakṛtisattvena vidyāt puruṣam ajvaram
sajvaro jvaramuktaśca vidāhīni gurūṇi ca
asātmyānyannapānāni viruddhāni ca varjayet
vyavāyamaticeṣṭāśca snānamatyaśanāni ca
tathā jvaraḥ śamaṃ yāti praśānto jāyate na ca
vyāyāmaṃ ca vyavāyaṃ ca snānaṃ caṅkramaṇāni ca
jvaramukto na seveta yāvanna balavān bhavet
asaṃjātabalo yastu jvaramukto niṣevate
varjyametannarastasya punarāvartate jvaraḥ
durhṛteṣu ca doṣeṣu yasya vā vinivartate
svalpenāpyapacāreṇa tasya vyāvartate punaḥ
cirakālaparikliṣṭaṃ durbalaṃ hīnatejasam
acireṇaiva kālena sa hanti punarāgataḥ
athavāpi parīpākaṃ dhātuṣveva kramānmalāḥ
yānti jvaramakurvantaste tathāpyapakurvate
dīnatāṃ śvayathuṃ glāniṃ pāṇḍutāṃ nānnakāmatām
kaṇḍūrutkoṭhapiḍakāḥ kurvantyagniṃ ca te mṛdum
evamanye 'pi ca gadā vyāvartante punargatāḥ
anirghātena doṣāṇām alpair apyahitair nṝṇām
nirvṛtte 'pi jvare tasmādyathāvasthaṃ yathābalam
yathāprāṇaṃ hareddoṣaṃ prayogairvā śamaṃ nayet
mṛdubhiḥ śodhanaiḥ śuddhiryāpanā bastayo hitāḥ
hitāśca laghavo yūṣā jāṅgalāmiṣajā rasāḥ
abhyaṅgodvartanasnānadhūpanānyañjanāni ca
hitāni punarāvṛtte jvare tiktaghṛtāni ca
gurvyabhiṣyandyasātmyānāṃ bhojanāt punarāgate
laṅghanoṣṇopacārādiḥ kramaḥ kāryaśca pūrvavat
kirātatiktakaṃ tiktā mustaṃ parpaṭako 'mṛtā
ghnanti pītāni cābhyāsāt punarāvartakaṃ jvaram
tasyāṃ tasyāmavasthāyāṃ jvaritānāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ
jvarakriyākramāpekṣī kuryāttattaccikitsitam
rogarāṭ sarvabhūtānāmantakṛddāruṇo jvaraḥ
tasmādviśeṣatastasya yateta praśame bhiṣak
tatra ślokaḥ
yathākramaṃ yathāpraśnamuktaṃ jvaracikitsitam
ātreyeṇāgniveśāya bhūtānāṃ hitakāmyayā
athāto raktapittacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
viharantaṃ jitātmānaṃ pañcagaṅge punarvasum
praṇamyovāca nirmohamagniveśo 'gnivarcasam
bhagavan raktapittasya heturuktaḥ salakṣaṇaḥ
vaktavyaṃ yat paraṃ tasya vaktumarhasi tadguro
gururuvāca
mahāgadaṃ mahāvegam agnivacchīghrakāri ca
hetulakṣaṇavicchīghraṃ raktapittamupācaret
tasyoṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇamamlaṃ ca kaṭūni lavaṇāni ca
gharmaścānnavidāhaśca hetuḥ pūrvaṃ nidarśitaḥ
tairhetubhiḥ samutkliṣṭaṃ pittaṃ raktaṃ prapadyate
tadyonitvāt prapannaṃ ca vardhate tat pradūṣayat
tasyoṣmaṇā dravo dhāturdhātordhātoḥ prasicyate
svidyatastena saṃvṛddhiṃ bhūyastadadhigacchati
saṃyogād dūṣaṇāttattu sāmānyādgandhavarṇayoḥ
raktasya pittamākhyātaṃ raktapittaṃ manīṣibhiḥ
plīhānaṃ ca yakṛccaiva tadadhiṣṭhāya vartate
srotāṃsi raktavāhīni tanmūlāni hi dehinām
sāndraṃ sapāṇḍu sasnehaṃ picchilaṃ ca kaphānvitam
śyāvāruṇaṃ saphenaṃ ca tanu rūkṣaṃ ca vātikam
raktapittaṃ kaṣāyābhaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gomūtrasaṃnibham
mecakāgāradhūmābhamañjanābhaṃ ca paittikam
saṃsṛṣṭaliṅgaṃ saṃsargāttriliṅgaṃ sānnipātikam
ekadoṣānugaṃ sādhyaṃ dvidoṣaṃ yāpyamucyate
yattridoṣamasādhyaṃ tanmandāgner ativegavat
vyādhibhiḥ kṣīṇadehasya vṛddhasyānaśnataśca yat
gatirūrdhvamadhaścaiva raktapittasya darśitā
ūrdhvā saptavidhadvārā dvidvārā tvadharā gatiḥ
sapta chidrāṇi śirasi dve cādhaḥ sādhyamūrdhvagam
yāpyaṃ tvadhogaṃ mārgau tu dvāvasādhyaṃ prapadyate
yadā tu sarvacchidrebhyo romakūpebhya eva ca
vartate tām asaṃkhyeyāṃ gatiṃ tasyāhur āntikīm
yaccobhayābhyāṃ mārgābhyāmatimātraṃ pravartate
tulyaṃ kuṇapagandhena raktaṃ kṛṣṇamatīva ca
saṃsṛṣṭaṃ kaphavātābhyāṃ kaṇṭhe sajati cāpi yat
yaccāpyupadravaiḥ sarvairyathoktaiḥ samabhidrutam
hāridranīlaharitatāmrair varṇair upadrutam
kṣīṇasya kāsamānasya yacca tacca na sidhyati
yaddvidoṣānugaṃ yadvā śāntaṃ śāntaṃ prakupyati
mārgānmārgaṃ caredyadvā yāpyaṃ pittamasṛk ca tat
ekamārgaṃ balavato nātivegaṃ navotthitam
raktapittaṃ sukhe kāle sādhyaṃ syānnirupadravam
snigdhoṣṇamuṣṇarūkṣaṃ ca raktapittasya kāraṇam
adhogasyottaraṃ prāyaḥ pūrvaṃ syādūrdhvagasya tu
ūrdhvagaṃ kaphasaṃsṛṣṭamadhogaṃ mārutānugam
dvimārgaṃ kaphavātābhyāmubhābhyāmanubadhyate
akṣīṇabalamāṃsasya raktapittaṃ yadaśnataḥ
taddoṣaduṣṭam utkliṣṭaṃ nādau stambhanamarhati
galagrahaṃ pūtinasyaṃ mūrcchāyamaruciṃ jvaram
gulmaṃ plīhānamānāhaṃ kilāsaṃ kṛcchramūtratām
kuṣṭhānyarśāṃsi vīsarpaṃ varṇanāśaṃ bhagandaram
buddhīndriyoparodhaṃ ca kuryāt sambhitam āditaḥ
tasmādupekṣyaṃ balino baladoṣavicāriṇā
raktapittaṃ prathamataḥ pravṛddhaṃ siddhimicchatā
prāyeṇa hi samutkliṣṭamāmadoṣāccharīriṇām
vṛddhiṃ prayāti pittāsṛk tasmāttallaṅghyam āditaḥ
mārgau doṣānubandhaṃ ca nidānaṃ prasamīkṣya ca
laṅghanaṃ raktapittādau tarpaṇaṃ vā prayojayet
hrīberacandanośīramustaparpaṭakaiḥ śṛtam
kevalaṃ śṛtaśītaṃ vā dadyāttoyaṃ pipāsave
ūrdhvage tarpaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ peyāṃ pūrvamadhogate
kālasātmyānubandhajño dadyāt prakṛtikalpavit
jalaṃ kharjūramṛdvīkāmadhūkaiḥ saparūṣakaiḥ
śṛtaśītaṃ prayoktavyaṃ tarpaṇārthe saśarkaram
tarpaṇaṃ saghṛtakṣaudraṃ lājacūrṇaiḥ pradāpayet
ūrdhvagaṃ raktapittaṃ tat pītaṃ kāle vyapohati
mandāgneramlasātmyāya tat sāmlamapi kalpayet
dāḍimāmalakairvidvānamlārthaṃ cānudāpayet
śāliṣaṣṭikanīvārakoradūṣapraśāntikāḥ
śyāmākaśca priyaṅguśca bhojanaṃ raktapittinām
mudgā masūrāścaṇakāḥ samakuṣṭhāḍhakīphalāḥ
praśastāḥ sūpayūṣārthe kalpitā raktapittinām
paṭolanimbavetrāgraplakṣavetasapallavāḥ
kirātatiktakaṃ śākaṃ gaṇḍīraḥ sakaṭhillakaḥ
kovidārasya puṣpāṇi kāśmaryasyātha śālmaleḥ
annapānavidhau śākaṃ yaccānyadraktapittanut
śākārthaṃ śākasātmyānāṃ tacchastaṃ raktapittinām
svinnaṃ vā sarpiṣā bhṛṣṭaṃ yūṣavadvā vipācitam
pārāvatān kapotāṃśca lāvān raktākṣavartakān
śaśān kapiñjalāneṇān hariṇānkālapucchakān
raktapitte hitān vidyādrasāṃsteṣāṃ prayojayet
īṣadamlānanamlān vā ghṛtabhṛṣṭān saśarkarān
kaphānuge yūṣaśākaṃ dadyādvātānuge rasam
raktapitte yavāgūnāmataḥ kalpaḥ pravakṣyate
padmotpalānāṃ kiñjalkaḥ pṛśniparṇī priyaṅgukāḥ
jale sādhyā rase tasmin peyā syādraktapittinām
candanośīralodhrāṇāṃ rase tadvat sanāgare
kirātatiktakośīramustānāṃ tadvadeva ca
dhātakīdhanvayāsāmbubilvānāṃ vā rase śṛtā
masūrapṛśniparṇyorvā sthirāmudgarase 'thavā
rase hareṇukānāṃ vā saghṛte sabalārase
siddhāḥ pārāvatādīnāṃ rase vā syuḥ pṛthakpṛthak
ityuktā raktapittaghnyaḥ śītāḥ samadhuśarkarāḥ
yavāgvaḥ kalpanā caiṣā kāryā māṃsaraseṣvapi
śaśaḥ savāstukaḥ śasto vibandhe raktapittinām
vātolbaṇe tittiriḥ syādudumbararase śṛtaḥ
mayūraḥ plakṣaniryūhe nyagrodhasya ca kukkuṭaḥ
rase bilvotpalādīnāṃ vartakakrakarau hitau
tṛṣyate tiktakaiḥ siddhaṃ tṛṣṇāghnaṃ vā phalodakam
siddhaṃ vidārigandhādyairathavā śṛtaśītalam
jñātvā doṣāvanubalau balamāhārameva ca
jalaṃ pipāsave dadyādvisargādalpaśo 'pi vā
nidānaṃ raktapittasya yatkiṃcit saṃprakāśitam
jīvitārogyakāmaistanna sevyaṃ raktapittibhiḥ
ityannapānaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ kramaśo raktapittanut
vakṣyate bahudoṣāṇāṃ kāryaṃ balavatāṃ ca yat
akṣīṇabalamāṃsasya yasya saṃtarpaṇotthitam
bahudoṣaṃ balavato raktapittaṃ śarīriṇaḥ
kāle saṃśodhanārhasya taddharennirupadravam
virecanenordhvabhāgamadhogaṃ vamanena ca
trivṛtāmabhayāṃ prājñaḥ phalānyāragvadhasya vā
trāyamāṇāṃ gavākṣyā vā mūlamāmalakāni vā
virecanaṃ prayuñjīta prabhūtamadhuśarkaram
rasaḥ praśasyate teṣāṃ raktapitte viśeṣataḥ
vamanaṃ madanonmiśro manthaḥ sakṣaudraśarkaraḥ
saśarkaraṃ vā salilamikṣūṇāṃ rasa eva vā
vatsakasya phalaṃ mustaṃ madanaṃ madhukaṃ madhu
adhovahe raktapitte vamanaṃ paramucyate
ūrdhvage śuddhakoṣṭhasya tarpaṇādiḥ kramo hitaḥ
adhogate yavāgvādirna cetsyānmāruto balī
balamāṃsaparikṣīṇaṃ śokabhārādhvakarśitam
jvalanādityasaṃtaptamanyairvā kṣīṇamāmayaiḥ
garbhiṇīṃ sthaviraṃ bālaṃ rūkṣālpapramitāśinam
avamyamavirecyaṃ vā yaṃ paśyedraktapittinam
śoṣeṇa sānubandhaṃ vā tasya saṃśamanī kriyā
śasyate raktapittasya paraṃ sātha pravakṣyate
aṭarūṣakamṛdvīkāpathyākvāthaḥ saśarkaraḥ
madhumiśraḥ śvāsakāsaraktapittanibarhaṇaḥ
aṭarūṣakaniryūhe priyaṅguṃ mṛttikāñjane
vinīya lodhraṃ kṣaudraṃ ca raktapittaharaṃ pibet
padmakaṃ padmakiñjalkaṃ dūrvāṃ vāstūkamutpalam
nāgapuṣpaṃ ca lodhraṃ ca tenaiva vidhinā pibet
prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ madhu cāśvaśakṛdrase
yavāsabhṛṅgarajasormūlaṃ vā gośakṛdrase
vinīya raktapittaghnaṃ peyaṃ syāttaṇḍulāmbunā
yuktaṃ vā madhusarpirbhyāṃ lihyād go'śvaśakṛdrasam
khadirasya priyaṅgūṇāṃ kovidārasya śālmaleḥ
puṣpacūrṇāni madhunā lihyānnā raktapittikaḥ
śṛṅgāṭakānāṃ lājānāṃ mustakharjūrayorapi
lihyāccūrṇāni madhunā padmānāṃ keśarasya ca
dhanvajānāmasṛglihyānmadhunā mṛgapakṣiṇām
sakṣaudraṃ grathite rakte lihyāt pārāvataṃ śakṛt
uśīrakālīyakalodhrapadmakapriyaṅgukākaṭphalaśaṅkhagairikāḥ
pṛthak pṛthak candanatulyabhāgikāḥ saśarkarāstaṇḍuladhāvanāplutāḥ
raktaṃ sapittaṃ tamakaṃ pipāsāṃ dāhaṃ ca pītāḥ śamayanti sadyaḥ
kirātatiktaṃ kramukaṃ samustaṃ prapauṇḍarīkaṃ kamalotpale ca
hrīberamūlāni paṭolapatraṃ durālabhā parpaṭako mṛṇālam
dhanañjayodumbaravetasatvaṅnyagrodhaśāleyayavāsakatvak
tugālatāvetasataṇḍulīyaṃ sasārivaṃ mocarasaḥ samaṅgā
pṛthak pṛthak candanayojitāni tenaiva kalpena hitāni tatra
niśi sthitā vā svarasīkṛtā vā kalkīkṛtā vā mṛditāḥ śṛtā vā
ete samastā gaṇaśaḥ pṛthagvā raktaṃ sapittaṃ śamayanti yogāḥ
mudgāḥ salājāḥ sayavāḥ sakṛṣṇāḥ sośīramustāḥ saha candanena
balājale paryuṣitāḥ kaṣāyā raktaṃ sapittaṃ śamayantyudīrṇam
vaidūryamuktāmaṇigairikāṇāṃ mṛcchaṅkhahemāmalakodakānām
madhūdakasyekṣurasasya caiva pānācchamaṃ gacchati raktapittam
uśīrapadmotpalacandanānāṃ pakvasya loṣṭasya ca yaḥ prasādaḥ
saśarkaraḥ kṣaudrayutaḥ suśīto raktātiyogapraśamāya deyaḥ
priyaṅgukācandanalodhrasārivāmadhūkamustābhayadhātakījalam
samṛtprasādaṃ saha yaṣṭikāmbunā saśarkaraṃ raktanibarhaṇaṃ param
kaṣāyayogairvividhairyathoktairdīpte 'nale śleṣmaṇi nirjite ca
yadraktapittaṃ praśamaṃ na yāti tatrānilaḥ syādanu tatra kāryam
chāgaṃ payaḥ syāt paramaṃ prayoge gavyaṃ śṛtaṃ pañcaguṇe jale vā
saśarkaraṃ mākṣikasamprayuktaṃ vidārigandhādigaṇaiḥ śṛtaṃ vā
drākṣāśṛtaṃ nāgarakaiḥ śṛtaṃ vā balāśṛtaṃ gokṣurakaiḥ śṛtaṃ vā
sajīvakaṃ sarṣabhakaṃ sasarpiḥ payaḥ prayojyaṃ sitayā śṛtaṃ vā
śatāvarīgokṣurakaiḥ śṛtaṃ vā śṛtaṃ payo vāpyatha parṇinībhiḥ
raktaṃ nihantyāśu viśeṣatastu yanmūtramārgāt sarujaṃ prayāti
viśeṣato viṭpathasampravṛtte payo mataṃ mocarasena siddham
vaṭāvarohair vaṭaśuṅgakair vā hrīberanīlotpalanāgarairvā
kaṣāyayogān payasā purā vā pītvānu cādyāt payasaiva śālīn
kaṣāyayogairathavā vipakvametaiḥ pibet sarpiratisrave ca
vāsāṃ saśākhāṃ sapalāśamūlāṃ kṛtvā kaṣāyaṃ kusumāni cāsyāḥ
pradāya kalkaṃ vipacedghṛtaṃ tat sakṣaudramāśveva nihanti raktam
iti vāsāghṛtam
palāśavṛntasvarasena siddhaṃ tasyaiva kalkena madhudraveṇa
lihyādghṛtaṃ vatsakakalkasiddhaṃ tadvat samaṅgotpalalodhrasiddham
syāttrāyamāṇāvidhireṣa eva sodumbare caiva paṭolapatre
sarpīṃṣi pittajvaranāśanāni sarvāṇi śastāni ca raktapitte
abhyaṅgayogāḥ pariṣecanāni sekāvagāhāḥ śayanāni veśma
śīto vidhirbastividhānamagryaṃ pittajvare yat praśamāya diṣṭam
tadraktapitte nikhilena kāryaṃ kālaṃ ca mātrāṃ ca purā samīkṣya
sarpirguḍā ye ca hitāḥ kṣatebhyaste raktapittaṃ śamayanti sadyaḥ
kaphānubandhe rudhire sapitte kaṇṭhāgate syādgrathite prayogaḥ
yuktasya yuktyā madhusarpiṣośca kṣārasya caivotpalanālajasya
mṛṇālapadmotpalakeśarāṇāṃ tathā palāśasya tathā priyaṅgoḥ
tathā madhūkasya tathāsanasya kṣārāḥ prayojyā vidhinaiva tena
śatāvarīdāḍimatintiḍīkaṃ kākolimede madhukaṃ vidārīm
piṣṭvā ca mūlaṃ phalapūrakasya ghṛtaṃ pacet kṣīracaturguṇaṃ jñaḥ
kāsajvarānāhavibandhaśūlaṃ tadraktapittaṃ ca ghṛtaṃ nihanyāt
yat pañcamūlairatha pañcabhirvā siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ tacca tadarthakāri
iti śatāvaryādighṛtam
kaṣāyayogā ya ihopadiṣṭāste cāvapīḍe bhiṣajā prayojyāḥ
ghrāṇāt pravṛttaṃ rudhiraṃ sapītaṃ yadā bhavenniḥsṛtaduṣṭadoṣam
rakte praduṣṭe hyavapīḍabandhe duṣṭapratiśyāyaśirovikārāḥ
raktaṃ sapūyaṃ kuṇapaśca gandhaḥ syād ghrāṇanāśaḥ kṛmayaśca duṣṭāḥ
nīlotpalaṃ gairikaśaṅkhayuktaṃ sacandanaṃ syāttu sitājalena
nasyaṃ tathāmrāsthirasaḥ samaṅgā sadhātakīmocarasaḥ salodhraḥ
drākṣārasasyekṣurasasya nasyaṃ kṣīrasya dūrvāsvarasasya caiva
yavāsamūlāni palāṇḍumūlaṃ nasyaṃ tathā dāḍimapuṣpatoyam
priyālatailaṃ madhukaṃ payaśca siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ māhiṣam ājikaṃ vā
āmrāsthipūrvaiḥ payasā ca nasyaṃ sasārivaiḥ syāt kamalotpalaiśca
bhadraśriyaṃ lohitacandanaṃ ca prapauṇḍarīkaṃ kamalotpale ca
uśīravānīrajalaṃ mṛṇālaṃ sahasravīryā madhukaṃ payasyā
śālīkṣumūlāni yavāsagundrāmūlaṃ nalānāṃ kuśakāśayośca
kucandanaṃ śaivalamapyanantā kālānusāryā tṛṇamūlamṛddhiḥ
mūlāni puṣpāṇi ca vārijānāṃ pralepanaṃ puṣkariṇīmṛdaśca
udumbarāśvatthamadhūkalodhrāḥ kaṣāyavṛkṣāḥ śiśirāśca sarve
pradehakalpe pariṣecane ca tathāvagāhe ghṛtatailasiddhau
raktasya pittasya ca śāntimicchan bhadraśriyādīni bhiṣak prayuñjyāt
dhārāgṛhaṃ bhūmigṛhaṃ suśītaṃ vanaṃ ca ramyaṃ jalavātaśītam
vaidūryamuktāmaṇibhājanānāṃ sparśāśca dāhe śiśirāmbuśītāḥ
patrāṇi puṣpāṇi ca vārijānāṃ kṣaumaṃ ca śītaṃ kadalīdalāni
pracchādanārthaṃ śayanāsanānāṃ padmotpalānāṃ ca dalāḥ praśastāḥ
priyaṅgukācandanarūṣitānāṃ sparśāḥ priyāṇāṃ ca varāṅganānām
dāhe praśastāḥ sajalāḥ suśītāḥ padmotpalānāṃ ca kalāpavātāḥ
sariddhradānāṃ himavaddarīṇāṃ candrodayānāṃ kamalākarāṇām
mano'nukūlāḥ śiśirāśca sarvāḥ kathāḥ saraktaṃ śamayanti pittam
tatra ślokau
hetuṃ vṛddhiṃ saṃjñāṃ sthānaṃ liṅgaṃ pṛthak praduṣṭasya
mārgau sādhyamasādhyaṃ yāpyaṃ kāryakramaṃ caiva
pānānnamiṣṭameva ca varjyaṃ saṃśodhanaṃ ca śamanaṃ ca
gururuktavānyathāvaccikitsite raktapittasya
athāto gulmacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
sarvaprajānāṃ pitṛvaccharaṇyaḥ punarvasurbhūtabhaviṣyadīśaḥ
cikitsitaṃ gulmanibarhaṇārthaṃ provāca siddhaṃ vadatāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
viṭśleṣmapittātiparisravādvā taireva vṛddhaiḥ paripīḍanādvā
vegair udīrṇair vihatairadho vā bāhyābhighātairatipīḍanairvā
rūkṣānnapānairatisevitairvā śokena mithyāpratikarmaṇā vā
viceṣṭitairvā viṣamātimātraiḥ koṣṭhe prakopaṃ samupaiti vāyuḥ
kaphaṃ ca pittaṃ ca sa duṣṭavāyuruddhūya mārgān vinibadhya tābhyām
hṛnnābhipārśvodarabastiśūlaṃ karotyatho yāti na baddhamārgaḥ
pakvāśaye pittakaphāśaye vā sthitaḥ svatantraḥ parasaṃśrayo vā
sparśopalabhyaḥ paripiṇḍitatvādgulmo yathādoṣamupaiti nāma
bastau ca nābhyāṃ hṛdi pārśvayorvā sthānāni gulmasya bhavanti pañca
pañcātmakasya prabhavaṃ tu tasya vakṣyāmi liṅgāni cikitsitaṃ ca
rūkṣānnapānaṃ viṣamātimātraṃ viceṣṭitaṃ vegavinigrahaśca
śoko 'bhighāto 'timalakṣayaśca nirannatā cānilagulmahetuḥ
yaḥ sthānasaṃsthānarujāṃ vikalpaṃ viḍvātasaṅgaṃ galavaktraśoṣam
śyāvāruṇatvaṃ śiśirajvaraṃ ca hṛtkukṣipārśvāṃsaśirorujaṃ ca
karoti jīrṇe 'bhyadhikaṃ prakopaṃ bhukte mṛdutvaṃ samupaiti yaśca
vātāt sa gulmo na ca tatra rūkṣaṃ kaṣāyatiktaṃ kaṭu copaśete
kaṭvamlatīkṣṇoṣṇavidāhirūkṣakrodhātimadyārkahutāśasevā
āmābhighāto rudhiraṃ ca duṣṭaṃ paittasya gulmasya nimittamuktam
jvaraḥ pipāsā vadanāṅgarāgaḥ śūlaṃ mahajjīryati bhojane ca
svedo vidāho vraṇavacca gulmaḥ sparśāsahaḥ paittikagulmarūpam
śītaṃ guru snigdhamaceṣṭanaṃ ca saṃpūraṇaṃ prasvapanaṃ divā ca
gulmasya hetuḥ kaphasaṃbhavasya sarvastu diṣṭo nicayātmakasya
staimityaśītajvaragātrasādahṛllāsakāsārucigauravāṇi
śaityaṃ rugalpā kaṭhinonnatatvaṃ gulmasya rūpāṇi kaphātmakasya
nimittaliṅgānyupalabhya gulme dvidoṣaje doṣabalābalaṃ ca
vyāmiśraliṅgānaparāṃstu gulmāṃstrīnādiśedauṣadhakalpanārtham
mahārujaṃ dāhaparītamaśmavadghanonnataṃ śīghravidāhi dāruṇam
manaḥśarīrāgnibalāpahāriṇaṃ tridoṣajaṃ gulmamasādhyamādiśet
ṛtāvanāhāratayā bhayena virūkṣaṇairvegavinigrahaiśca
saṃstambhanollekhanayonidoṣairgulmaḥ striyaṃ raktabhavo 'bhyupaiti
yaḥ spandate piṇḍita eva nāṅgaiścirāt saśūlaḥ samagarbhaliṅgaḥ
sa raudhiraḥ strībhava eva gulmo māse vyatīte daśame cikitsyaḥ
kriyākramamataḥ siddhaṃ gulmināṃ gulmanāśanam
pravakṣyāmyata ūrdhvaṃ ca yogān gulmanibarhaṇān
rūkṣavyāyāmajaṃ gulmaṃ vātikaṃ tīvravedanam
baddhaviṇmārutaṃ snehairāditaḥ samupācaret
bhojanābhyañjanaiḥ pānairnirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ
snigdhasya bhiṣajā svedaḥ kartavyo gulmaśāntaye
srotasāṃ mārdavaṃ kṛtvā jitvā mārutamulbaṇam
bhittvā vibandhaṃ snigdhasya svedo gulmamapohati
snehapānaṃ hitaṃ gulme viśeṣeṇordhvanābhije
pakvāśayagate bastirubhayaṃ jaṭharāśraye
dīpte 'gnau vātike gulme vibandhe 'nilavarcasoḥ
bṛṃhaṇānyannapānāni snigdhoṣṇāni prayojayet
punaḥ punaḥ snehapānaṃ nirūhāḥ sānuvāsanāḥ
prayojyā vātagulmeṣu kaphapittānurakṣiṇā
kapho vāte jitaprāye pittaṃ śoṇitameva vā
yadi kupyati vā tasya kriyamāṇe cikitsite
yatholbaṇasya doṣasya tatra kāryaṃ bhiṣagjitam
ādāvante ca madhye ca mārutaṃ parirakṣatā
vātagulme kapho vṛddho hatvāgnimaruciṃ yadi
hṛllāsaṃ gauravaṃ tandrāṃ janayedullikhettu tam
śūlānāhavibandheṣu gulme vātakapholbaṇe
vartayo guṭikāścūrṇaṃ kaphavātaharaṃ hitam
pittaṃ vā yadi saṃvṛddhaṃ saṃtāpaṃ vātagulminaḥ
kuryādvirecyaḥ sa bhavet sasnehairānulomikaiḥ
gulmo yadyanilādīnāṃ kṛte samyagbhiṣagjite
na praśāmyati raktasya so 'vasekāt praśāmyati
snigdhoṣṇenodite gulme paittike sraṃsanaṃ hitam
rūkṣoṣṇena tu sambhūte sarpiḥ praśamanaṃ param
pittaṃ vā pittagulmaṃ vā jñātvā pakvāśayasthitam
kālavinnirharet sadyaḥ satiktaiḥ kṣīrabastibhiḥ
payasā vā sukhoṣṇena satiktena virecayet
bhiṣagagnibalāpekṣī sarpiṣā tailvakena vā
tṛṣṇājvaraparīdāhaśūlasvedāgnimārdave
gulmināmarucau cāpi raktamevāvasecayet
chinnamūlā vidahyante na gulmā yānti ca kṣayam
raktaṃ hi vyamlatāṃ yāti tacca nāsti na cāsti ruk
hṛtadoṣaṃ parimlānaṃ jāṅgalaistarpitaṃ rasaiḥ
samāśvastaṃ saśeṣārtiṃ sarpirabhyāsayet punaḥ
raktapittātivṛddhatvāt kriyām anupalabhya ca
yadi gulmo vidahyeta śastraṃ tatra bhiṣagjitam
guruḥ kaṭhinasaṃsthāno gūḍhamāṃsāntarāśrayaḥ
avivarṇaḥ sthiraścaiva hyapakvo gulma ucyate
dāhaśūlārtisaṃkṣobhasvapnanāśāratijvaraiḥ
vidahyamānaṃ jānīyādgulmaṃ tamupanāhayet
vidāhalakṣaṇe gulme bahistuṅge samunnate
śyāve saraktaparyante saṃsparśe bastisaṃnibhe
nipīḍitonnate stabdhe supte tatpārśvapīḍanāt
tatraiva piṇḍite śūle saṃpakvaṃ gulmamādiśet
tatra dhānvantarīyāṇām adhikāraḥ kriyāvidhau
vaidyānāṃ kṛtayogyānāṃ vyadhaśodhanaropaṇe
antarbhāgasya cāpyetat pacyamānasya lakṣaṇam
hṛtkroḍaśūnatāntaḥsthe pārśvanirgatiḥ
pakvaḥ srotāṃsi saṃkledya vrajatyūrdhvamadho 'pi vā
svayaṃpravṛttaṃ taṃ doṣamupekṣeta hitāśanaiḥ
daśāhaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā rakṣan bhiṣagupadravān
ata ūrdhvaṃ hitaṃ pānaṃ sarpiṣaḥ saviśodhanam
śuddhasya tiktaṃ sakṣaudraṃ prayoge sarpiriṣyate
śītalairgurubhiḥ snigdhairgulme jāte kaphātmake
avamyasyālpakāyāgneḥ kuryāllaṅghanamāditaḥ
mando 'gnirvedanā mandā gurustimitakoṣṭhatā
sotkleśā cāruciryasya sa gulmī vamanopagaḥ
uṣṇair evopacaryaśca kṛte vamanalaṅghane
yojyaścāhārasaṃsargo bheṣajaiḥ kaṭutiktakaiḥ
sānāhaṃ savibandhaṃ ca gulmaṃ kaṭhinamunnatam
dṛṣṭvādau svedayedyuktyā svinnaṃ ca vilayedbhiṣak
laṅghanollekhane svede kṛte 'gnau saṃpradhukṣite
kaphagulmī pibet kāle sakṣārakaṭukaṃ ghṛtam
sthānādapasṛtaṃ jñātvā kaphagulmaṃ virecanaiḥ
sasnehair bastibhir vāpi śodhayeddāśamūlikaiḥ
mande 'gnāvanile mūḍhe jñātvā sasnehamāśayam
guṭikācūrṇaniryūhāḥ prayojyāḥ kaphagulminām
kṛtamūlaṃ mahāvāstuṃ kaṭhinaṃ stimitaṃ gurum
jayetkaphakṛtaṃ gulmaṃ kṣārāriṣṭāgnikarmabhiḥ
doṣaprakṛtigulmartuyogaṃ buddhvā kapholbaṇe
baladoṣapramāṇajñaḥ kṣāraṃ gulme prayojayet
ekāntaraṃ dvyantaraṃ vā tryahaṃ viśramya vā punaḥ
śarīrabaladoṣāṇāṃ vṛddhikṣapaṇakovidaḥ
śleṣmāṇaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ māṃsakṣīraghṛtāśinaḥ
chittvā chittvāśayāt kṣāraḥ kṣaratvāt kṣārayatyadhaḥ
mande 'gnāvarucau sātmye madye sasnehamaśnatām
prayojyā mārgaśuddhyarthamariṣṭāḥ kaphagulminām
laṅghanollekhanaiḥ svedaiḥ sarpiḥpānairvirecanaiḥ
bastibhirguṭikācūrṇakṣārāriṣṭagaṇairapi
ślaiṣmikaḥ kṛtamūlatvādyasya gulmo na śāmyati
tasya dāho hṛto rakte śaralohādibhirhitaḥ
auṣṇyāttaikṣṇyācca śamayedagnirgulme kaphānilau
tayoḥ śamācca saṃghāto gulmasya vinirvartate
dāhe dhānvantarīyāṇāmatrāpi bhiṣajāṃ balam
kṣāraprayoge bhiṣajāṃ kṣāratantravidāṃ balam
vyāmiśradoṣe vyāmiśra eṣa eva kriyākramaḥ
siddhānataḥ pravakṣyāmi yogān gulmanibarhaṇān
tryūṣaṇatriphalādhānyaviḍaṅgacavyacitrakaiḥ
kalkīkṛtairghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ sakṣīraṃ vātagulmanut
iti tryūṣaṇādighṛtam
eta eva ca kalkāḥ syuḥ kaṣāyaḥ pañcamūlikaḥ
dvipañcamūliko vāpi tadghṛtaṃ gulmanut param
iti tryūṣaṇādighṛtamaparam
ṣaṭpalaṃ vā pibet sarpiryaduktaṃ rājayakṣmaṇi
prasannayā vā kṣīrārthaṃ surayā dāḍimena vā
dadhnaḥ sareṇa vā kāryaṃ ghṛtaṃ mārutagulmanut
hiṅgusauvarcalājājīviḍadāḍimadīpyakaiḥ
puṣkaravyoṣadhanyākavetasakṣāracitrakaiḥ
śaṭīvacājagandhailāsurasaiśca vipācitam
śūlānāhaharaṃ sarpirdadhnā cānilagulminām
iti hiṅgusauvarcalādyaṃ ghṛtam
hapuṣāvyoṣapṛthvīkācavyacitrakasaindhavaiḥ
sājājīpippalīmūladīpyakairvipacedghṛtam
sakolamūlakarasaṃ sakṣīradadhidāḍimam
tat paraṃ vātagulmaghnaṃ śūlānāhavimokṣaṇam
yonyarśograhaṇīdoṣaśvāsakāsārucijvarān
bastihṛtpārśvaśūlaṃ ca ghṛtametadvyapohati
iti hapuṣādyaṃ ghṛtam
pippalyā picuradhyardho dāḍimāddvipalaṃ palaṃ
dhānyātpañca ghṛtācchuṇṭhyāḥ karṣaḥ kṣīraṃ caturguṇam
siddhametairghṛtaṃ sadyo vātagulmaṃ vyapohati
yoniśūlaṃ śiraḥśūlamarśāṃsi viṣamajvaram
iti pippalyādyaṃ ghṛtam
ghṛtānāmauṣadhagaṇā ya ete parikīrtitāḥ
te cūrṇayogā vartyastāḥ kaṣāyāste ca gulminām
koladāḍimagharmāmbusurāmaṇḍāmlakāñjikaiḥ
śūlānāhaharī peyā bījapūrarasena vā
cūrṇāni mātuluṅgasya bhāvitāni rasena vā
kuryādvartīḥ saguṭikā gulmānāhārtiśāntaye
hiṅgu trikaṭukaṃ pāṭhāṃ hapuṣāmabhayāṃ śaṭīm
ajamodājagandhe ca tintiḍīkāmlavetasau
dāḍimaṃ puṣkaraṃ dhānyamajājīṃ citrakaṃ vacām
dvau kṣārau lavaṇe dve ca cavyaṃ caikatra cūrṇayet
cūrṇametat prayoktavyamannapāneṣvanatyayam
prāgbhaktamathavā peyaṃ madyenoṣṇodakena vā
pārśvahṛdbastiśūleṣu gulme vātakaphātmake
ānāhe mūtrakṛcchre ca śūle ca gudayonije
grahaṇyarśovikāreṣu plīhni pāṇḍvāmaye 'rucau
urovibandhe hikkāyāṃ kāse śvāse galagrahe
bhāvitaṃ mātuluṅgasya cūrṇametadrasena vā
bahuśo guṭikāḥ kāryāḥ kārmukāḥ syustato 'dhikam
iti hiṅgvādicūrṇaṃ guṭikā ca
mātuluṅgaraso hiṅgu dāḍimaṃ biḍasaindhave
surāmaṇḍena pātavyaṃ vātagulmarujāpaham
śaṭīpuṣkarahiṅgvamlavetasakṣāracitrakān
dhānyakaṃ ca yavānīṃ ca viḍaṅgaṃ saindhavaṃ vacām
sacavyapippalīmūlāmajagandhāṃ sadāḍimām
ajājīṃ cājamodāṃ ca cūrṇaṃ kṛtvā prayojayet
rasena mātuluṅgasya madhuśuktena vā punaḥ
bhāvitaṃ guṭikāṃ kṛtvā supiṣṭāṃ kolasaṃmitām
gulmaṃ plīhānamānāhaṃ śvāsaṃ kāsamarocakam
hikkāṃ hṛdrogamarśāṃsi vividhāṃ śiraso rujam
pāṇḍvāmayaṃ kaphotkleśaṃ sarvajāṃ ca pravāhikām
pārśvahṛdbastiśūlaṃ ca guṭikaiṣā vyapohati
nāgarārdhapalaṃ piṣṭvā dve pale luñcitasya ca
tilasyaikaṃ guḍapalaṃ kṣīreṇoṣṇena nā pibet
vātagulmamudāvartaṃ yoniśūlaṃ ca nāśayet
pibederaṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ vāruṇīmaṇḍamiśritam
tadeva tailaṃ payasā vātagulmī pibennaraḥ
śleṣmaṇyanubale pūrvaṃ hitaṃ pittānuge param
sādhayecchuddhaśuṣkasya laśunasya catuṣpalam
kṣīrodake 'ṣṭaguṇite kṣīraśeṣaṃ ca nā pibet
vātagulmamudāvartaṃ gṛdhrasīṃ viṣamajvaram
hṛdrogaṃ vidradhiṃ śothaṃ sādhayatyāśu tatpayaḥ
iti laśunakṣīram
tailaṃ prasannā gomūtramāranālaṃ yavāgrajam
gulmaṃ jaṭharamānāhaṃ pītamekatra sādhayet
iti tailapañcakam
pañcamūlīkaṣāyeṇa sakṣāreṇa śilājatu
pibettasya prayogeṇa vātagulmāt pramucyate
iti śilājatuprayogaḥ
vāṭyaṃ pippalīyūṣeṇa mūlakānāṃ rasena vā
bhuktvā snigdhamudāvartādvātagulmādvimucyate
śūlānāhavibandhārtaṃ svedayedvātagulminam
svedaiḥ svedavidhāvuktairnāḍīprastarasaṅkaraiḥ
bastikarma paraṃ vidyādgulmaghnaṃ taddhi mārutam
sve sthāne prathamaṃ jitvā sadyo gulmamapohati
tasmādabhīkṣṇaśo gulmā nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ
prayujyamānaiḥ śāmyanti vātapittakaphātmakāḥ
gulmaghnā vividhā diṣṭāḥ siddhāḥ siddhiṣu bastayaḥ
gulmaghnāni ca tailāni vakṣyante vātarogike
tāni mārutaje gulme pānābhyaṅgānuvāsanaiḥ
prayuktānyāśu sidhyanti tailaṃ hyanilajitparam
nīlinīcūrṇasaṃyuktaṃ pūrvoktaṃ ghṛtameva
samalāya pradātavyaṃ śodhanaṃ vātagulmine
nīlinītrivṛtādantīpathyākampillakaiḥ saha
śodhanārthaṃ ghṛtaṃ deyaṃ sabiḍakṣāranāgaram
nīlinīṃ triphalāṃ rāsnāṃ balāṃ kaṭukarohiṇīm
pacedviḍaṅgaṃ vyāghrīṃ ca palikāni jalāḍhake
tena pādāvaśeṣeṇa ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet
dadhnaḥ prasthena saṃyojya sudhākṣīrapalena ca
tato ghṛtapalaṃ dadyādyavāgūmaṇḍamiśritam
jīrṇe samyagviriktaṃ ca bhojayedrasabhojanam
gulmakuṣṭhodaravyaṅgaśophapāṇḍvāmayajvarān
śvitraṃ plīhānamunmādaṃ ghṛtametadvyapohati
iti nīlinyādyaṃ ghṛtam
kukkuṭāśca mayūrāśca tittirikrauñcavartakāḥ
śālayo madirā sarpirvātagulmabhiṣagjitam
hitamuṣṇaṃ dravaṃ snigdhaṃ bhojanaṃ vātagulminām
samaṇḍavāruṇīpānaṃ pakvaṃ vā dhānyakairjalam
mande 'gnau vardhate gulmo dīpte cāgnau praśāmyati
tasmānnā nātisauhityaṃ kuryānnātivilaṅghanam
sarvatra gulme prathamaṃ snehasvedopapādite
yā kriyā kriyate siddhiṃ sā yāti na virūkṣite
bhiṣagātyayikaṃ buddhvā pittagulmamupācaret
vairecanikasiddhena sarpiṣā tiktakena vā
rohiṇīkaṭukānimbamadhukatriphalātvacaḥ
karṣāṃśāstrāyamāṇā ca paṭolatrivṛtoḥ pale
dve pale ca masūrāṇāṃ sādhyamaṣṭaguṇe 'mbhasi
śṛtāccheṣaṃ ghṛtasamaṃ sarpiṣaśca catuṣpalam
pibet saṃmūrchitaṃ tena gulmaḥ śāmyati paittikaḥ
jvarastṛṣṇā ca śūlaṃ ca bhramo mūrcchārucistathā
iti rohiṇyādyaṃ ghṛtam
jale daśaguṇe sādhyaṃ trāyamāṇācatuṣpalam
pañcabhāgasthitaṃ pūtaṃ kalkaiḥ saṃyojya kārṣikaiḥ
rohiṇī kaṭukā mustā trāyamāṇā durālabhā
kalkaistāmalakīvīrājīvantīcandanotpalaiḥ
rasasyāmalakānāṃ ca kṣīrasya ca ghṛtasya ca
palāni pṛthagaṣṭāṣṭau dattvā samyagvipācayet
pittaraktabhavaṃ gulmaṃ vīsarpaṃ paittikaṃ jvaram
hṛdrogaṃ kāmalāṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanyādetadghṛtottamam
iti trāyamāṇādyaṃ ghṛtam
rasenāmalakekṣūṇāṃ ghṛtapādaṃ vipācayet
pathyāpādaṃ pibetsarpistatsiddhaṃ pittagulmanut
ityāmalakādyaṃ ghṛtam
drākṣāṃ madhūkaṃ kharjūraṃ vidārīṃ saśatāvarīm
parūṣakāṇi triphalāṃ sādhayetpalasaṃmitam
jalāḍhake pādaśeṣe rasamāmalakasya ca
ghṛtamikṣurasaṃ kṣīramabhayākalkapādikam
sādhayettadghṛtaṃ siddhaṃ śarkarākṣaudrapādikam
prayogāt pittagulmaghnaṃ sarvapittavikāranut
iti drākṣādyaṃ ghṛtam
vṛṣaṃ samūlamāpothya pacedaṣṭaguṇe jale
śeṣe 'ṣṭabhāge tasyaiva puṣpakalkaṃ pradāpayet
tena siddhaṃ ghṛtaṃ śītaṃ sakṣaudraṃ pittagulmanut
raktapittajvaraśvāsakāsahṛdroganāśanam
iti vāsāghṛtam
dvipalaṃ trāyamāṇāyā jaladviprasthasādhitam
aṣṭabhāgasthitaṃ pūtaṃ koṣṇaṃ kṣīrasamaṃ pibet
pibedupari tasyoṣṇaṃ kṣīrameva yathābalam
tena nirhṛtadoṣasya gulmaḥ śāmyati paittikaḥ
drākṣābhayārasaṃ gulme paittike saguḍaṃ pibet
lihyātkampillakaṃ vāpi virekārthaṃ madhudravam
dāhapraśamano 'bhyaṅgaḥ sarpiṣā pittagulminām
candanādyena tailena tailena madhukasya vā
ye ca pittajvaraharāḥ satiktāḥ kṣīrabastayaḥ
hitāste pittagulmibhyo vakṣyante ye ca siddhiṣu
śālayo jāṅgalaṃ māṃsaṃ gavyāje payasī ghṛtam
kharjūrāmalakaṃ drākṣāṃ dāḍimaṃ saparūṣakam
āhārārthaṃ prayoktavyaṃ pānārthaṃ salilaṃ śṛtam
balāvidārīgandhādyaiḥ pittagulmacikitsitam
āmānvaye pittagulme sāme vā kaphavātike
yavāgūbhiḥ khaḍairyūṣaiḥ saṃdhukṣyo 'gnirvilaṅghite
śamaprakopau doṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāmagnisaṃśritau
tasmādagniṃ sadā rakṣennidānāni ca varjayet
vamanaṃ vamanārhāya pradadyāt kaphagulmine
snigdhasvinnaśarīrāya gulme śaithilyamāgate
pariveṣṭya pradīptāṃstu balvajānathavā kuśān
bhiṣakkumbhe samāvāpya gulmaṃ ghaṭamukhe nyaset
saṃgṛhīto yadā gulmastadā ghaṭamathoddharet
vastrāntaraṃ tataḥ kṛtvā bhindyādgulmaṃ pramāṇavit
vimārgājapadādarśair yathālābhaṃ prapīḍayet
mṛdnīyād gulmamevaikaṃ na tvantrahṛdayaṃ spṛśet
tilairaṇḍātasībījasarṣapaiḥ parilipya ca
śleṣmagulmamayaḥpātraiḥ sukhoṣṇaiḥ svedayedbhiṣak
savyoṣakṣāralavaṇaṃ daśamūlīśṛtaṃ ghṛtam
kaphagulmaṃ jayatyāśu sahiṅgubiḍadāḍimam
iti daśamūlīghṛtam
bhallātakānāṃ dvipalaṃ pañcamūlaṃ palonmitam
sādhyaṃ vidārīgandhādyamāpothya salilāḍhake
pādaśeṣe rase tasmin pippalīṃ nāgaraṃ vacām
viḍaṅgaṃ saindhavaṃ hiṅgu yāvaśūkaṃ biḍaṃ śaṭīm
citrakaṃ madhukaṃ rāsnāṃ piṣṭvā karṣasamaṃ bhiṣak
prasthaṃ ca payaso dattvā ghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet
etadbhallātakaghṛtaṃ kaphagulmaharaṃ param
plīhapāṇḍvāmayaśvāsagrahaṇīrogakāsanut
iti bhallātakādyaṃ ghṛtam
pippalīpippalīmūlacavyacitrakanāgaraiḥ
palikaiḥ sayavakṣārairghṛtaprasthaṃ vipācayet
kṣīraprasthaṃ ca tat sarpir hanti gulmaṃ kaphātmakam
grahaṇīpāṇḍurogaghnaṃ plīhakāsajvarāpaham
iti kṣīraṣaṭpalakaṃ ghṛtam
trivṛtāṃ triphalāṃ dantīṃ daśamūlaṃ palonmitam
jale caturguṇe paktvā caturbhāgasthitaṃ rasam
sarpireraṇḍajaṃ tailaṃ kṣīraṃ caikatra sādhayet
sa siddho miśrakasnehaḥ sakṣaudraḥ kaphagulmanut
kaphavātavibandheṣu kuṣṭhaplīhodareṣu ca
prayojyo miśrakaḥ sneho yoniśūleṣu cādhikam
iti miśrakaḥ snehaḥ
yaduktaṃ vātagulmaghnaṃ sraṃsanaṃ nīlinīghṛtam
dviguṇaṃ tadvirekārthaṃ prayojyaṃ kaphagulminām
sudhākṣīradrave cūrṇaṃ trivṛtāyāḥ subhāvitam
kārṣikaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ līḍhvā sādhu virecyate
jaladroṇe vipaktavyā viṃśatiḥ pañca cābhayāḥ
dantyāḥ palāni tāvanti citrakasya tathaiva ca
aṣṭabhāgāvaśeṣaṃ tu rasaṃ pūtamadhikṣipet
dantīsamaṃ guḍaṃ pūtaṃ kṣipettatrābhayāśca tāḥ
tailārdhakuḍavaṃ caiva trivṛtāyāścatuṣpalam
cūrṇitaṃ palamekaṃ tu pippalīviśvabheṣajam
tat sādhyaṃ lehavacchīte tasmiṃstailasamaṃ madhu
kṣipeccūrṇapalaṃ caikaṃ tvagelāpatrakeśarāt
tato lehapalaṃ līḍhvā jagdhvā caikāṃ harītakīm
sukhaṃ viricyate snigdho doṣaprasthamanāmayam
gulmaṃ śvayathumarśāṃsi pāṇḍurogamarocakam
hṛdrogaṃ grahaṇīdoṣaṃ kāmalāṃ viṣamajvaram
kuṣṭhaṃ plīhānamānāhameṣā hantyupasevitā
niratyayaḥ kramaścāsyā dravo māṃsarasaudanaḥ
iti dantīharītakī
siddhāḥ siddhiṣu vakṣyante nirūhāḥ kaphagulminām
ariṣṭayogāḥ siddhāśca grahaṇyarśaścikitsite
yaccūrṇaṃ guṭikā yāśca vihitā vātagulminām
dviguṇakṣārahiṅgvamlavetasāstāḥ kaphe hitāḥ
ya eva grahaṇīdoṣe kṣārāste kaphagulminām
siddhā niratyayāḥ śastā dāhastvante praśasyate
prapurāṇāni dhānyāni jāṅgalā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
kaulattho mudgayūṣaśca pippalyā nāgarasya ca
śuṣkamūlakayūṣaśca bilvasya varuṇasya ca
cirabilvāṅkurāṇāṃ ca yavānyāścitrakasya ca
bījapūrakahiṅgvamlavetasakṣāradāḍimaiḥ
takreṇa tailasarpirbhyāṃ vyañjanānyupakalpayet
pañcamūlīśṛtaṃ toyaṃ purāṇaṃ vāruṇīrasam
kaphagulmī pibetkāle jīrṇaṃ mādhvīkameva vā
yavānīcūrṇitaṃ takraṃ biḍena lavaṇīkṛtam
pibet saṃdīpanaṃ vātakaphamūtrānulomanam
saṃcitaḥ kramaśo gulmo mahāvāstuparigrahaḥ
kṛtamūlaḥ sirānaddho yadā kūrma ivonnataḥ
daurbalyārucihṛllāsakāsavamyaratijvaraiḥ
tṛṣṇātandrāpratiśyāyairyujyate na sa sidhyati
gṛhītvā sajvaraśvāsaṃ vamyatīsārapīḍitam
hṛnnābhihastapādeṣu śophaḥ karṣati gulminam
raudhirasya tu gulmasya garbhakālavyatikrame
snigdhasvinnaśarīrāyai dadyāt snehavirecanam
palāśakṣārapātre dve dve pātre tailasarpiṣoḥ
gulmaśaithilyajananīṃ paktvā mātrāṃ prayojayet
prabhidyeta na yadyevaṃ dadyādyoniviśodhanam
kṣāreṇa yuktaṃ palalaṃ sudhākṣīreṇa vā punaḥ
ābhyāṃ vā bhāvitān dadyādyonau kaṭukamatsyakān
varāhamatsyapittābhyāṃ laktakān vā subhāvitān
adhoharaiścordhvaharairbhāvitān vā samākṣikaiḥ
kiṇvaṃ vā saguḍakṣāraṃ dadyādyoniviśodhanam
raktapittaharaṃ kṣāraṃ lehayenmadhusarpiṣā
laśunaṃ madirāṃ tīkṣṇāṃ matsyāṃścāsyai pradāpayet
bastiṃ sakṣīragomūtraṃ sakṣāraṃ dāśamūlikam
adṛśyamāne rudhire dadyādgulmaprabhedanam
pravartamāne rudhire dadyānmāṃsarasaudanam
ghṛtatailena cābhyaṅgaṃ pānārthaṃ taruṇīṃ surām
rudhire 'tipravṛtte tu raktapittaharīḥ kriyāḥ
