kāryā vātarugārtāyāḥ sarvā vātaharīḥ punaḥ
ghṛtatailāvasekāṃśca tittirīṃścaraṇāyudhān
surāṃ samaṇḍāṃ pūrvaṃ ca pānamamlasya sarpiṣaḥ
prayojayeduttaraṃ vā jīvanīyena sarpiṣā
atipravṛtte rudhire satiktenānuvāsanam
tatra ślokāḥ
snehaḥ svedaḥ sarpirbastiścūrṇāni bṛṃhaṇaṃ guḍikāḥ
vamanavirekau mokṣaḥ kṣatajasya ca vātagulmavatām
sarpiḥ satiktasiddhaṃ kṣīraṃ prasraṃsanaṃ nirūhāśca
raktasya cāvasecanam āśvāsanasaṃśamanayogāḥ
upanāhanaṃ saśastraṃ pakvasyābhyantaraprabhinnasya
saṃśodhanasaṃśamane pittaprabhavasya gulmasya
snehaḥ svedo bhedo laṅghanamullekhanaṃ virekaśca
sarpirbastirguṭikāścūrṇamariṣṭāśca sakṣārāḥ
gulmasyānte dāhaḥ kaphajasyāgre 'panītaraktasya
gulmasya raudhirasya kriyākramaḥ strībhavasyoktaḥ
pathyānnapānasevā hetūnāṃ varjanaṃ yathāsvaṃ ca
nityaṃ cāgnisamādhiḥ snigdhasya ca sarvakarmāṇi
heturliṅgaṃ siddhiḥ kriyākramaḥ sādhyatā na yogāśca
gulmacikitsitasaṃgraha etāvān vyāhṛto 'gniveśasya
athātastṛṣṇācikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
jñānapraśamatapobhiḥ khyāto'trisuto jagaddhite'bhirataḥ
tṛṣṇānāṃ praśamārthaṃ cikitsitaṃ prāha pañcānām
kṣobhādbhayācchramād api śokāt krodhād vilaṅghanānmadyāt
kṣārāmlalavaṇakaṭukoṣṇarūkṣaśuṣkānnasevābhiḥ
dhātukṣayagadakarṣaṇavamanādyatiyogasūryasaṃtāpaiḥ
pittānilau pravṛddhau saumyān dhātūṃś ca śoṣayataḥ
rasavāhinīśca nāḍīr jihvāmūlagalatālukaklomnaḥ
saṃśoṣya nṛṇāṃ dehe kurutastṛṣṇāṃ mahābalāvetau
pītaṃ pītaṃ hi jalaṃ śoṣayatastāvato na yāti śamam
ghoravyādhikṛśānāṃ prabhavatyupasargabhūtā sā
prāgrūpaṃ mukhaśoṣaḥ svalakṣaṇaṃ sarvadāmbukāmitvam
tṛṣṇānāṃ sarvāsāṃ liṅgānāṃ lāghavamapāyaḥ
mukhaśoṣasvarabhedabhramasaṃtāpapralāpasaṃstambhān
tālvoṣṭhakaṇṭhajihvākarkaśatāṃ cittanāśaṃ ca
jihvānirgamamaruciṃ bādhiryaṃ marmadūyanaṃ sādam
tṛṣṇodbhūtā kurute pañcavidhāṃ liṅgataḥ śṛṇu tām
abdhātuṃ dehasthaṃ kupitaḥ pavano yadā viśoṣayati
tasmiñśuṣke śuṣyatyabalastṛṣyatyatha viśuṣyan
nidrānāśaḥ śiraso bhramastathā śuṣkavirasamukhatā ca sroto'varodha iti ca syālliṅgaṃ vātatṛṣṇāyāḥ
pittaṃ matamāgneyaṃ kupitaṃ cet tāpayaty apāṃ dhātum
saṃtaptaḥ sa hi janayettṛṣṇāṃ dāholbaṇāṃ nṛṇām
tiktāsyatvaṃ śiraso dāhaḥ śītābhinandatā mūrchā
pītākṣimūtravarcastvam ākṛtiḥ pittatṛṣṇāyāḥ
tṛṣṇā yāmaprabhavā sāpyāgneyāmapittajanitatvāt
liṅgaṃ tasyāś cārucir ādhmānakaphaprasekau ca
deho rasajo'mbubhavo rasaśca tasya kṣayācca tṛṣyeddhi
dīnasvaraḥ pratāmyan saṃśuṣkahṛdayagalatāluḥ
bhavati khalu yopasargāttṛṣṇā sā śoṣiṇī kaṣṭā
jvaramehakṣayaśoṣaśvāsādyupasṛṣṭadehānām
sarvāstvatiprasaktā rogakṛśānāṃ vamiprasaktānām
ghoropadravayuktās tṛṣṇā maraṇāya vijñeyāḥ
iti mūlaviṣaviśeṣāḥ proktāḥ śṛṇu jaṅgamasyātaḥ
saviśeṣacikitsitamevādau tatrocyate tu sarpāṇām
iha darvīkaraḥ sarpo maṇḍalī rājimāniti
trayo yathākramaṃ vātapittaśleṣmaprakopaṇāḥ
darvīkaraḥ phaṇī jñeyo maṇḍalī maṇḍalāphaṇaḥ
bindulekhavicitrāṅgaḥ pannagaḥ syāttu rājimān
viśeṣādrūkṣakaṭukamamloṣṇaṃ svādu śītalam
viṣaṃ yathākramaṃ teṣāṃ tasmādvātādikopanam
darvīkarakṛto daṃśaḥ sūkṣmadaṃṣṭrāpado 'sitaḥ
niruddharaktaḥ kūrmābho vātavyādhikaro mataḥ
pṛthvarpitaḥ saśothaśca daṃśo maṇḍalinā kṛtaḥ
pītābhaḥ pītaraktaśca sarvapittavikārakṛt
kṛto rājimatā daṃśaḥ picchilaḥ sthiraśophakṛt
snigdhaḥ pāṇḍuśca sāndrāsṛk śleṣmavyādhisamīraṇaḥ
vṛttabhogo mahākāyaḥ śvasannūrdhvekṣaṇaḥ pumān
sthūlamūrdhā samāṅgaśca strī tvataḥ syādviparyayāt
klībastrasatyadhodṛṣṭiḥ svarahīnaḥ prakampate
striyā daṣṭo viparyastairetaiḥ puṃsā naro mataḥ
vyāmiśraliṅgairetaistu klībadaṣṭaṃ naraṃ vadet
ityetaduktaṃ sarpāṇāṃ strīpuṃklībanidarśanam
pāṇḍuvaktrastu garbhiṇyā śūnauṣṭho 'pyasitekṣaṇaḥ
jṛmbhākrodhopajihvārtaḥ sūtayā raktamūtravān
sarpo gaudherako nāma godhāyāṃ syāccatuṣpadaḥ
kṛṣṇasarpeṇa tulyaḥ syānnānā syurmiśrajātayaḥ
gūḍhasampāditaṃ vṛttaṃ pīḍitaṃ lambitārpitam
sarpitaṃ ca bhṛśābādhaṃ daṃśā ye 'nye na te bhṛśāḥ
taruṇāḥ kṛṣṇasarpāstu gonasāḥ sthavirāstathā
rājimanto vayomadhye bhavantyāśīviṣopamāḥ
sarpadaṃṣṭrāścatasrastu tāsāṃ vāmādharā sitā
pītā vāmottarā daṃṣṭrā raktaśyāvādharottarā
yanmātraḥ patate bindur govālāt saliloddhṛtāt
vāmādharāyāṃ daṃṣṭrāyāṃ tanmātraṃ syādaherviṣam
ekadvitricaturvṛddhaviṣabhāgottarottarāḥ
savarṇāstatkṛtā daṃśā bahūttaraviṣā bhṛśāḥ
sarpāṇām eva viṇmūtrāt kīṭāḥ syuḥ kīṭasaṃmatāḥ
dūṣīviṣāḥ prāṇaharā iti saṃkṣepato matāḥ
śmaśānacaityavalmīkayajñāśramasurālaye
pakṣasandhiṣu madhyāhne sārdharātre 'ṣṭamīṣu ca
na sidhyanti narā daṣṭāḥ pāṣaṇḍāyataneṣu ca
dṛṣṭiśvāsamalasparśaviṣairāśīviṣais tathā
vinaśyantyāśu samprāptā daṣṭāḥ sarveṣu marmasu
yena kenāpi sarpeṇa saṃbhavaḥ sarva eva ca
bhavanti cātra
iti sarvavikārāṇāmuktametaccikitsitam
sthānametaddhi tantrasya rahasyaṃ paramuttamam
asmin saptadaśādhyāyāḥ kalpāḥ siddhaya eva ca
nāsādyante 'gniveśasya tantre carakasaṃskṛte
tānetān kāpilabaliḥ śeṣān dṛḍhabalo 'karot
tantrasyāsya mahārthasya pūraṇārthaṃ yathātatham
rogā ye 'pyatra noddiṣṭā bahutvānnāmarūpataḥ
teṣāmapyetadeva syāddoṣādīn vīkṣya bheṣajam
siddhiṃ cānuttamāṃ loke prāpnoti vidhinā paṭhan
vistārayati leśoktaṃ saṃkṣipatyativistaram
saṃskartā kurute tantraṃ purāṇaṃ ca punarnavam
atastantrottamamidaṃ carakeṇātibuddhinā
saṃskṛtaṃ tattvasampūrṇaṃ tribhāgenopalakṣyate
tacchaṅkaraṃ bhūtapatiṃ saṃprasādya samāpayat
akhaṇḍārthaṃ dṛḍhabalo jātaḥ pañcanade pure
kṛtvā bahubhyastantrebhyo viśeṣoñchaśiloccayam
saptadaśauṣadhādhyāyasiddhikalpairapūrayat
idamanyūnaśabdārthaṃ tantradoṣavivarjitam
ṣaḍviṃśatā vicitrābhirbhūṣitaṃ tantrayuktibhiḥ
tatrādhikaraṇaṃ yogo hetvartho 'rthaḥ padasya ca
pradeśoddeśanirdeśavākyaśeṣāḥ prayojanam
upadeśāpadeśātideśārthāpattinirṇayāḥ
prasaṅgaikāntanaikāntāḥ sāpavargo viparyayaḥ
pūrvapakṣavidhānānumatavyākhyānasaṃśayāḥ
atītānāgatāvekṣāsvasaṃjñohyasamuccayāḥ
nidarśanaṃ nirvacanaṃ saṃniyogo vikalpanam
pratyutsāras tathoddhāraḥ saṃbhavastantrayuktayaḥ
tantre samāsavyāsokte bhavantyetā hi kṛtsnaśaḥ
ekadeśena dṛśyante samāsābhihite tathā
yathāmbujavanasyārkaḥ pradīpo veśmano yathā
prabodhanaprakāśārthastathā tantrasya yuktayaḥ
ekasminnapi yasyeha śāstre labdhāspadā matiḥ
sa śāstramanyadapyāśu yuktijñatvāt prabudhyate
adhīyāno 'pi śāstrāṇi tantrayuktyā vinā bhiṣak
nādhigacchati śāstrārthānarthān bhāgyakṣaye yathā
durgṛhītaṃ kṣiṇotyeva śāstraṃ śastramivābudham
sugṛhītaṃ tadeva jñaṃ śāstraṃ śastraṃ ca rakṣati
tasmādetāḥ pravakṣyante vistareṇottare punaḥ
tattvajñānārthamasyaiva tantrasya guṇadoṣataḥ
idamakhilamadhītya samyagarthān vimṛśati yo 'vimanāḥ prayoganityaḥ
sa manujasukhajīvitapradātā bhavati dhṛtismṛtibuddhidharmavṛddhaḥ
yasya dvādaśasāhasrī hṛdi tiṣṭhati saṃhitā
so 'rthajñaḥ sa vicārajñaścikitsākuśalaśca saḥ
rogāṃsteṣāṃ cikitsāṃ ca sa kimarthaṃ na budhyate
cikitsā vahniveśasya susthāturahitaṃ prati
yadihāsti tadanyatra yannehāsti na tatkvacit
agniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte
siddhisthāne 'ṣṭame prāpte tasmin dṛḍhabalena tu
siddhisthānaṃ svasiddhyarthaṃ samāsena samāpitam
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte 'prāpte dṛḍhabalasampūrite siddhisthāne uttarabastisiddhirnāma dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
athātaḥ karapracitīyaṃ rasāyanapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
karapracitānāṃ yathoktaguṇānām āmalakānāmuddhṛtāsthnāṃ śuṣkacūrṇitānāṃ punarmāghe phālgune vā māse triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ svarasaparipītānāṃ punaḥ śuṣkacūrṇīkṛtānām āḍhakam ekaṃ grāhayet atha jīvanīyānāṃ bṛṃhaṇīyānāṃ stanyajananānāṃ śukrajananānāṃ vayaḥsthāpanānāṃ ṣaḍvirecanaśatāśritīyoktānām auṣadhagaṇānāṃ candanāgurudhavatiniśakhadiraśiṃśapāsanasārāṇāṃ cāṇuśaḥ kṛttānām abhayāvibhītakapippalīvacācavyacitrakaviḍaṅgānāṃ ca samastānāmāḍhakamekaṃ daśaguṇenāmbhasā sādhayet tasminnāḍhakāvaśeṣe rase supūte tāny āmalakacūrṇāni dattvā gomayāgnibhir vaṃśavidalaśaratejanāgnibhir vā sādhayed yāvad apanayādrasasya tam anupadagdham upahṛtyāyasīṣu pātrīṣvāstīrya śoṣayet suśuṣkaṃ tat kṛṣṇājinasyopari dṛṣadi ślakṣṇapiṣṭam ayaḥsthālyāṃ nidhāpayet samyak taccūrṇam ayaś cūrṇāṣṭabhāgasamprayuktaṃ madhusarpirbhyām agnibalam abhisamīkṣya prayojayediti
etadrasāyanaṃ pūrvaṃ vasiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapo 'ṅgirāḥ
jamadagnirbharadvājo bhṛguranye ca tadvidhāḥ
prayujya prayatā muktāḥ śramavyādhijarābhayāt
yāvad aicchaṃs tapastepus tatprabhāvān mahābalāḥ
idaṃ rasāyanaṃ cakre brahmā vārṣasahasrikam
jarāvyādhipraśamanaṃ buddhīndriyabalapradam
tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yānena praśamena ca
rasāyanavidhānena kālayuktena cāyuṣā
sthitā maharṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ nahi kiṃcid rasāyanam
grāmyānāmanyakāryāṇāṃ sidhyatyaprayatātmanām
saṃvatsaraṃ payovṛttirgavāṃ madhye vaset sadā
sāvitrīṃ manasā dhyāyan brahmacārī yatendriyaḥ
saṃvatsarānte pauṣīṃ vā māghīṃ vā phālgunīṃ tithim
tryahoṣavāsī śuklasya praviśyāmalakīvanam
bṛhatphalāḍhyam āruhya drumaṃ śākhāgataṃ phalam
gṛhītvā pāṇinā tiṣṭhejjapan brahmāmṛtāgamāt
tadā hy avaśyamamṛtaṃ vasatyāmalake kṣaṇam
śarkarāmadhukalpāni snehavanti mṛdūni ca
bhavantyamṛtasaṃyogāttāni yāvanti bhakṣayet
jīved varṣasahasrāṇi tāvantyāgatayauvanaḥ
sauhityameṣāṃ gatvā tu bhavatyamarasaṃnibhaḥ
svayaṃ cāsyopatiṣṭhante śrīr vedā vākca rūpiṇī
triphalāyā rase mūtre gavāṃ kṣāre ca lāvaṇe
krameṇa ceṅgudīkṣāre kiṃśukakṣāra eva ca
tīkṣṇāyasasya pattrāṇi vahnivarṇāni sādhayet
caturaṅguladīrghāṇi tilotsedhatanūni ca
jñātvā tānyañjanābhāni sūkṣmacūrṇāni kārayet
tāni cūrṇāni madhunā rasenāmalakasya ca
yuktāni lehavatkumbhe sthitāni ghṛtabhāvite
saṃvatsaraṃ nidheyāni yavapalle tathaiva ca
dadyādāloḍanaṃ māse sarvatrāloḍayan budhaḥ
saṃvatsarātyaye tasya prayogo madhusarpiṣā
prātaḥ prātarbalāpekṣī sātmyaṃ jīrṇe ca bhojanam
eṣa eva ca lauhānāṃ prayogaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ
nābhighātairna cātaṅkairjarayā na ca mṛtyunā
sa dhṛṣyaḥ syādgajaprāṇaḥ sadā cātibalendriyaḥ
dhīmān yaśasvī vāksiddhaḥ śrutadhārī mahādhanaḥ
bhavetsamāṃ prayuñjāno naro lauharasāyanam
anenaiva vidhānena hemnaśca rajatasya ca
āyuḥprakarṣakṛtsiddhaḥ prayogaḥ sarvaroganut
aindrī matsyākhyako brāhmī vacā brahmasuvarcalā
pippalyo lavaṇaṃ hema śaṅkhapuṣpī viṣaṃ ghṛtam
eṣāṃ triyavakān bhāgān hemasarpirviṣair vinā
dvau yavau tatra hemnastu tilaṃ dadyādviṣasya ca
sarpiṣaśca palaṃ dadyāttadaikadhyaṃ prayojayet
ghṛtaprabhūtaṃ sakṣaudraṃ jīrṇe cānnaṃ praśasyate
jarāvyādhipraśamanaṃ smṛtimedhākaraṃ param
āyuṣyaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ dhanyaṃ svaravarṇaprasādanam
paramojaskaraṃ caitatsiddhamaindraṃ rasāyanam
nainat prasahate kṛtyā nālakṣmīrna viṣaṃ na ruk
śvitraṃ sakuṣṭhaṃ jaṭharāṇi gulmāḥ plīhā purāṇo viṣamajvaraśca
medhāsmṛtijñānaharāśca rogāḥ śāmyantyanenātibalāśca vātāḥ
maṇḍūkaparṇyāḥ svarasaḥ prayojyaḥ kṣīreṇa yaṣṭīmadhukasya cūrṇam
raso guḍūcyāstu samūlapuṣpyāḥ kalkaḥ prayojyaḥ khalu śaṅkhapuṣpyāḥ
āyuḥpradānyāmayanāśanāni balāgnivarṇasvaravardhanāni
medhyāni caitāni rasāyanāni medhyā viśeṣeṇa ca śaṅkhapuṣpī
pañcāṣṭau sapta daśa vā pippalīrmadhusarpiṣā
rasāyanaguṇānveṣī samāmekāṃ prayojayet
tisrastisrastu pūrvāhṇaṃ bhuktvāgre bhojanasya ca
pippalyaḥ kiṃśukakṣārabhāvitā ghṛtabharjitāḥ
prayojyā madhurasammiśrā rasāyanaguṇaiṣiṇā
jetuṃ kāsaṃ kṣayaṃ śoṣaṃ śvāsaṃ hikkāṃ galāmayān
arśāṃsi grahaṇīdoṣaṃ pāṇḍutāṃ viṣamajvaram
vaisvaryaṃ pīnasaṃ śophaṃ gulmaṃ vātabalāsakam
kramavṛddhyā daśāhāni daśapaippalikaṃ dinam
vardhayet payasā sārdhaṃ tathaivāpanayet punaḥ
jīrṇe jīrṇe ca bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā
pippalīnāṃ sahasrasya prayogo'yaṃ rasāyanam
piṣṭās tā balibhiḥ sevyāḥ śṛtā madhyabalair naraiḥ
cūrṇīkṛtā hrasvabalair yojyā doṣāmayān prati
daśapaippalikaḥ śreṣṭho madhyamaḥ ṣaṭ prakīrtitaḥ
prayogo yas triparyantaḥ sa kanīyān sa cābalaiḥ
bṛṃhaṇaṃ svaryam āyuṣyaṃ plīhodaravināśanam
vayasaḥ sthāpanaṃ medhyaṃ pippalīnāṃ rasāyanam
jaraṇānte 'bhayām ekāṃ prāgbhuktād dve vibhītake
bhuktvā tu madhusarpirbhyāṃ catvāryāmalakāni ca
prayojayan samām ekāṃ triphalāyā rasāyanam
jīved varṣaśataṃ pūrṇam ajaro 'vyādhireva ca
traiphalenāyasīṃ pātrīṃ kalkenālepayen navām
tam ahorātrikaṃ lepaṃ pibet kṣaudrodakāplutam
prabhūtasneham aśanaṃ jīrṇe tatra praśasyate
ajaro 'ruk samābhyāsāj jīvec caiva samāḥ śatam
madhukena tugākṣīryā pippalyā kṣaudrasarpiṣā
triphalā sitayā cāpi yuktā siddhaṃ rasāyanam
sarvalauhaiḥ suvarṇena vacayā madhusarpiṣā
viḍaṅgapippalībhyāṃ ca triphalā lavaṇena ca
saṃvatsaraprayogeṇa medhāsmṛtibalapradā
bhavatyāyuḥpradā dhanyā jarāroganibarhaṇī
anamlaṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ ca kaṭu pāke śilājatu
nātyuṣṇaśītaṃ dhātubhyaścaturbhyastasya sambhavaḥ
hemnaśca rajatāttāmrādvarāt kṛṣṇāyasādapi
rasāyanaṃ tadvidhibhistad vṛṣyaṃ tacca roganut
vātapittakaphaghnaiśca niryūhais tat subhāvitam
vīryotkarṣaṃ paraṃ yāti sarvairekaikaśo 'pi vā
prakṣiptoddhṛtam apy enat punas tat prakṣiped rase
koṣṇe saptāhametena vidhinā tasya bhāvanā
pūrvoktena vidhānena lohaiścūrṇīkṛtaiḥ saha
tatpītaṃ payasā dadyād dīrghamāyuḥ sukhānvitam
jarāvyādhipraśamanaṃ dehadārḍhyakaraṃ param
medhāsmṛtikaraṃ dhanyaṃ kṣīrāśī tatprayojayet
prayogaḥ saptasaptāhās trayaś caikaśca saptakaḥ
nirdiṣṭas trividhastasya paro madhyo'varastathā
palamardhapalaṃ karṣo mātrā tasya tridhā matā
jāterviśeṣaṃ savidhiṃ tasya vakṣyāmyataḥ param
hemādyāḥ sūryasaṃtaptāḥ sravanti giridhātavaḥ
jatvābhaṃ mṛdu mṛtsnācchaṃ yanmalaṃ tacchilājatu
madhuraśca satiktaśca japāpuṣpanibhaśca yaḥ
kaṭurvipāke śītaśca sa suvarṇasya nisravaḥ
rūpyasya kaṭukaḥ śvetaḥ śītaḥ svādu vipacyate
tāmrasya barhikaṇṭhābhastiktoṣṇaḥ pacyate kaṭu
yastu guggulukābhāsastiktako lavaṇānvitaḥ
kaṭurvipāke śītaśca sarvaśreṣṭhaḥ sa cāyasaḥ
gomūtragandhayaḥ sarve sarvakarmasu yaugikāḥ
rasāyanaprayogeṣu paścimastu viśiṣyate
yathākramaṃ vātapitte śleṣmapitte kaphe triṣu
viśeṣataḥ praśasyante malā hemādidhātujāḥ
śilājatuprayogeṣu vidāhīni gurūṇi ca
varjayet sarvakālaṃ tu kulatthānparivarjayet
te hy atyantaviruddhatvād aśmano bhedanāḥ param
loke dṛṣṭāstatasteṣāṃ prayogaḥ pratiṣidhyate
payāṃsi takrāṇi rasāḥ sayūṣās toyaṃ samūtrā vividhāḥ kaṣāyāḥ
āloḍanārthaṃ girijasya śastās te te prayojyāḥ prasamīkṣya kāryam
na so 'sti rogo bhuvi sādhyarūpaḥ śilāhvayaṃ yaṃ na jayet prasahya
tat kālayogairvidhibhiḥ prayuktaṃ svasthasya corjāṃ vipulāṃ dadāti
karapracitike pāde daśa ṣaṭ ca maharṣiṇā
rasāyanānāṃ siddhānāṃ saṃyogāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne rasāyanādhyāye karapracitīyo nāma rasāyanapādastṛtīyaḥ
athāta āyurvedasamutthānīyaṃ rasāyanapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
ṛṣayaḥ khalu kadācicchālīnā yāyāvarāśca grāmyauṣadhyāhārāḥ santaḥ sāmpannikā mandaceṣṭā nātikalyāśca prāyeṇa babhūvuḥ
te sarvāsām itikartavyatānām asamarthāḥ santo grāmyavāsakṛtamātmadoṣaṃ matvā pūrvanivāsam apagatagrāmyadoṣaṃ śivaṃ puṇyam udāraṃ medhyam agamyam asukṛtibhir gaṅgāprabhavam amaragandharvakiṃnarānucaritam anekaratnanicayamacintyādbhutaprabhāvaṃ brahmarṣisiddhacāraṇānucaritaṃ divyatīrthauṣadhiprabhavam atiśaraṇyaṃ himavantam amarādhipatiguptaṃ jagmur bhṛgvaṅgiro'trivasiṣṭhakaśyapāgastyapulastyavāmadevāsitagautamaprabhṛtayo maharṣayaḥ
tān indraḥ sahasradṛg amaragurur abravītsvāgataṃ brahmavidāṃ jñānatapodhanānāṃ brahmarṣīṇām
asti nanu vo glānir aprabhāvatvaṃ vaisvaryaṃ vaivarṇyaṃ ca grāmyavāsakṛtam asukham asukhānubandhaṃ ca grāmyo hi vāso mūlam aśastānāṃ tat kṛtaḥ puṇyakṛdbhir anugrahaḥ prajānāṃ svaśarīramavekṣituṃ kālaḥ kālaścāyamāyurvedopadeśasya brahmarṣīṇām ātmanaḥ prajānāṃ cānugrahārtham āyurvedamaśvinau mahyaṃ prāyacchatāṃ prajāpatiraśvibhyāṃ prajāpataye brahmā prajānām alpam āyur jarāvyādhibahulam asukham asukhānubandham alpatvād alpatapodamaniyamadānādhyayanasaṃcayaṃ matvā puṇyatamam āyuḥprakarṣakaraṃ jarāvyādhipraśamanam ūrjaskaram amṛtaṃ śivaṃ śaraṇyamudāraṃ bhavanto mattaḥ śrotumarhatāthopadhārayituṃ prakāśayituṃ ca prajānugrahārthamārṣaṃ brahma ca prati maitrīṃ kāruṇyam ātmanaś cānuttamaṃ puṇyamudāraṃ brāhmamakṣayaṃ karmeti
tacchrutvā vibudhapativacanam ṛṣayaḥ sarva evāmaravaram ṛgbhis tuṣṭuvuḥ prahṛṣṭāśca tadvacanamabhinananduśceti
athendras tadāyurvedāmṛtam ṛṣibhyaḥ saṃkramyovāca etatsarvamanuṣṭheyam ayaṃ ca śivaḥ kālo rasāyanānāṃ divyāścauṣadhayo himavatprabhavāḥ prāptavīryāḥ tadyathā aindrī brāhmī payasyā kṣīrapuṣpī śrāvaṇī mahāśrāvaṇī śatāvarī vidārī jīvantī punarnavā nāgabalā sthirā vacā chattrā aticchatrā medā mahāmedā jīvanīyāścānyāḥ payasā prayuktāḥ ṣaṇmāsāt paramāyurvayaśca taruṇamanāmayatvaṃ svaravarṇasampadam upacayaṃ medhāṃ smṛtimuttamabalam iṣṭāṃścāparān bhāvān āvahanti siddhāḥ
brahmasuvarcalā nāmauṣadhir yā hiraṇyakṣīrā puṣkarasadṛśapattrā ādityaparṇī nāmauṣadhiryā sūryakāntā iti vijñāyate suvarṇakṣīrā sūryamaṇḍalākārapuṣpā ca nārīnāmauṣadhiḥ aśvabalā iti vijñāyate yā bilvajasadṛśapattrā kāṣṭhagodhā nāmauṣadhir godhākārā sarpānāmauṣadhiḥ sarpākārā somo nāmauṣadhirājaḥ pañcadaśaparvā sa soma iva hīyate vardhate ca padmā nāmauṣadhiḥ padmākārā padmaraktā padmagandhā ca ajānām auṣadhiḥ ajaśṛṅgī iti vijñāyate nīlā nāmauṣadhistu nīlakṣīrā nīlapuṣpā latāpratānabahuleti āsāmoṣadhīnāṃ yāṃ yāmevopalabheta tasyās tasyāḥ svarasasya sauhityaṃ gatvā snehabhāvitāyām ārdrapalāśadroṇyāṃ sapidhānāyāṃ digvāsāḥ śayīta tatra pralīyate ṣaṇmāsena punaḥ sambhavati tasyājaṃ payaḥ pratyavasthāpanaṃ ṣaṇmāsena devatānukārī bhavati vayovarṇasvarākṛtibalaprabhābhiḥ svayaṃ cāsya sarvavācogatāni prādurbhavanti divyaṃ cāsya cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ ca bhavati gatir yojanasahasraṃ daśavarṣasahasrāṇy āyur anupadravaṃ ceti
divyānāmoṣadhīnāṃ yaḥ prabhāvaḥ sa bhavadvidhaiḥ
śakyaḥ soḍhumaśakyastu syātsoḍhumakṛtātmabhiḥ
oṣadhīnāṃ prabhāveṇa tiṣṭhatāṃ sve ca karmaṇi
bhavatāṃ nikhilaṃ śreyaḥ sarvamevopapatsyate
vānaprasthairgṛhasthaiśca prayatairniyatātmabhiḥ
śakyā oṣadhayo hy etāḥ sevituṃ viṣayābhijāḥ
yāstu kṣetraguṇaisteṣāṃ madhyamena ca karmaṇā
mṛduvīryatarās tāsāṃ vidhirjñeyaḥ sa eva tu
paryeṣṭuṃ tāḥ prayoktuṃ vā ye 'samarthāḥ sukhārthinaḥ
rasāyanavidhisteṣāmayamanyaḥ praśasyate
balyānāṃ jīvanīyānāṃ bṛṃhaṇīyāś ca yā daśa
vayasaḥ sthāpanānāṃ ca khadirasyāsanasya ca
kharjūrāṇāṃ madhūkānāṃ mustānāmutpalasya ca
mṛdvīkānāṃ viḍaṅgānāṃ vacāyāścitrakasya ca
śatāvaryāḥ payasyāyāḥ pippalyā joṅgakasya ca
ṛddhyā nāgabalāyāśca dvāradāyā dhavasya ca
triphalākaṇṭakāryoś ca vidāryāścandanasya ca
ikṣūṇāṃ śaramūlānāṃ śrīparṇyāstiniśasya ca
rasāḥ pṛthak pṛthag grāhyāḥ palāśakṣāra eva ca
eṣāṃ palonmitān bhāgān payo gavyaṃ caturguṇam
dve pātre tilatailasya dve ca gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ
tat sādhyaṃ sarvam ekatra susiddhaṃ snehamuddharet
tatrāmalakacūrṇānāmāḍhakaṃ śatabhāvitam
svarasenaiva dātavyaṃ kṣaudrasyābhinavasya ca
śarkarācūrṇapātraṃ ca prasthamekaṃ pradāpayet
tugākṣīryāḥ sapippalyāḥ sthāpyaṃ saṃmūrchitaṃ ca tat
sucaukṣe mārttike kumbhe māsārdhaṃ ghṛtabhāvite
mātrāmagnisamāṃ tasya tata ūrdhvaṃ prayojayet
hematāmrapravālānām ayasaḥ sphaṭikasya ca
muktāvaiḍūryaśaṅkhānāṃ cūrṇānāṃ rajatasya ca
prakṣipya ṣoḍaśīṃ mātrāṃ vihāyāyāsamaithunam
jīrṇe jīrṇe ca bhuñjīta ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā
sarvarogapraśamanaṃ vṛṣyamāyuṣyam uttamam
sattvasmṛtiśarīrāgnibuddhīndriyabalapradam
paramūrjaskaraṃ caiva varṇasvarakaraṃ tathā
viṣālakṣmīpraśamanaṃ sarvavācogatapradam
siddhārthatāṃ cābhinavaṃ vayaśca prajāpriyatvaṃ ca yaśaśca loke
prayojyam icchadbhiridaṃ yathāvad rasāyanaṃ brāhmamudāravīryam
samarthānāmarogāṇāṃ dhīmatāṃ niyatātmanām
kuṭīpraveśaḥ kṣaṇināṃ paricchadavatāṃ hitaḥ
ato'nyathā tu ye teṣāṃ sauryamārutiko vidhiḥ
tayoḥ śreṣṭhataraḥ pūrvo vidhiḥ sa tu suduṣkaraḥ
rasāyanavidhibhraṃśājjāyeran vyādhayo yadi
yathāsvamauṣadhaṃ teṣāṃ kāryaṃ muktvā rasāyanam
satyavādinamakrodhaṃ nivṛttaṃ madyamaithunāt
ahiṃsakamanāyāsaṃ praśāntaṃ priyavādinam
japaśaucaparaṃ dhīraṃ dānanityaṃ tapasvinam
devagobrāhmaṇācāryaguruvṛddhārcane ratam
ānṛśaṃsyaparaṃ nityaṃ nityaṃ karuṇavedinam
samajāgaraṇasvapnaṃ nityaṃ kṣīraghṛtāśinam
deśakālapramāṇajñaṃ yuktijñam anahaṃkṛtam
śastācāram asaṃkīrṇam adhyātmapravaṇendriyam
upāsitāraṃ vṛddhānāmāstikānāṃ jitātmanām
dharmaśāstraparaṃ vidyānnaraṃ nityarasāyanam
guṇair etaiḥ samuditaiḥ prayuṅkte yo rasāyanam
rasāyanaguṇān sarvān yathoktān sa samaśnute
yathāsthūlam anirvāhya doṣāñchārīramānasān
rasāyanaguṇair jantur yujyate na kadācana
yogā hy āyuḥprakarṣārthā jarāroganibarhaṇāḥ
manaḥśarīraśuddhānāṃ sidhyanti prayatātmanām
tadetanna bhavedvācyaṃ sarvameva hatātmasu
arujebhyo 'dvijātibhyaḥ śuśrūṣā yeṣu nāsti ca
ye rasāyanasaṃyogā vṛṣyayogāśca ye matāḥ
yaccauṣadhaṃ vikārāṇāṃ sarvaṃ tadvaidyasaṃśrayam
prāṇācāryaṃ budhastasmāddhīmantaṃ vedapāragam
aśvināv iva devendraḥ pūjayed atiśaktitaḥ
aśvinau devabhiṣajau yajñavāhāv iti smṛtau
yajñasya hi śiraśchinnaṃ punastābhyāṃ samāhitam
praśīrṇā daśanāḥ pūṣṇo netre naṣṭe bhagasya ca
vajriṇaśca bhujastambhastābhyāmeva cikitsitaḥ
cikitsitaśca śītāṃśurgṛhīto rājayakṣmaṇā
somābhipatitaścandraḥ kṛtastābhyāṃ punaḥ sukhī
bhārgavaścyavanaḥ kāmī vṛddhaḥ san vikṛtiṃ gataḥ
vītavarṇasvaropetaḥ kṛtastābhyāṃ punaryuvā
etaiścānyaiśca bahubhiḥ karmabhir bhiṣaguttamau
babhūvaturbhṛśaṃ pūjyāv indrādīnāṃ mahātmanām
grahāḥ stotrāṇi mantrāṇi tathā nānāhavīṃṣi ca
dhūmrāśca paśavastābhyāṃ prakalpyante dvijātibhiḥ
prātaśca savane somaṃ śakro 'śvibhyāṃ sahāśnute
sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca bhagavānaśvibhyāṃ saha modate
indrāgnī cāśvinau caiva stūyante prāyaśo dvijaiḥ
stūyante vedavākyeṣu na tathānyā hi devatāḥ
ajarairamaraistāvadvibudhaiḥ sādhipair dhruvaiḥ
ete prayatairevamaśvinau bhiṣajāv iti
mṛtyuvyādhijarāvaśyair duḥkhaprāyaiḥ sukhārthibhiḥ
kiṃ punarbhiṣajo martyaiḥ pūjyāḥ syur nātiśaktitaḥ
śīlavānmatimān yukto dvijātiḥ śāstrapāragaḥ
prāṇibhirguruvatpūjyaḥ prāṇācāryaḥ sa hi smṛtaḥ
vidyāsamāptau bhiṣajo dvitīyā jātirucyate
aśnute vaidyaśabdaṃ hi na vaidyaḥ pūrvajanmanā
vidyāsamāptau brāhmaṃ vā sattvamārṣamathāpi vā
dhruvam āviśati jñānāt tasmād vaidyo dvijaḥ smṛtaḥ
nābhidhyāyenna cākrośed ahitaṃ na samācaret
prāṇācāryaṃ budhaḥ kaścid icchann āyur anitvaram
cikitsitastu saṃśrutya yo vāsaṃśrutya mānavaḥ
nopākaroti vaidyāya nāsti tasyeha niṣkṛtiḥ
bhiṣagapyāturān sarvān svasutāniva yatnavān
ābādhebhyo hi saṃrakṣed icchan dharmam anuttamam
dharmārthaṃ cārthakāmārthamāyurvedo maharṣibhiḥ
prakāśito dharmaparair icchadbhiḥ sthānamakṣaram
nārthārthaṃ nāpi kāmārthamatha bhūtadayāṃ prati
vartate yaścikitsāyāṃ sa sarvam ativartate
kurvate ye tu vṛttyarthaṃ cikitsāpaṇyavikrayam
te hitvā kāñcanaṃ rāśiṃ pāṃśurāśimupāsate
dāruṇaiḥ kṛṣyamāṇānāṃ gadair vaivasvatakṣayam
chittvā vaivasvatān pāśān jīvitaṃ yaḥ prayacchati
dharmārthadātā sadṛśastasya nehopalabhyate
na hi jīvitadānāddhi dānam anyad viśiṣyate
paro bhūtadayā dharma iti matvā cikitsayā
vartate yaḥ sa siddhārthaḥ sukham atyantam aśnute
āyurvedasamutthānaṃ divyauṣadhividhiṃ śubham
amṛtālpāntaraguṇaṃ siddhaṃ ratnarasāyanam
siddhebhyo brahmacāribhyo yaduvācāmareśvaraḥ
āyurvedasamutthāne tat sarvaṃ saṃprakāśitam
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsitasthāne rasāyanādhyāye āyurvedasamutthānīyo nāma rasāyanapādaścaturthaḥ
athātaḥ saṃyogaśaramūlīyaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
vājīkaraṇam anvicchet puruṣo nityamātmavān
tadāyattau hi dharmārthau prītiśca yaśa eva ca
putrasyāyatanaṃ hy etadguṇāścaite sutāśrayāḥ
vājīkaraṇam agryaṃ ca kṣetraṃ strī yā praharṣiṇī
iṣṭā hy ekaikaśo 'py arthāḥ paraṃ prītikarāḥ smṛtāḥ
kiṃ punaḥ strīśarīre ye saṃghātena pratiṣṭhitāḥ
saṃghāto hīndriyārthānāṃ strīṣu nānyatra vidyate
stryāśrayo hīndriyārtho yaḥ sa prītijanano'dhikam
strīṣu prītirviśeṣeṇa strīṣv apatyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
dharmārthau strīṣu lakṣmīśca strīṣu lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
surūpā yauvanasthā yā lakṣaṇairyā vibhūṣitā
yā vaśyā śikṣitā yā ca sā strī vṛṣyatamā matā
nānābhaktyā tu lokasya daivayogācca yoṣitām
taṃ taṃ prāpya vivardhante naraṃ rūpādayo guṇāḥ
vayorūpavacohāvair yā yasya paramāṅganā
praviśatyāśu hṛdayaṃ daivād vā karmaṇo 'pi vā
hṛdayotsavarūpā yā yā samānamanaḥśayā
samānasattvā yā vaśyā yā yasya prīyate priyaiḥ
yā pāśabhūtā sarveṣām indriyāṇāṃ parairguṇaiḥ
yayā viyukto nistrīkam aratir manyate jagat
yasyā ṛte śarīraṃ nā dhatte śūnyam ivendriyaiḥ
śokodvegāratibhayair yāṃ dṛṣṭvā nābhibhūyate
yāti yāṃ prāpya visrambhaṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyatyatīva yām
apūrvāmiva yāṃ yāti nityaṃ harṣātivegataḥ
gatvā gatvāpi bahuśo yāṃ tṛptiṃ naiva gacchati
sā strī vṛṣyatamā tasya nānābhāvā hi mānavāḥ
atulyagotrāṃ vṛṣyāṃ ca prahṛṣṭāṃ nirupadravām
śuddhasnātāṃ vrajennārīmapatyārthī nirāmayaḥ
acchāyaś caikaśākhaś ca niṣphalaśca yathā drumaḥ
aniṣṭagandhaścaikaśca nirapatyastathā naraḥ
citradīpaḥ saraḥ śuṣkam adhātur dhātusaṃnibhaḥ
niṣprajas tṛṇapūlīti mantavyaḥ puruṣākṛtiḥ
apratiṣṭhaśca nagnaśca śūnyaścaikendriyaśca nā
mantavyo niṣkriyaścaiva yasyāpatyaṃ na vidyate
bahumūrtir bahumukho bahuvyūho bahukriyaḥ
bahucakṣur bahujñāno bahvātmā ca bahuprajaḥ
maṅgalyo'yaṃ praśasyo'yaṃ dhanyo'yaṃ vīryavān ayam
bahuśākho'yamiti ca stūyate nā bahuprajaḥ
prītirbalaṃ sukhaṃ vṛttir vistāro vipulaṃ kulam
yaśo lokāḥ sukhodarkāstuṣṭiś cāpatyasaṃśritāḥ
tasmādapatyamanvicchan guṇāṃścāpatyasaṃśritān
vājīkaraṇanityaḥ syādicchan kāmasukhāni ca
upabhogasukhān siddhān vīryāpatyavivardhanān
vājīkaraṇasaṃyogān pravakṣyāmyata uttaram
śaramūlekṣumūlāni kāṇḍekṣuḥ sekṣubālikā
śatāvarī payasyā ca vidārī kaṇṭakārikā
jīvantī jīvako medā vīrā carṣabhako balā
ṛddhir gokṣurakaṃ rāsnā sātmaguptā punarnavā
eṣāṃ tripalikān bhāgān māṣāṇām āḍhakaṃ navam
vipācayejjaladroṇe caturbhāgaṃ ca śeṣayet
tatra peṣyāṇi madhukaṃ drākṣā phalgūni pippalī
ātmaguptā madhūkāni kharjūrāṇi śatāvarī
vidāryāmalakekṣūṇāṃ rasasya ca pṛthak pṛthak
sarpiṣaś cāḍhakaṃ dadyāt kṣīradroṇaṃ ca tadbhiṣak
sādhayedghṛtaśeṣaṃ ca supūtaṃ yojayet punaḥ
śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāś cūrṇaiḥ prasthonmitaiḥ pṛthak
palaiś caturbhir māgadhyāḥ palena maricasya ca
tvagelākesarāṇāṃ ca cūrṇair ardhapalonmitaiḥ
madhunaḥ kuḍavābhyāṃ ca dvābhyāṃ tatkārayedbhiṣak
palikā gulikāstyānāstā yathāgni prayojayet
eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ yogo bṛṃhaṇo balavardhanaḥ
anenāśva ivodīrṇo balī liṅgaṃ samarpayet
māṣāṇāmātmaguptāyā bījānāmāḍhakaṃ navam
jīvakarṣabhakau vīrāṃ medām ṛddhiṃ śatāvarīm
madhukaṃ cāśvagandhāṃ ca sādhayet kuḍavonmitām
rase tasmin ghṛtaprasthaṃ gavyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ payaḥ
vidārīṇāṃ rasaprasthaṃ prasthamikṣurasasya ca
dattvā mṛdvagninā sādhyaṃ siddhaṃ sarpirnidhāpayet
śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasya ca pṛthak pṛthak
bhāgāṃścatuṣpalāṃs tatra pippalyāścāvapet palam
palaṃ pūrvamato līḍhvā tato'nnam upayojayet
ya icchedakṣayaṃ śukraṃ śephasaś cottamaṃ balam
śarkarā māṣavidalāstugākṣīrī payo ghṛtam
godhūmacūrṇaṣaṣṭhāni sarpiṣy utkārikāṃ pacet
tāṃ nātipakvāṃ mṛditāṃ kaukkuṭe madhure rase
sugandhe prakṣiped uṣṇe yathā sāndrībhaved rasaḥ
eṣa piṇḍaraso vṛṣyaḥ pauṣṭiko balavardhanaḥ
anenāśva ivodīrṇo balī liṅgaṃ samarpayet
śikhitittirihaṃsānāmevaṃ piṇḍaraso mataḥ
balavarṇasvarakaraḥ pumāṃstena vṛṣāyate
ghṛtaṃ māṣān sabastāṇḍān sādhayenmāhiṣe rase
bharjayettaṃ rasaṃ pūtaṃ phalāmlaṃ navasarpiṣi
īṣat salavaṇaṃ yuktaṃ dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ
eṣa vṛṣyaśca balyaśca bṛṃhaṇaśca rasottamaḥ
caṭakāṃstittirirase tittirīn kaukkuṭe rase
kukkuṭān bārhiṇarase hāṃse bārhiṇameva ca
navasarpiṣi saṃtaptān phalāmlān kārayed rasān
madhurānvā yathāsātmyaṃ gandhāḍhyān balavardhanān
tṛptiṃ caṭakamāṃsānāṃ gatvā yo 'nupibet payaḥ
na tasya liṅgaśaithilyaṃ syānna śukrakṣayo niśi
māṣasūpeṇa yo bhuktvā ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam
payaḥ pibati rātriṃ sa kṛtsnāṃ jāgarti vegavān
na nā svapiti rātriṣu nityastabdhena śephasā
tṛptaḥ kukkuṭamāṃsānāṃ bhṛṣṭānāṃ nakraretasi
niḥsrāvya matsyāṇḍarasaṃ bhṛṣṭaṃ sarpiṣi bhakṣayet
haṃsabarhiṇadakṣāṇām evamaṇḍāni bhakṣayet
srotaḥsu śuddheṣvamale śarīre vṛṣyaṃ yadā nā mitamatti kāle
vṛṣāyate tena paraṃ manuṣyas tadbṛṃhaṇaṃ caiva balapradaṃ ca
tasmāt purā śodhanameva kāryaṃ balānurūpaṃ na hi vṛṣyayogāḥ
sidhyanti dehe maline prayuktāḥ kliṣṭe yathā vāsasi rāgayogāḥ
vājīkaraṇasāmarthyaṃ kṣetraṃ strī yasya caiva yā
ye doṣā nirapatyānāṃ guṇāḥ putravatāṃ ca ye
daśa pañca ca saṃyogā vīryāpatyavivardhanāḥ
uktāste śaramūlīye pāde puṣṭibalapradāḥ
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye saṃyogaśaramūlīyo nāma vājīkaraṇapādaḥ prathamaḥ
athāta āsiktakṣīrikaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
āsiktakṣīram āpūrṇam aśuṣkaṃ śuddhaṣaṣṭikam
udūkhale samāpothya pīḍayet kṣīramarditam
gṛhītvā taṃ rasaṃ pūtaṃ gavyena payasā saha
bījānāmātmaguptāyā dhānyamāṣarasena ca
balāyāḥ śūrpaparṇyāśca jīvantyā jīvakasya ca
ṛddhyarṣabhakakākolīśvadaṃṣṭrāmadhukasya ca
śatāvaryā vidāryāśca drākṣākharjūrayor api
saṃyuktaṃ mātrayā vaidyaḥ sādhayettatra cāvapet
tugākṣīryāḥ samāṣāṇāṃ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikasya ca
godhūmānāṃ ca cūrṇāni yaiḥ sa sāndrībhavedrasaḥ
sāndrībhūtaṃ ca kuryāt prabhūtamadhuśarkaram
guṭikā badaraistulyāstāś ca sarpiṣi bharjayet
tā yathāgni prayuñjānaḥ kṣīramāṃsarasāśanaḥ
paśyatyapatyaṃ vipulaṃ vṛddho 'pyātmajamakṣayam
caṭakānāṃ sahaṃsānāṃ dakṣāṇāṃ śikhināṃ tathā
śiśumārasya nakrasya bhiṣakśukrāṇi saṃharet
gavyaṃ sarpir varāhasya kuliṅgasya vasāmapi
ṣaṣṭikānāṃ ca cūrṇāni cūrṇaṃ godhūmakasya ca
ebhiḥ pūpalikāḥ kāryāḥ śaṣkulyo vartikāstathā
pūpā dhānāś ca vividhā bhakṣyāścānye pṛthagvidhāḥ
eṣāṃ prayogādbhakṣyāṇāṃ stabdhenāpūrṇaretasā
śephasā vājivadyāti yāvadicchaṃ striyo naraḥ
ātmaguptāphalaṃ māṣān kharjūrāṇi śatāvarīm
śṛṅgāṭakāni mṛdvīkāṃ sādhayetprasṛtonmitam
kṣīraprasthaṃ jalaprasthametat prasthāvaśeṣitam
śuddhena vāsasā pūtaṃ yojayet prasṛtais tribhiḥ
śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ sarpiṣo 'bhinavasya ca
tat pāyayet sakṣaudraṃ ṣaṣṭikānnaṃ ca bhojayet
jarāparīto'pyabalo yogenānena vindati
naro'patyaṃ suvipulaṃ yuveva ca sa hṛṣyati
kharjūrīmastakaṃ māṣān payasyāṃ ca śatāvarīm
kharjūrāṇi madhūkāni mṛdvīkāmajaḍāphalam
palonmitāni matimān sādhayet salilāḍhake
tena pādāvaśeṣeṇa kṣīraprasthaṃ vipācayet
kṣīraśeṣeṇa tenādyād ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam
saśarkareṇa saṃyoga eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ smṛtaḥ
jīvakarṣabhakau medāṃ jīvantīṃ śrāvaṇīdvayam
kharjūraṃ madhukaṃ drākṣāṃ pippalīṃ viśvabheṣajam
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ vidārīṃ ca navaṃ sarpiḥ payo jalam
siddhaṃ ghṛtāvaśeṣaṃ taccharkarākṣaudrapādikam
ṣaṣṭikānnena saṃyuktamupayojyaṃ yathābalam
vṛṣyaṃ balyaṃ ca varṇyaṃ ca kaṇṭhyaṃ bṛṃhaṇam uttamam
dadhnaḥ saraṃ śaraccandrasaṃnibhaṃ doṣavarjitam
śarkarākṣaudramaricais tugākṣīryā ca buddhimān
yuktyā yuktaṃ sasūkṣmailaṃ nave kumbhe śucau paṭe
mārjitaṃ prakṣipecchīte ghṛtāḍhye ṣaṣṭikaudane
pibenmātrāṃ rasālāyāstaṃ bhuktvā ṣaṣṭikaudanam
varṇasvarabalopetaḥ pumāṃstena vṛṣāyate
candrāṃśukalpaṃ payasā ghṛtāḍhyaṃ ṣaṣṭikaudanam
śarkarāmadhusaṃyuktaṃ prayuñjāno vṛṣāyate
tapte sarpiṣi nakrāṇḍaṃ tāmracūḍāṇḍamiśritam
yuktaṃ ṣaṣṭikacūrṇena sarpiṣābhinavena ca
paktvā pūpalikāḥ khādedvāruṇīmaṇḍapo naraḥ
ya icchedaśvavad gantuṃ prasektuṃ gajavac ca yaḥ
etaiḥ prayogairvidhivadvapuṣmān vīryopapanno balavarṇayuktaḥ
harṣānvito vājivad aṣṭavarṣo bhavet samarthaśca varāṅganāsu
yadyacca kiṃcin manasaḥ priyaṃ syādramyā vanāntāḥ pulināni śailāḥ
iṣṭāḥ striyo bhūṣaṇagandhamālyaṃ priyā vayasyāśca tadatra yogyam
āsiktakṣīrike pāde ye yogāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
aṣṭāv apatyakāmaiste prayojyāḥ pauruṣārthibhiḥ
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye āsiktakṣīriko nāma vājīkaraṇapādo dvitīyaḥ
athāto māṣaparṇabhṛtīyaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
māṣaparṇabhṛtāṃ dhenuṃ gṛṣṭiṃ puṣṭāṃ catuḥstanīm
samānavarṇavatsāṃ ca jīvadvatsāṃ ca buddhimān
rohiṇīmathavā kṛṣṇām ūrdhvaśṛṅgīm adāruṇām
ikṣvādām arjunādāṃ vā sāndrakṣīrāṃ ca dhārayet
kevalaṃ tu payastasyāḥ śṛtaṃ vāśṛtameva vā
śarkarākṣaudrasarpirbhiryuktaṃ tadvṛṣyamuttamam
śukralair jīvanīyaiśca bṛṃhaṇair balavardhanaiḥ
kṣīrasaṃjananaiścaiva payaḥ siddhaṃ pṛthak pṛthak
yuktaṃ godhūmacūrṇena saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram
paryāyeṇa prayoktavyamicchatā śukramakṣayam
medāṃ payasyāṃ jīvantīṃ vidārīṃ kaṇṭakārikām
śvadaṃṣṭrāṃ kṣīrikāṃ māṣān godhūmāñchāliṣaṣṭikān
payasyardhodake paktvā kārṣikān āḍhakonmite
vivarjayet payaḥśeṣaṃ tatpūtaṃ kṣaudrasarpiṣā
yuktaṃ saśarkaraṃ pītvā vṛddhaḥ saptatiko 'pi vā
vipulaṃ labhate'patyaṃ yuveva ca sa hṛṣyati
maṇḍalairjātarūpasya tasyā eva payaḥ śṛtam
apatyajananaṃ siddhaṃ saghṛtakṣaudraśarkaram
triṃśat supiṣṭāḥ pippalyaḥ prakuñce tailasarpiṣoḥ
bhṛṣṭāḥ saśarkarakṣaudrāḥ kṣīradhārāvadohitāḥ
pītvā yathābalaṃ cordhvaṃ ṣaṣṭikaṃ kṣīrasarpiṣā
bhuktvā na rātrim astabdhaṃ liṅgaṃ paśyati nā kṣarat
śvadaṃṣṭrāyā vidāryāśca rase kṣīracaturguṇe
ghṛtāḍhyaḥ sādhito vṛṣyo māṣaṣaṣṭikapāyasaḥ
phalānāṃ jīvanīyānāṃ snigdhānāṃ rucikāriṇām
kuḍavaścūrṇitānāṃ syāt svayaṃguptāphalasya ca
kuḍavaścaiva māṣāṇāṃ dvau dvau ca tilamudgayoḥ
godhūmaśālicūrṇānāṃ kuḍavaḥ kuḍavo bhavet
sarpiṣaḥ kuḍavaścaikastat sarvaṃ kṣīramarditam
paktvā pūpalikāḥ khāded bahvyaḥ syur yasya yoṣitaḥ
ghṛtaṃ śatāvarīgarbhaṃ kṣīre daśaguṇe pacet
śarkarāpippalīkṣaudrayuktaṃ tadvṛṣyamuttamam
karṣaṃ madhukacūrṇasya ghṛtakṣaudrasamāṃśikam
prayuṅkte yaḥ payaścānu nityavegaḥ sa nā bhavet
ghṛtakṣīrāśano nirbhīr nirvyādhir nityago yuvā
saṃkalpapravaṇo nityaṃ naraḥ strīṣu vṛṣāyate
kṛtaikakṛtyāḥ siddhārthā ye cānyonyānuvartinaḥ
kalāsu kuśalāstulyāḥ sattvena vayasā ca ye
kulamāhātmyadākṣiṇyaśīlaśaucasamanvitāḥ
ye kāmanityā ye hṛṣṭā ye viśokā gatavyathāḥ
ye tulyaśīlā ye bhaktā ye priyā ye priyaṃvadāḥ
tair naraḥ saha visrabdhaḥ suvayasyair vṛṣāyate
abhyaṅgotsādanasnānagandhamālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ
gṛhaśayyāsanasukhair vāsobhirahataiḥ priyaiḥ
vihaṃgānāṃ rutairiṣṭaiḥ strīṇāṃ cābharaṇasvanaiḥ
saṃvāhanair varastrīṇām iṣṭānāṃ ca vṛṣāyate
mattadvirephācaritāḥ sapadmāḥ salilāśayāḥ
jātyutpalasugandhīni śītagarbhagṛhāṇi ca
nadyaḥ phenottarīyāśca girayo nīlasānavaḥ
unnatir nīlameghānāṃ ramyacandrodayā niśāḥ
vāyavaḥ sukhasaṃsparśāḥ kumudākaragandhinaḥ
ratibhogakṣamā rātryaḥ saṃkocāguruvallabhāḥ
sukhāḥ sahāyāḥ parapuṣṭaghuṣṭāḥ phullā vanāntā viśadānnapānāḥ
gāndharvaśabdāśca sugandhayogāḥ sattvaṃ viśālaṃ nirupadravaṃ ca
siddhārthatā cābhinavaśca kāmaḥ strī cāyudhaṃ sarvamihātmajasya
vayo navaṃ jātamadaśca kālo harṣasya yoniḥ paramā narāṇām
praharṣayonayo yogā vyākhyātā daśa pañca ca
māṣaparṇabhṛtīye'smin pāde śukrabalapradāḥ
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye māṣaparṇabhṛtīyo nāma vājīkaraṇapādastṛtīyaḥ
athātaḥ pumāñjātabalādikaṃ vājīkaraṇapādaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
iti ha smāha bhagavānātreyaḥ
pumān yathā jātabalo yāvadicchaṃ striyo vrajet
yathā cāpatyavān sadyo bhavet tad upadekṣyate
na hi jātabalāḥ sarve narāś cāpatyabhāginaḥ
bṛhaccharīrā balinaḥ santi nārīṣu durbalāḥ
santi cālpāśrayāḥ strīṣu balavanto bahuprajāḥ
prakṛtyā cābalāḥ santi santi cāmayadurbalāḥ
narāścaṭakavat kecid vrajanti bahuśaḥ striyam
gajavacca prasiñcanti kecin na bahugāminaḥ
kālayogabalāḥ kecit kecidabhyasanadhruvāḥ
kecitprayatnairvyajyante vṛṣāḥ kecit svabhāvataḥ
tasmāt prayogānvakṣyāmo durbalānāṃ balapradān
sukhopabhogān balināṃ bhūyaśca balavardhanān
pūrvaṃ śuddhaśarīrāṇāṃ nirūhaiḥ sānuvāsanaiḥ
balāpekṣī prayuñjīta śukrāpatyavivardhanān
ghṛtatailarasakṣīraśarkarāmadhusaṃyutāḥ
vastayaḥ saṃvidhātavyāḥ kṣīramāṃsarasāśinām
piṣṭvā varāhamāṃsāni dattvā maricasaindhave
kolavadgulikāḥ kṛtvā tapte sarpiṣi vartayet
vartanastambhitāstāśca prakṣepyāḥ kaukkuṭe rase
ghṛtāḍhye gandhapiśune dadhidāḍimasārike
yathā na bhindyād gulikās tathā taṃ sādhayed rasam
taṃ piban bhakṣayaṃs tāśca labhate śukramakṣayam
māṃsānām evam anyeṣāṃ medyānāṃ kārayedbhiṣak
guṭikāḥ sarasās tāsāṃ prayogaḥ śukravardhanaḥ
māṣānaṅkuritāñchuddhān vituṣān sājaḍāphalān
ghṛtāḍhye māhiṣarase dadhidāḍimasārike
prakṣipenmātrayā yukto dhānyajīrakanāgaraiḥ
bhuktaḥ pītaśca sa rasaḥ kurute śukramakṣayam
ārdrāṇi matsyamāṃsāni śapharīrvā subharjitāḥ
tapte sarpiṣi yaḥ khādetsa gacchet strīṣu na kṣayam
ghṛtabhṛṣṭān rase chāge rohitān phalasārike
anupītarasān snigdhānapatyārthī prayojayet
kuṭṭakaṃ matsyamāṃsānāṃ hiṅgusaindhavadhānyakaiḥ
yuktaṃ godhūmacūrṇena ghṛte pūpalikāḥ pacet
māhiṣe ca rase matsyān snigdhāmlalavaṇān pacet
rase cānugate māṃsaṃ pothayettatra cāvapet
maricaṃ jīrakaṃ dhānyamalpaṃ hiṅgu navaṃ ghṛtam
māṣapūpalikānāṃ tadgarbhārtham upakalpayet
etau pūpalikāyogau bṛṃhaṇau balavardhanau
harṣasaubhāgyadau putryau paraṃ śukrābhivardhanau
māṣātmaguptāgodhūmaśāliṣaṣṭikapaiṣṭikam
śarkarāyā vidāryāśca cūrṇamikṣurakasya ca
saṃyojya masṛṇe kṣīre ghṛte pūpalikāḥ pacet
payo'nupānāstāḥ śīghraṃ kurvanti vṛṣatāṃ parām
śarkarāyāstulaikā syādekā gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ
prastho vidāryāścūrṇasya pippalyāḥ prastha eva ca
ardhāḍhakaṃ tugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasyābhinavasya ca
tatsarvaṃ mūrchitaṃ tiṣṭhen mārttike ghṛtabhājane
mātrāmagnisamāṃ tasya prātaḥ prātaḥ prayojayet
eṣa vṛṣyaḥ paraṃ yogo balyo bṛṃhaṇa eva ca
śatāvaryā vidāryāśca tathā māṣātmaguptayoḥ
śvadaṃṣṭrāyāśca niṣkvāthāñjaleṣu ca pṛthak pṛthak
sādhayitvā ghṛtaprasthaṃ payasyaṣṭaguṇe punaḥ
śarkarāmadhuyuktaṃ tadapatyārthī prayojayet
ghṛtapātraṃ śataguṇe vidārīsvarase pacet
siddhaṃ punaḥ śataguṇe gavye payasi sādhayet
śarkarāyāstugākṣīryāḥ kṣaudrasyekṣurakasya ca
pippalyāḥ sājaḍāyāśca bhāgaiḥ pādāṃśikairyutam
guṭikāḥ kārayedvaidyo yathā sthūlamudumbaram
tāsāṃ prayogātpuruṣaḥ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati
sitopalāpalaśataṃ tadardhaṃ navasarpiṣaḥ
kṣaudrapādena saṃyuktaṃ sādhayejjalapādikam
sāndraṃ godhūmacūrṇānāṃ pādaṃ stīrṇe śilātale
śucau ślakṣṇe samutkīrya mardanenopapādayet
śuddhā utkārikāḥ kāryāś candramaṇḍalasaṃnibhāḥ
tāsāṃ prayogādgajavannārīḥ saṃtarpayennaraḥ
yat kiṃcin madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ jīvanaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ guru
harṣaṇaṃ manasaścaiva sarvaṃ tadvṛṣyamucyate
dravyairevaṃvidhaistasmādbhāvitaḥ pramadāṃ vrajet
ātmavegena codīrṇaḥ strīguṇaiśca praharṣitaḥ
gatvā snātvā payaḥ pītvā rasaṃ vānu śayīta nā
tathāsyāpyāyate bhūyaḥ śukraṃ ca balameva ca
yathā mukulapuṣpasya sugandho nopalabhyate
labhyate tadvikāśāttu tathā śukraṃ hi dehinām
narte vai ṣoḍaśād varṣāt saptatyāḥ parato na ca
āyuṣkāmo naraḥ strībhiḥ saṃyogaṃ kartumarhati
atibālo hy asaṃpūrṇasarvadhātuḥ striyaṃ vrajan
upaśuṣyeta sahasā taḍāgamiva kājalam
śuṣkaṃ rūkṣaṃ yathā kāṣṭhaṃ jantudagdhaṃ vijarjaram
spṛṣṭamāśu viśīryeta tathā vṛddhaḥ striyo vrajan
jarayā cintayā śukraṃ vyādhibhiḥ karmakarṣaṇāt
kṣayaṃ gacchatyanaśanāt strīṇāṃ cātiniṣevaṇāt
kṣayādbhayādaviśrambhācchokātstrīdoṣadarśanāt
nārīṇāmarasajñatvād avicārād asevanāt
tṛptasyāpi striyo gantuṃ na śaktirupajāyate
dehasattvabalāpekṣī harṣaḥ śaktiśca harṣajā
rasa ikṣau yathā dadhni sarpistailaṃ tile yathā
sarvatrānugataṃ dehe śukraṃ saṃsparśane tathā
tat strīpuruṣasaṃyoge ceṣṭāsaṃkalpapīḍanāt
śukraṃ pracyavate sthānājjalamārdrātpaṭādiva
harṣāttarṣāt saratvācca paicchilyād gauravādapi
aṇupravaṇabhāvācca drutatvān mārutasya ca
aṣṭābhya ebhyo hetubhyaḥ śukraṃ dehāt prasicyate
carato viśvarūpasya rūpadravyaṃ yaducyate
bahalaṃ madhuraṃ snigdham avisraṃ guru picchilam
śuklaṃ ca yacchukraṃ phalavattadasaṃśayam
yena nārīṣu sāmarthyaṃ vājīvallabhate naraḥ
vrajeccābhyadhikaṃ yena vājīkaraṇameva tat
heturyogopadeśasya yogā dvādaśa cottamāḥ
yat pūrvaṃ maithunāt sevyaṃ sevyaṃ yanmaithunād anu
yadā na sevyāḥ pramadāḥ kṛtsnaḥ śukraviniścayaḥ
niruktaṃ ceha nirdiṣṭaṃ pumāñjātabalādike
ityagniveśakṛte tantre carakapratisaṃskṛte cikitsāsthāne vājīkaraṇādhyāye pumāñjātabalādiko nāma vājīkaraṇapādaścaturthaḥ
samāptaścāyaṃ dvitīyo vājīkaraṇādhyāyaḥ
